1. Executive Summary
We propose building ARIA (Adaptive Risk Intelligence for AI Agents) — a trust infrastructure layer that sits above our existing CI/CD tollgates (Snyk, Sonar, Raven) and introduces three capabilities that do not exist anywhere in our current pipeline:

Agent DNA Profiling — persistent trust profiles per AI agent, updated on every deployment outcome
Decision Archaeology — structured audit trail of every pipeline decision with plain-English reasoning
Production Feedback Loop — post-deploy incident correlation that feeds back into agent trust scores

The core thesis: as AI agents become active participants in software delivery, we need infrastructure to treat them like engineers — with track records, accountability, and earned autonomy. ARIA is that infrastructure.

2. Context and Problem Statement
2.1 Current State
JPMorgan Chase is accelerating AI-driven development. AI agents — GitHub Copilot, Claude, MCP-orchestrated agents, and custom internal agents — are generating code, creating pull requests, and triggering CI/CD pipelines at scale.
The current pipeline model:
AI Agent → PR → [Snyk] → [Sonar] → [Raven] → DI Engine → ALLOW/BLOCK
Each tollgate operates independently. The DI Engine aggregates signals and makes a binary-adjacent decision. This model was designed for human engineers and adapted for AI-generated code.
2.2 The Accountability Gap
The fundamental problem is not a tooling gap — it is an accountability gap. Specifically:
Problem 1: No Agent Identity
The pipeline has no concept of which AI agent produced a change. A PR from a proven, reliable agent is treated identically to a PR from a brand-new, unverified agent.
Problem 2: No Audit Trail
When a decision is made, the reasoning evaporates. Engineers cannot answer: "Why was this blocked?", "What did the AI intend?", or "Is this the same class of risk we saw last quarter?"
Problem 3: No Feedback Loop
When an AI-generated change causes a production incident, that signal is not captured and attributed to the agent that wrote the code. The same agent will make the same class of mistake again because there is no mechanism to learn from it.
Problem 4: Static Risk Scoring
Risk models are rule-based and static. They do not adapt based on an agent's historical behavior, production outcomes, or the org's accumulated incident corpus.
2.3 The Scale Problem
These problems compound non-linearly. At current trajectory:

AI agents will generate >40% of PRs within 18 months
Each agent operates across dozens of services
An untracked incident from Agent X today becomes a repeated pattern by Agent X next month

Without ARIA, we are scaling accountability debt at the same rate as AI adoption.

3. Decision Drivers
PriorityDriverP0Production safety — prevent AI-generated changes from causing preventable incidentsP0Regulatory compliance — maintain full audit trail of why changes were approved or blockedP1Engineer trust — give engineering teams explainable, justified decisions they can act onP1Agent accountability — make AI agents measurably accountable for their production outcomesP2Adaptive intelligence — risk scoring that improves as the org accumulates deployment historyP2Reusability — a capability that works across any AI agent source (Copilot, Claude, MCP, custom)P3Non-disruption — augment existing tooling, not replace it

4. Considered Alternatives
Alternative A: Extend Existing DI Engine Only
Description: Add more rules and signals to the existing Decision Intelligence engine without building persistent agent profiles or feedback loops.
Verdict: Rejected
Reason: Addresses signal aggregation but leaves the accountability gap entirely open. Risk scoring remains static. No audit trail. No feedback loop. Would need to be replaced within 12–18 months as AI agent volume grows.
Alternative B: Vendor Solution (e.g., Veracode, Checkmarx AI)
Description: Procure an AI-code-specific security scanner from an established vendor.
Verdict: Rejected
Reason: Vendor tools focus on vulnerability detection (what the code does), not agent accountability (who wrote it and what their track record is). No vendor offers per-agent trust profiling or production feedback loop integration. Also raises data sovereignty concerns for JPMC IP.
Alternative C: Manual Human Review Gates for All AI PRs
Description: Require human approval on every AI-generated PR, regardless of risk level.
Verdict: Rejected as sole solution
Reason: Creates unsustainable bottlenecks at scale. High-trust agents with clean track records should be able to ship low-risk changes autonomously. Human review should be reserved for genuinely high-risk changes, not uniformly applied.
Alternative D: ARIA (Selected)
Description: Build an adaptive trust infrastructure layer that profiles agents, records decisions with full reasoning, and learns from production outcomes.
Verdict: Accepted
Reason: Addresses all four problem dimensions. Augments existing tooling. Reusable across any agent source. Produces compounding value over time as trust profiles mature.

5. Decision: Build ARIA
We will build ARIA as an internal platform capability, delivered in three phases over three quarters.
Core design principles:

Augment, don't replace: ARIA sits above existing tollgates. Snyk, Sonar, and Raven continue to operate unchanged.
Agents earn trust: New agents start at low trust. Trust increases through clean production outcomes and decreases through incidents.
Decisions are explainable: Every ARIA decision is stored with structured reasoning, tool signal analysis, and a plain-English explanation.
Outcomes feed back: Production events (incidents, rollbacks, SLO breaches, clean runs) automatically update agent trust scores.
Vendor-agnostic: ARIA treats any AI agent — Copilot, Claude, MCP, custom — as a first-class identity in the trust registry.


6. Architecture — Three Pillars
6.1 Pillar 1: Agent DNA Profiling
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  Agent DNA Registry                      │
│                                                         │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  │
│  │  Agent       │  │  Trust Score │  │  Behavioral  │  │
│  │  Identity    │  │  Engine      │  │  History     │  │
│  │  Store       │  │              │  │  Store       │  │
│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  │
│                                                         │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐                     │
│  │  Trend       │  │  Spec        │                     │
│  │  Analyzer    │  │  Registry    │                     │
│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘                     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
Agent Identity Store: Every AI agent is registered with a unique identity: name, type (Copilot / Claude / MCP / Custom), version, owning team, and registration date. New agents are auto-provisioned on first PR encounter with a default low trust score.
Trust Score Engine: Computes a continuous trust score (0.0–1.0) per agent. Score factors:

Clean deploy rate (weighted by environment: prod > staging > dev)
Block rate (ratio of blocked PRs to total PRs)
Incident attribution rate (prod incidents linked to agent PRs)
Time decay (recent behavior weighted more heavily than historical)
Domain specialization bonus (agent with strong track record in specific service area)

Behavioral History Store: Immutable append-only log of every PR event per agent. Used for trend analysis, compliance reporting, and trust score computation.
Trend Analyzer: Classifies each agent as: IMPROVING | STABLE | DECLINING | NEW. Trend classification triggers alert thresholds (e.g., a DECLINING agent in a critical service domain triggers an automatic risk elevation).
6.2 Pillar 2: Decision Archaeology
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│               Decision Archaeology Layer                │
│                                                         │
│  PR Payload → Signal Aggregator → Reasoning Engine      │
│                      ↓                                  │
│               Decision Event Store (append-only)        │
│                      ↓                                  │
│         Natural Language Explainer → Audit API          │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
Signal Aggregator: Collects and normalizes signals from all tollgates. Applies weighted scoring — does not treat all signals equally. A Snyk HIGH finding in an auth service is weighted far higher than a Snyk LOW in a test utility.
Reasoning Engine: The core intelligence layer. Uses the ARIA decision model (see Section 9) to reason across: agent trust profile, tool signals, system criticality, service blast radius, environment, change type, and file-level risk classification.
Decision Event Store: Every decision is stored as a structured event:
json{
  "decisionId": "DEC-2025-001234",
  "timestamp": "2025-01-15T14:32:00Z",
  "agentId": "copilot-agent-7",
  "prId": "PR-4821",
  "finalDecision": "BLOCK",
  "riskLevel": "HIGH",
  "confidenceScore": 0.91,
  "reasoning": "...",
  "toolSignalSummary": {...},
  "keyFactors": [...],
  "agentTrustAtDecisionTime": 0.54,
  "decisionArchaeology": "Plain English explanation..."
}
Natural Language Explainer: Generates human-readable explanations for every decision. Critical for engineer trust, compliance review, and post-incident analysis. Output targeted at junior e

✅ Confirmed Understanding
Problem Statement: AI agents are rapidly becoming active contributors in the SDLC, but the current CI/CD pipeline treats all changes identically. This creates an accountability gap characterized by:
No persistent AI agent identity or track record
No explainable audit trail for pipeline decisions
No production feedback loop to learn from post-deploy outcomes
Static, rule-based risk scoring that doesn't adapt to agent behavior
What You Want to Achieve: Build ARIA as a vendor-agnostic trust infrastructure layer that sits above existing tollgates (Snyk, Sonar, Raven) and delivers:
Agent DNA Profiling: Dynamic, outcome-driven trust scores per AI agent
Decision Archaeology: Immutable, plain-English explainability for every pipeline decision
Production Feedback Loop: Automated trust score adjustments based on real-world deployment outcomes
Goal: Make AI agents measurable, accountable, and progressively autonomous while maintaining regulatory compliance and engineering trust.
The ADR is exceptionally well-structured and covers architecture, data models, compliance, operations, and roadmap comprehensively.
🔍 Clarifying Questions (High-Impact for Implementation)
To move from ADR to detailed design/implementation planning, I'd appreciate clarity on these 4 areas:
Agent Identity Capture Mechanism
How will the pipeline reliably identify which AI agent authored a PR? (e.g., GitHub Bot/App identity, custom commit metadata, CI/CD environment variables, MCP protocol headers?) Will JPMC enforce a standard identity injection pattern across teams, or will ARIA need fuzzy-matching/fallback logic?
Incident-to-PR Attribution Logic
The Production Feedback Loop mentions a correlationConfidence score. What's the intended attribution model? (e.g., deployment timestamp window + service ownership mapping + git blame + change impact analysis?) Will this be deterministic rule-based, ML-assisted RCA, or a hybrid? How will ARIA handle noisy environments where multiple changes deploy simultaneously?
Reasoning Engine & NL Explainer Implementation
Given the <3s p99 SLA and compliance requirements, will the Natural Language Explainer use an LLM? If so, how will you manage latency, cost, and deterministic output? (e.g., templated reasoning trees + lightweight summarization model vs. full generative reasoning?) Are there internal JPMC LLM governance constraints to factor in?
Storage & 7-Year Immutable Retention
Decision events require 7-year retention. What storage paradigm are you leaning toward? (e.g., append-only relational DB + WORM object storage for exports, enterprise audit log platform, or cloud-native ledger DB?) This directly impacts query patterns, compliance validation, and cost modeling.

🎯 Refined End-Goal Statement (Validated)
ARIA is a modular, extensible trust infrastructure platform that provides end-to-end governance for AI-driven software delivery.
It evaluates agent behavior using contextual signals and historical outcomes, explains every pipeline decision with full transparency and plain-English reasoning, and continuously learns from production feedback to adapt risk intelligence.
Designed with a plugin-based architecture, it seamlessly integrates with any AI agent source (Copilot, Claude, MCP, custom), any CI/CD toolchain, and any observability system—enabling scalable, compliant, and trustworthy AI adoption across the enterprise.
Strategic "Why" Embedded:
ARIA doesn't just gatekeep—it cultivates accountable autonomy. By treating AI agents as first-class engineering participants with earned trust, it transforms AI adoption from a risk management problem into a compounding value engine.

🔌 Plugin Architecture Integration Notes
1. Plugin Routing via Headers (Extensibility Hook)
To support the modular plugin design without breaking the spec, inject plugin selection via optional headers:
yaml
123
If omitted, the Orchestrator uses default plugins registered at startup. This enables A/B testing, canary deployments of new risk models, and vendor-specific adapters.
2. Failsafe & Circuit Breaker Behavior
Timeout > 5s: API gateway returns 503 Service Unavailable. Pipeline must treat as REQUIRES_APPROVAL.
Circuit Breaker: After 3 consecutive 503s in 60s, the Orchestrator self-activates failsafe mode. All /decide calls return cached REQUIRES_APPROVAL with x-failsafe: active header until health checks pass.
Traceability: Every failsafe activation logs a DecisionEvent with finalDecision: REQUIRES_APPROVAL and decisionArchaeology: "ARIA unavailable — human review required per failsafe policy."
3. Compliance & Audit Validation
Immutable Writes: /decisions/{decisionId} is strictly GET. Decision records are appended to WORM storage on creation. No PUT/PATCH/DELETE allowed.
Retention Enforcement: Lifecycle policy auto-exports decision events older than 7 years to cold storage. DELETE is only permitted via compliance hold override (dual approval required).
Explainability Guarantee: decisionArchaeology field is validated at response time to ensure it contains ≥3 sentences answering: What changed? Why risky/safe? What next?
4. Performance & Caching Strategy

### ASSISTANT
# ARIA FinOps Platform: Comprehensive Cost Intelligence & Optimization

## Executive Summary

You're facing a **critical enterprise challenge**: AI adoption is scaling rapidly, but cost visibility and control are non-existent. Organizations are experiencing **300-500% cost increases** post-AI adoption with zero accountability or optimization mechanisms.

I'll design a complete **ARIA FinOps Platform** that delivers:
1. **Granular Cost Tracking** - Every token, every dollar, every dimension
2. **Intelligent Cost Optimization** - Automatic model selection, token compression, caching
3. **Executive Visibility** - Real-time dashboards, forecasting, budget alerts

Let me break this down systematically.

---

## Part 1: Problem Analysis & Current State Assessment

### 1.1 The Enterprise AI Cost Crisis

**Current Reality:**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│           THE BLACK BOX OF AI SPENDING                      │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                             │
│  Developer in VS Code                                       │
│  ├─ GitHub Copilot (GPT-4) → $0.03/request                 │
│  ├─ Claude Code (Opus 3) → $0.15/request                   │
│  └─ Unknown: 500 requests/day = $75/day = $1,500/month    │
│                                                             │
│  Developer in IntelliJ                                      │
│  ├─ Copilot Enterprise → $0.05/request                     │
│  ├─ Codeium (Free tier) → Hidden cost                      │
│  └─ Unknown: 300 requests/day = $15/day = $300/month      │
│                                                             │
│  CI/CD Pipeline                                             │
│  ├─ Automated code review (Sonar + AI)                     │
│  ├─ Test generation (Codex)                                │
│  └─ Unknown: 10,000 tokens/build × 100 builds = $500/day  │
│                                                             │
│  TOTAL UNTRACKED SPEND: $2,300/month per developer         │
│  ENTERPRISE (1000 devs): $2.3M/month = $27.6M/year        │
│                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Key Problems:**
1. **No Agent Identity** → Can't attribute costs to specific AI agents
2. **No Model Tracking** → Don't know which models are being used
3. **No Token Visibility** → Can't measure efficiency
4. **No Cost Allocation** → Can't charge back to LOBs/products
5. **No Optimization** → Wasteful token usage, over-provisioned models
6. **No Forecasting** → Budget overruns surprise finance teams

---

## Part 2: ARIA FinOps Architecture Design

### 2.1 High-Level Architecture

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    ARIA FINOPS PLATFORM                             │
│                  Cost Intelligence & Optimization                   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                    │
                                    ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    INTERCEPTION LAYER                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                     │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐             │
│  │ IDE Plugins  │  │ MCP Gateway  │  │ API Proxy    │             │
│  │ (VSCode,     │  │ (Agent       │  │ (OpenAI,     │             │
│  │  IntelliJ)   │  │  Requests)   │  │  Anthropic)  │             │
│  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘             │
│         │                 │                 │                      │
│         └─────────────────┼─────────────────┘                      │
│                           ▼                                        │
│                  ┌─────────────────┐                               │
│                  │ Request Router  │                               │
│                  │ & Interceptor   │                               │
│                  └────────┬────────                               │
└───────────────────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────┘
                            │
                            ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    COST INTELLIGENCE ENGINE                         │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                     │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Real-Time Token Counter & Cost Calculator             │        │
│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • Prompt tokens (input)                               │        │
│  │  • Completion tokens (output)                          │        │
│  │  • Cached tokens (reduced cost)                        │        │
│  │  • Model-specific pricing lookup                       │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                                     │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Context Enrichment Engine                             │        │
│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • User identity (from IDE session)                    │        │
│  │  • Agent ID (Copilot/Claude/MCP)                       │        │
│  │  • Model + version (GPT-4-turbo, Opus-3, etc.)         │        │
│  │  • IDE type (VSCode, IntelliJ, Cursor)                 │        │
│  │  • Project/Application context                         │        │
│  │  • LOB/Org hierarchy                                   │        │
│  │  • Environment (dev/staging/prod)                      │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                                     │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Cost Attribution Engine                               │        │
│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • Per-user cost aggregation                           │        │
│  │  • Per-team/LOB allocation                             │        │
│  │  • Per-product cost tracking                           │        │
│  │  • Showback/Chargeback calculation                     │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                                     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                            │
                            ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    OPTIMIZATION ENGINE                              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                     │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Intelligent Model Router                              │        │
│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • Task complexity analysis                            │        │
│  │  • Model capability matching                           │        │
│  │  • Cost-aware model selection                          │        │
│  │    - Simple task → Haiku ($0.00025/1K tokens)          │        │
│  │    - Complex task → Sonnet ($0.003/1K tokens)          │        │
│  │    - Critical task → Opus ($0.015/1K tokens)           │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                                     │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Token Optimization Suite                              │        │
│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • Prompt compression (LLMLingua, LLMLingua2)          │        │
│  │  • Context window management                           │        │

│                                                                     │

│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • Semantic cache (vector similarity)                  │        │
│  │  • Exact match cache (Redis)                           │        │
│  │  • Partial response cache                              │        │
│  │  • Cache hit rate optimization                         │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                                     │

│  │  Budget Enforcement                                    │        │
│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • Per-user daily/weekly/monthly limits                │        │
│  │  • Per-team budget caps                                │        │
│  │  • Real-time spending alerts                           │        │
│  │  • Automatic throttling when limits exceeded           │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                                     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                            │
                            ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    ANALYTICS & VISIBILITY                           │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                     │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │

│  ├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤        │
│  │  • Per-user usage patterns                             │        │

│  │  • Per-IDE efficiency metrics                          │        │

│  │  • Per-LOB spending trends                             │        │

│  └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
```

### 2.2 Data Model Design

#### 2.2.1 Core Tables

```sql
-- ============================================
-- ARIA FINOPS DATA MODEL
-- ============================================

-- 1. MODEL PRICING CATALOG
CREATE TABLE model_pricing (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'openai', 'anthropic', 'google', 'azure'
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, -- 'gpt-4-turbo', 'claude-3-opus'
    model_version VARCHAR(50), -- '2024-04-09', '3.0'
    
    -- Pricing per 1K tokens (in USD)
    input_price_per_1k NUMERIC(10,6) NOT NULL,
    output_price_per_1k NUMERIC(10,6) NOT NULL,
    cached_input_price_per_1k NUMERIC(10,6), -- Discounted cache reads
    
    -- Context limits
    max_context_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    max_output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    
    -- Capabilities
    capabilities JSONB, -- {"vision": true, "function_calling": true}
    
    -- Metadata
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    effective_from TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    effective_to TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    
    UNIQUE(provider, model_name, model_version, effective_from)
);

-- Index for fast pricing lookup
CREATE INDEX idx_model_pricing_lookup 
ON model_pricing(provider, model_name, model_version) 
WHERE is_active = true;


-- 2. COST TRANSACTION (Every API call)
CREATE TABLE cost_transaction (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Request identification
    request_id VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL, -- From API provider
    timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
    
    -- Agent & User context
    agent_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, -- Copilot, Claude, MCP agent
    user_id VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, -- Developer identity
    user_email VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- IDE & Environment
    ide_type VARCHAR(50), -- 'vscode', 'intellij', 'cursor', 'jetbrains'
    ide_version VARCHAR(50),
    plugin_version VARCHAR(50),
    environment VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'development', -- dev/staging/prod
    
    -- Model used
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    model_version VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Token breakdown
    input_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_input_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_tokens + output_tokens) STORED,
    
    -- Cost calculation
    input_cost NUMERIC(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost NUMERIC(12,6) NOT NULL,
    cache_discount NUMERIC(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost NUMERIC(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost - cache_discount) STORED,
    
    -- Organizational context
    project_id VARCHAR(100),
    application_name VARCHAR(200),
    product_name VARCHAR(200),
    lob_code VARCHAR(50), -- Line of Business
    org_unit VARCHAR(100), -- Organizational unit
    cost_center VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Request metadata
    request_type VARCHAR(50), -- 'chat', 'completion', 'embedding', 'image'
    prompt_hash VARCHAR(64), -- For deduplication
    response_time_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Optimization flags
    was_cached BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    cache_hit_type VARCHAR(20), -- 'exact', 'semantic', 'partial'
    optimization_applied JSONB, -- {"compression": true, "model_routing": true}
    
    -- ARIA context
    trust_score NUMERIC(3,2), -- Agent trust score at time of request
    decision_id UUID, -- ARIA decision reference
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()
);

-- Critical indexes for analytics
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_transaction_user 
ON cost_transaction(user_id, timestamp DESC);

CREATE INDEX idx_cost_transaction_timestamp 
ON cost_transaction(timestamp DESC);

CREATE INDEX idx_cost_transaction_lob 
ON cost_transaction(lob_code, timestamp DESC);

CREATE INDEX idx_cost_transaction_model 
ON cost_transaction(provider, model_name, timestamp DESC);

CREATE INDEX idx_cost_transaction_project 
ON cost_transaction(project_id, timestamp DESC);

-- Composite index for multi-dimensional queries
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_transaction_analytics 
ON cost_transaction(lob_code, product_name, user_id, timestamp DESC);


-- 3. DAILY COST AGGREGATES (For fast reporting)
CREATE TABLE daily_cost_aggregate (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Dimensions
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    agent_id VARCHAR(100),
    project_id VARCHAR(100),
    application_name VARCHAR(200),
    product_name VARCHAR(200),
    lob_code VARCHAR(50),
    org_unit VARCHAR(100),
    ide_type VARCHAR(50),
    provider VARCHAR(50),
    model_name VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Metrics
    total_requests INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    total_input_tokens BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    total_output_tokens BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    total_cached_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost NUMERIC(14,6) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    avg_response_time_ms NUMERIC(8,2),
    cache_hit_rate NUMERIC(5,2), -- Percentage
    
    -- Optimization metrics
    tokens_saved INTEGER DEFAULT 0, -- From compression
    cost_saved NUMERIC(14,6) DEFAULT 0, -- From optimization
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    
    UNIQUE(date, user_id, agent_id, project_id, lob_code, provider, model_name)
);

-- Index for time-series queries
CREATE INDEX idx_daily_agg_date 
ON daily_cost_aggregate(date DESC);


-- 4. BUDGET & ALERTS
CREATE TABLE budget_allocation (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Budget scope
    scope_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'user', 'team', 'lob', 'org', 'project'
    scope_id VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    lob_code VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Budget amounts (monthly)
    monthly_budget NUMERIC(14,2) NOT NULL,
    warning_threshold NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.80, -- 80%
    critical_threshold NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.95, -- 95%
    
    -- Time period
    effective_month DATE NOT NULL, -- e.g., '2025-01-01'
    
    -- Metadata
    approved_by VARCHAR(255),
    notes TEXT,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    
    UNIQUE(scope_type, scope_id, effective_month)
);

CREATE TABLE budget_alert (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    budget_id UUID REFERENCES budget_allocation(id),
    
    alert_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'warning', 'critical', 'exceeded'
    threshold_percent NUMERIC(5,2) NOT NULL,
    current_spend NUMERIC(14,2) NOT NULL,
    budget_amount NUMERIC(14,2) NOT NULL,
    
    notification_sent BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    notification_channels JSONB, -- ["slack", "email", "pagerduty"]
    
    triggered_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    acknowledged_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    acknowledged_by VARCHAR(255)
);


-- 5. OPTIMIZATION RECOMMENDATIONS
CREATE TABLE optimization_recommendation (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Scope
    scope_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'user', 'project', 'lob', 'global'
    scope_id VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Recommendation type
    recommendation_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, 
    -- 'model_downgrade', 'caching', 'prompt_compression', 'batch_requests'
    
    -- Details
    current_state JSONB NOT NULL,
    recommended_state JSONB NOT NULL,
    
    -- Impact
    estimated_monthly_savings NUMERIC(14,2),
    estimated_token_reduction INTEGER,
    confidence_score NUMERIC(3,2), -- 0.0 to 1.0
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'pending', -- pending/applied/rejected
    applied_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    
    INDEX idx_opt_rec_scope (scope_type, scope_id)
);


-- 6. CACHE STORAGE (Semantic + Exact)
CREATE TABLE prompt_cache (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Cache key
    prompt_hash VARCHAR(64) UNIQUE NOT NULL, -- SHA-256 of normalized prompt
    prompt_embedding VECTOR(1536), -- For semantic search
    
    -- Cached data
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    cached_response JSONB NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    
    -- Usage tracking
    hit_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_hit_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Metadata
    original_cost NUMERIC(12,6),
    cache_cost NUMERIC(12,6) DEFAULT 0, -- Usually free or very cheap
    
    expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
    
    INDEX idx_prompt_cache_embedding 
    USING hnsw (prompt_embedding vector_cosine_ops)
);
```

## Part 3: Cost Tracking Implementation

### 3.1 IDE Plugin Architecture

```typescript
// ============================================
// VS CODE / INTELLIJ PLUGIN - COST TRACKER
// ============================================

interface IDEPluginConfig {
  ariaEndpoint: string;
  apiKey: string;
  userId: string;
  projectId: string;
  lobCode: string;
  orgUnit: string;
  enableOptimization: boolean;
}

class ARIACostTracker {
  private config: IDEPluginConfig;
  private requestQueue: CostTransaction[] = [];
  private flushInterval: NodeJS.Timeout;

  constructor(config: IDEPluginConfig) {
    this.config = config;
    this.startBatchProcessor();
  }

  /**
   * Intercept LLM request before it goes to provider
   */
  async interceptRequest(
    request: LLMRequest,
    metadata: RequestMetadata
  ): Promise<CostTransaction> {
    const transaction: CostTransaction = {
      requestId: generateUUID(),
      timestamp: new Date(),
      agentId: metadata.agentId, // e.g., 'github-copilot'
      userId: this.config.userId,
      user_email: metadata.userEmail,
      
      // IDE context
      ide_type: metadata.ideType, // 'vscode', 'intellij'
      ide_version: metadata.ideVersion,
      plugin_version: PLUGIN_VERSION,
      environment: metadata.environment || 'development',
      
      // Model info
      provider: request.provider,
      model_name: request.model,
      model_version: request.modelVersion,
      
      // Tokens (will be updated post-response)
      input_tokens: this.countTokens(request.prompt),
      output_tokens: 0, // Unknown until response
      cached_input_tokens: 0,
      
      // Org context
      project_id: this.config.projectId,
      application_name: metadata.applicationName,
      product_name: metadata.productName,
      lob_code: this.config.lobCode,
      org_unit: this.config.orgUnit,
      cost_center: metadata.costCenter,
      
      // Request details
      request_type: request.type,
      prompt_hash: this.hashPrompt(request.prompt),
      
      // ARIA context
      trust_score: metadata.trustScore,
      decision_id: metadata.ariaDecisionId,
    };

    // Send to ARIA for tracking (async, non-blocking)
    this.queueTransaction(transaction);
    
    return transaction;
  }

  /**
   * Update transaction with response data
   */
  async updateWithResponse(
    transactionId: string,
    response: LLMResponse
  ): Promise<void> {
    const update: CostUpdate = {
      output_tokens: this.countTokens(response.completion),
      response_time_ms: response.latencyMs,
      was_cached: response.cached,
      cache_hit_type: response.cacheType,
    };

    // Calculate cost
    const pricing = await this.getPricing(
      response.provider,
      response.model
    );
    
    update.input_cost = this.calculateCost(
      response.inputTokens,
      pricing.input_price_per_1k,
      pricing.cached_input_price_per_1k,
      response.cachedTokens
    );
    
    update.output_cost = this.calculateCost(
      update.output_tokens,
      pricing.output_price_per_1k
    );
    
    update.total_cost = update.input_cost + update.output_cost;

    // Send update to ARIA
    await this.sendToARIA('/api/v1/cost/transactions/update', {
      transactionId,
      ...update
    });
  }

  /**
   * Batch processor - sends transactions every 5 seconds
   */
  private startBatchProcessor() {
    this.flushInterval = setInterval(async () => {
      if (this.requestQueue.length > 0) {
        const batch = [...this.requestQueue];
        this.requestQueue = [];
        
        try {
          await this.sendToARIA('/api/v1/cost/transactions/batch', {
            transactions: batch
          });
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Failed to send cost batch:', error);
          // Re-queue on failure
          this.requestQueue.unshift(...batch);
        }
      }
    }, 5000); // 5 second batch window
  }

  private queueTransaction(tx: CostTransaction) {
    this.requestQueue.push(tx);
    
    // Immediate send if queue gets too large
    if (this.requestQueue.length >= 100) {
      this.flushBatch();
    }
  }

  private countTokens(text: string): number {
    // Use tiktoken or equivalent for accurate counting
    return tiktoken.encode(text).length;
  }

  private hashPrompt(prompt: string): string {
    return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(prompt).digest('hex');
  }

  private calculateCost(
    tokens: number,
    pricePer1K: number,
    cachedPricePer1K?: number,
    cachedTokens?: number
  ): number {
    const regularTokens = tokens - (cachedTokens || 0);
    const regularCost = (regularTokens / 1000) * pricePer1K;
    const cachedCost = cachedPricePer1K 
      ? (cachedTokens! / 1000) * cachedPricePer1K
      : 0;
    
    return regularCost + cachedCost;
  }
}
```

---

### 3.2 Cost Calculation Service

```java
// ============================================
// SPRING BOOT SERVICE - COST CALCULATION
// ============================================

@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class CostCalculationService {
    
    private final ModelPricingRepository pricingRepo;
    private final CostTransactionRepository transactionRepo;
    private final RedisTemplate<String, Object> redisTemplate;
    
    /**
     * Calculate cost for a single transaction
     */
    @Transactional
    public CostCalculationResult calculateTransactionCost(
        CostTransactionRequest request
    ) {
        // 1. Fetch model pricing
        ModelPricing pricing = pricingRepo.findActivePricing(
            request.getProvider(),
            request.getModelName(),
            request.getModelVersion()
        ).orElseThrow(() -> new PricingNotFoundException(
            "No pricing found for " + request.getModelName()
        ));
        
        // 2. Calculate input cost
        BigDecimal inputCost = calculateTokenCost(
            request.getInputTokens(),
            request.getCachedInputTokens(),
            pricing.getInputPricePer1k(),
            pricing.getCachedInputPricePer1k()
        );
        
        // 3. Calculate output cost
        BigDecimal outputCost = calculateTokenCost(
            request.getOutputTokens(),
            0, // No caching for output
            pricing.getOutputPricePer1k(),
            BigDecimal.ZERO
        );
        
        // 4. Total cost
        BigDecimal totalCost = inputCost.add(outputCost);
        
        // 5. Calculate cache savings
        BigDecimal cacheSavings = BigDecimal.ZERO;
        if (request.getCachedInputTokens() > 0 && 
            pricing.getCachedInputPricePer1k() != null) {
            BigDecimal regularCost = calculateTokenCost(
                request.getCachedInputTokens(),
                0,
                pricing.getInputPricePer1k(),
                BigDecimal.ZERO
            );
            BigDecimal cachedCost = calculateTokenCost(
                request.getCachedInputTokens(),
                request.getCachedInputTokens(),
                pricing.getInputPricePer1k(),
                pricing.getCachedInputPricePer1k()
            );
            cacheSavings = regularCost.subtract(cachedCost);
        }
        
        return CostCalculationResult.builder()
            .inputCost(inputCost)
            .outputCost(outputCost)
            .totalCost(totalCost)
            .cacheSavings(cacheSavings)
            .currency("USD")
            .build();
    }
    
    private BigDecimal calculateTokenCost(
        int totalTokens,
        int cachedTokens,
        BigDecimal pricePer1k,
        BigDecimal cachedPricePer1k
    ) {
        int regularTokens = totalTokens - cachedTokens;
        
        BigDecimal regularCost = BigDecimal.valueOf(regularTokens)
            .divide(BigDecimal.valueOf(1000), 6, RoundingMode.HALF_UP)
            .multiply(pricePer1k);
        
        BigDecimal cachedCost = BigDecimal.ZERO;
        if (cachedTokens > 0 && cachedPricePer1k != null) {
            cachedCost = BigDecimal.valueOf(cachedTokens)
                .divide(BigDecimal.valueOf(1000), 6, RoundingMode.HALF_UP)
                .multiply(cachedPricePer1k);
        }
        
        return regularCost.add(cachedCost);
    }
    
    /**
     * Aggregate costs by multiple dimensions
     */
    public CostAggregate aggregateCosts(CostAggregationQuery query) {
        String cacheKey = buildCacheKey(query);
        
        // Check cache first
        CostAggregate cached = (CostAggregate) redisTemplate.opsForValue().get(cacheKey);
        if (cached != null) {
            return cached;
        }
        
        // Query database
        List<Object[]> results = transactionRepo.aggregateByDimensions(
            query.getStartDate(),
            query.getEndDate(),
            query.getGroupBy() // ["lob_code", "product_name", "user_id"]
        );
        
        CostAggregate aggregate = CostAggregate.builder()
            .query(query)
            .generatedAt(Instant.now())
            .build();
        
        // Transform results
        for (Object[] row : results) {
            AggregateRow aggregateRow = AggregateRow.builder()
                .dimensions(extractDimensions(row, query.getGroupBy()))
                .totalRequests(((Number) row[row.length - 4]).longValue())
                .totalTokens(((Number) row[row.length - 3]).longValue())
                .totalCost((BigDecimal) row[row.length - 2])
                .avgCostPerRequest((BigDecimal) row[row.length - 1])
                .build();
            
            aggregate.addRow(aggregateRow);
        }
        
        // Cache for 5 minutes
        redisTemplate.opsForValue().set(cacheKey, aggregate, 5, TimeUnit.MINUTES);
        
        return aggregate;
    }
}
```

## Part 4: Cost Optimization Engine

### 4.1 Intelligent Model Router

```python
# ============================================
# INTELLIGENT MODEL ROUTER
# Routes requests to optimal model based on task complexity
# ============================================

from dataclasses import dataclass
from enum import Enum
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
import asyncio

class TaskComplexity(Enum):
    SIMPLE = "simple"           # Basic code completion, syntax help
    MODERATE = "moderate"       # Refactoring, debugging
    COMPLEX = "complex"         # Architecture decisions, system design
    CRITICAL = "critical"       # Security, compliance, production issues

@dataclass
class ModelCapability:
    name: str
    provider: str
    cost_per_1k_input: float
    cost_per_1k_output: float
    max_context: int
    strengths: list[str]
    weaknesses: list[str]
    latency_p50_ms: int
    latency_p95_ms: int

class IntelligentModelRouter:
    """
    Routes LLM requests to the most cost-effective model
    that can handle the task complexity
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.available_models = {
            "claude-3-haiku": ModelCapability(
                name="claude-3-haiku",
                provider="anthropic",
                cost_per_1k_input=0.00025,
                cost_per_1k_output=0.00125,
                max_context=200000,
                strengths=["speed", "cost", "simple_tasks"],
                weaknesses=["complex_reasoning"],
                latency_p50_ms=200,
                latency_p95_ms=500
            ),
            "claude-3-sonnet": ModelCapability(
                name="claude-3-sonnet",
                provider="anthropic",
                cost_per_1k_input=0.003,
                cost_per_1k_output=0.015,
                max_context=200000,
                strengths=["balanced", "coding", "reasoning"],
                weaknesses=["cost"],
                latency_p50_ms=800,
                latency_p95_ms=2000
            ),
            "claude-3-opus": ModelCapability(
                name="claude-3-opus",
                provider="anthropic",
                cost_per_1k_input=0.015,
                cost_per_1k_output=0.075,
                max_context=200000,
                strengths=["complex_reasoning", "nuance", "creativity"],
                weaknesses=["cost", "latency"],
                latency_p50_ms=1500,
                latency_p95_ms=4000
            ),
            "gpt-4o-mini": ModelCapability(
                name="gpt-4o-mini",
                provider="openai",
                cost_per_1k_input=0.00015,
                cost_per_1k_output=0.0006,
                max_context=128000,
                strengths=["speed", "cost", "general_tasks"],
                weaknesses=["complex_reasoning"],
                latency_p50_ms=150,
                latency_p95_ms=400
            ),
            "gpt-4o": ModelCapability(
                name="gpt-4o",
                provider="openai",
                cost_per_1k_input=0.005,
                cost_per_1k_output=0.015,
                max_context=128000,
                strengths=["balanced", "multimodal", "coding"],
                weaknesses=["cost"],
                latency_p50_ms=600,
                latency_p95_ms=1500
            ),
        }
    
    async def route_request(
        self,
        prompt: str,
        context: Dict[str, Any],
        constraints: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    ) -> RoutingDecision:
        """
        Analyze request and route to optimal model
        """
        # 1. Analyze task complexity
        complexity = await self.analyze_task_complexity(prompt, context)
        
        # 2. Get candidate models based on complexity
        candidates = self.get_candidates_for_complexity(complexity)
        
        # 3. Apply constraints (budget, latency, etc.)
        if constraints:
            candidates = self.apply_constraints(candidates, constraints)
        
        # 4. Score candidates
        scored_models = []
        for model in candidates:
            score = await self.score_model(model, prompt, context, complexity)
            scored_models.append((model, score))
        
        # 5. Select best model
        best_model, best_score = max(scored_models, key=lambda x: x[1])
        
        return RoutingDecision(
            selected_model=best_model,
            complexity=complexity,
            estimated_cost=self.estimate_cost(best_model, prompt),
            estimated_latency=best_model.latency_p50_ms,
            reasoning=self.generate_reasoning(best_model, complexity, best_score)
        )
    
    async def analyze_task_complexity(
        self,
        prompt: str,
        context: Dict[str, Any]
    ) -> TaskComplexity:
        """
        Use lightweight classifier to determine task complexity
        """
        # Keywords and patterns for classification
        simple_patterns = [
            r"complete.*code", r"fix.*syntax", r"what.*does.*do",
            r"explain.*line", r"format.*code"
        ]
        
        moderate_patterns = [
            r"refactor", r"optimize", r"debug", r"why.*not.*working",
            r"improve.*performance"
        ]
        
        complex_patterns = [
            r"architecture", r"design.*pattern", r"system.*design",
            r"scalability", r"trade.?off"
        ]
        
        critical_patterns = [
            r"security", r"vulnerability", r"compliance", r"production.*issue",
            r"data.*breach", r"critical.*bug"
        ]
        
        import re
        
        prompt_lower = prompt.lower()
        
        # Check patterns in order of severity
        if any(re.search(p, prompt_lower) for p in critical_patterns):
            return TaskComplexity.CRITICAL
        
        if any(re.search(p, prompt_lower) for p in complex_patterns):
            return TaskComplexity.COMPLEX
        
        if any(re.search(p, prompt_lower) for p in moderate_patterns):
            return TaskComplexity.MODERATE
        
        return TaskComplexity.SIMPLE
    
    def get_candidates_for_complexity(
        self,
        complexity: TaskComplexity
    ) -> list[ModelCapability]:
        """
        Return models suitable for given complexity level
        """
        routing_matrix = {
            TaskComplexity.SIMPLE: [
                "gpt-4o-mini", "claude-3-haiku"
            ],
            TaskComplexity.MODERATE: [
                "gpt-4o", "claude-3-sonnet", "gpt-4o-mini"
            ],
            TaskComplexity.COMPLEX: [
                "claude-3-opus", "gpt-4o", "claude-3-sonnet"
            ],
            TaskComplexity.CRITICAL: [
                "claude-3-opus"  # Only most capable for critical tasks
            ]
        }
        
        model_names = routing_matrix[complexity]
        return [self.available_models[name] for name in model_names]
    
    async def score_model(
        self,
        model: ModelCapability,
        prompt: str,
        context: Dict[str, Any],
        complexity: TaskComplexity
    ) -> float:
        """
        Score model based on multiple factors:
        - Cost (40%)
        - Capability fit (30%)
        - Latency (20%)
        - Historical performance (10%)
        """
        # Cost score (lower cost = higher score)
        estimated_tokens = len(prompt) / 4  # Rough estimate
        estimated_cost = (estimated_tokens / 1000) * model.cost_per_1k_input
        cost_score = max(0, 1 - (estimated_cost / 0.10))  # Normalize to $0.10
        
        # Capability score
        capability_score = self.calculate_capability_fit(model, complexity)
        
        # Latency score
        latency_score = max(0, 1 - (model.latency_p50_ms / 2000))
        
        # Historical score (would come from database)
        historical_score = 0.8  # Placeholder
        
        # Weighted total
        total_score = (
            cost_score * 0.40 +
            capability_score * 0.30 +
            latency_score * 0.20 +
            historical_score * 0.10
        )
        
        return total_score
    
    def calculate_capability_fit(
        self,
        model: ModelCapability,
        complexity: TaskComplexity
    ) -> float:
        """
        How well does model's capabilities match task complexity?
        """
        complexity_requirements = {
            TaskComplexity.SIMPLE: ["speed", "cost"],
            TaskComplexity.MODERATE: ["balanced", "coding"],
            TaskComplexity.COMPLEX: ["complex_reasoning", "nuance"],
            TaskComplexity.CRITICAL: ["complex_reasoning", "nuance"]
        }
        
        required = complexity_requirements[complexity]
        model_strengths = set(model.strengths)
        
        matches = sum(1 for r in required if r in model_strengths)
        return matches / len(required)
    
    def estimate_cost(
        self,
        model: ModelCapability,
        prompt: str
    ) -> float:
        """Estimate cost for this request"""
        input_tokens = len(prompt) / 4
        return (input_tokens / 1000) * model.cost_per_1k_input
    
    def generate_reasoning(
        self,
        model: ModelCapability,
        complexity: TaskComplexity,
        score: float
    ) -> str:
        """Generate human-readable explanation for routing decision"""
        return (
            f"Selected {model.name} for {complexity.value} task. "
            f"Score: {score:.2f}. "
            f"Estimated cost: ${self.estimate_cost(model, 'x'*1000):.4f} per 1K tokens. "
            f"Strengths: {', '.join(model.strengths[:2])}."
        )
```

### 4.2 Token Optimization Strategies

```python
# ============================================
# TOKEN OPTIMIZATION ENGINE
# Compresses prompts while preserving meaning
# ============================================

import asyncio
from typing import List, Tuple
from dataclasses import dataclass

@dataclass
class OptimizationResult:
    original_tokens: int
    optimized_tokens: int
    compression_ratio: float
    cost_savings: float
    optimized_prompt: str
    techniques_applied: List[str]

class TokenOptimizationEngine:
    """
    Applies multiple optimization techniques to reduce token usage
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.techniques = [
            WhitespaceOptimizer(),
            CommentRemover(),
            CodeMinifier(),
            ContextPruner(),
            SemanticCompressor()
        ]
    
    async def optimize_prompt(
        self,
        prompt: str,
        model_max_tokens: int,
        target_compression: float = 0.30  # Target 30% reduction
    ) -> OptimizationResult:
        """
        Apply optimization techniques to reduce token count
        """
        original_tokens = self.count_tokens(prompt)
        optimized_prompt = prompt
        techniques_applied = []
        
        # Apply techniques iteratively until target reached
        for technique in self.techniques:
            if self.get_compression_ratio(original_tokens, optimized_prompt) >= target_compression:
                break
            
            result = await technique.apply(optimized_prompt)
            if result.success and result.tokens_saved > 0:
                optimized_prompt = result.optimized_text
                techniques_applied.append(technique.name)
        
        optimized_tokens = self.count_tokens(optimized_prompt)
        compression_ratio = (original_tokens - optimized_tokens) / original_tokens
        
        # Calculate cost savings (using average model price)
        avg_cost_per_token = 0.000003  # $3 per 1M tokens
        cost_savings = (original_tokens - optimized_tokens) * avg_cost_per_token
        
        return OptimizationResult(
            original_tokens=original_tokens,
            optimized_tokens=optimized_tokens,
            compression_ratio=compression_ratio,
            cost_savings=cost_savings,
            optimized_prompt=optimized_prompt,
            techniques_applied=techniques_applied
        )
    
    def count_tokens(self, text: str) -> int:
        """Count tokens using tiktoken"""
        import tiktoken
        encoder = tiktoken.get_encoding("cl100k_base")
        return len(encoder.encode(text))
    
    def get_compression_ratio(self, original: int, optimized: int) -> float:
        return (original - optimized) / original


class WhitespaceOptimizer:
    """Removes unnecessary whitespace"""
    name = "whitespace_optimization"
    
    async def apply(self, text: str) -> OptimizationResult:
        import re
        
        # Remove multiple spaces
        optimized = re.sub(r' {2,}', ' ', text)
        
        # Remove trailing whitespace
        optimized = re.sub(r'[ \t]+$', '', optimized, flags=re.MULTILINE)
        
        # Remove blank lines
        optimized = re.sub(r'\n{3,}', '\n\n', optimized)
        
        tokens_saved = len(text) - len(optimized)
        
        return OptimizationResult(
            success=tokens_saved > 0,
            tokens_saved=tokens_saved,
            optimized_text=optimized
        )


class CommentRemover:
    """Removes code comments while preserving structure"""
    name = "comment_removal"
    
    async def apply(self, text: str) -> OptimizationResult:
        import re
        
        # Remove single-line comments
        optimized = re.sub(r'//.*$', '', text, flags=re.MULTILINE)
        
        # Remove multi-line comments
        optimized = re.sub(r'/\*.*?\*/', '', optimized, flags=re.DOTALL)
        
        # Remove docstrings (Python)
        optimized = re.sub(r'""".*?"""', '', optimized, flags=re.DOTALL)
        optimized = re.sub(r"'''.*?'''", '', optimized, flags=re.DOTALL)
        
        tokens_saved = len(text) - len(optimized)
        
        return OptimizationResult(
            success=tokens_saved > 0,
            tokens_saved=tokens_saved,
            optimized_text=optimized
        )


class ContextPruner:
    """Intelligently prunes less relevant context"""
    name = "context_pruning"
    
    async def apply(self, text: str) -> OptimizationResult:
        # This would use NLP to identify and remove less relevant sections
        # For now, simple heuristic: remove very old context
        
        lines = text.split('\n')
        
        # Keep first 10 lines (likely important)
        # Keep last 50 lines (most recent context)
        # Remove middle if too long
        
        if len(lines) > 200:
            optimized_lines = lines[:10] + ['... [context truncated] ...'] + lines[-50:]
            optimized = '\n'.join(optimized_lines)
        else:
            optimized = text
        
        tokens_saved = len(text) - len(optimized)
        
        return OptimizationResult(
            success=tokens_saved > 0,
            tokens_saved=tokens_saved,
            optimized_text=optimized
        )
```

### 5.1 Multi-Dimensional Analytics API

```java
// ============================================
// FINOPS ANALYTICS CONTROLLER
// ============================================

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/finops/analytics")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class FinOpsAnalyticsController {
    
    private final FinOpsAnalyticsService analyticsService;
    
    /**
     * Get cost breakdown by multiple dimensions
     */
    @GetMapping("/cost-breakdown")
    public CompletableFuture<ResponseEntity<CostBreakdownResponse>> getCostBreakdown(
        @RequestParam String startDate,
        @RequestParam String endDate,
        @RequestParam List<String> dimensions,
        @RequestParam(required = false) String lobCode
    ) {
        CostBreakdownQuery query = CostBreakdownQuery.builder()
            .startDate(LocalDate.parse(startDate))
            .endDate(LocalDate.parse(endDate))
            .dimensions(dimensions) // ["user", "model", "ide", "project"]
            .lobCode(lobCode)
            .build();
        
        CostBreakdownResponse breakdown = analyticsService.getCostBreakdown(query);
        
        return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(
            ResponseEntity.ok(breakdown)
        );
    }
    
    /**
     * Get top cost drivers
     */
    @GetMapping("/top-cost-drivers")
    public CompletableFuture<ResponseEntity<TopCostDriversResponse>> getTopCostDrivers(
        @RequestParam String period, // "day", "week", "month"
        @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int limit
    ) {
        TopCostDriversResponse drivers = analyticsService.getTopCostDrivers(period, limit);
        return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(ResponseEntity.ok(drivers));
    }
    
    /**
     * Get cost trends and forecasting
     */
    @GetMapping("/trends")
    public CompletableFuture<ResponseEntity<CostTrendsResponse>> getCostTrends(
        @RequestParam String startDate,
        @RequestParam String endDate,
        @RequestParam String granularity // "day", "week", "month"
    ) {
        CostTrendsResponse trends = analyticsService.getCostTrends(
            LocalDate.parse(startDate),
            LocalDate.parse(endDate),
            granularity
        );
        
        return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(ResponseEntity.ok(trends));
    }
    
    /**
     * Get optimization recommendations
     */
    @GetMapping("/optimization-recommendations")
    public CompletableFuture<ResponseEntity<OptimizationRecommendationsResponse>> 
    getOptimizationRecommendations(
        @RequestParam(required = false) String scopeType,
        @RequestParam(required = false) String scopeId
    ) {
        OptimizationRecommendationsResponse recommendations = 
            analyticsService.getOptimizationRecommendations(scopeType, scopeId);
        
        return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(ResponseEntity.ok(recommendations));
    }
}
```


## Part 9: Integration with Existing ARIA Architecture

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    ARIA PLATFORM (Complete)                     │
│                                                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │              TRUST MODEL (Existing)                      │  │
│  │  • Agent DNA Profiles                                    │  │
│  │  • Trust Scores                                          │  │
│  │  • Decision Archaeology                                  │  │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                     │                                          │
│                     ▼                                          │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │              FINOPS LAYER (New)                          │  │
│  │  • Cost Tracking                                         │  │
│  │  • Model Optimization                                    │  │
│  │  • Budget Enforcement                                    │  │
│  │  • Token Compression                                     │  │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                     │                                          │
│                     ▼                                          │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │           GOVERNANCE DECISION ENGINE                     │  │
│  │                                                          │  │
│  │  Decision = f(Trust Score, Cost, Risk, Budget)          │  │
│  │                                                          │  │
│  │  Example Logic:                                          │  │
│  │  IF trust_score > 0.80 AND cost < budget THEN ALLOW     │  │
│  │  IF cost > budget THEN REQUIRES_APPROVAL                │  │
│  │  IF trust_score < 0.40 AND high_cost THEN BLOCK         │  │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Integration Points:**

1. **Trust Score → Model Selection:**
   - High-trust agents (≥0.80) get access to premium models (Opus, GPT-4)
   - Low-trust agents (<0.40) restricted to cost-effective models (Haiku, GPT-4o-mini)

2. **Cost → Trust Score:**
   - Agents with high cost-per-value ratio see trust score penalties
   - Efficient agents (low cost, high quality) get trust bonuses

3. **Budget → Autonomy:**
   - Teams within budget → higher autonomy
   - Teams over budget → require approval for expensive operations

## 📋 EXECUTIVE SUMMARY & DESIGN PRINCIPLES

### 🎯 Business Objective
Eliminate the AI cost black box by deploying a **modular, plugin-driven FinOps platform** that:
1. Tracks 100% of LLM/token spend across every dimension (user, IDE, model, LOB, org, app, prompt, use-case)
2. Optimizes spend via intelligent model routing, token compression, semantic caching, and budget enforcement
3. Integrates natively with ARIA's Trust Model to align cost efficiency with agent autonomy
4. Delivers executive-grade analytics, forecasting, and compliance-ready audit trails

### 🔑 Architectural Decisions
| Decision | Rationale |
|----------|-----------|
| **Oracle 23c AI Database** | Native vector search, JSON relational duality, VPD for multi-tenancy, Autonomous scaling, OML for forecasting |
| **Oracle VPD (Row-Level Security)** | Enforces strict data isolation per LOB/Org/User without application-layer filters |
| **Time-Series Partitioning** | Monthly range partitions on cost transactions for sub-second analytics & automated 7-year archival |
| **Plugin-First Design** | IDE interceptors, MCP gateways, CI/CD hooks, and scanner adapters implement a uniform contract |
| **Async Event Pipeline** | Kafka/Pulsar → Oracle via Oracle GoldenGate or native async inserts to keep governance latency <3s |
| **Trust-Cost Feedback Loop** | High-trust agents get premium models; cost-inefficient agents trigger trust penalties |

## ️ PHASE 1: ORACLE 23C DATA MODEL & SECURITY

### 1.1 Core Schema DDL (Oracle 23c Syntax)
```sql
-- ============================================
-- ARIA FINOPS SCHEMA — ORACLE 23C AI DATABASE
-- ============================================

-- 1. MODEL PRICING CATALOG
CREATE TABLE finops_model_pricing (
    pricing_id          NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    provider            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    model_version       VARCHAR2(50),
    input_price_per_1k  NUMBER(10,6) NOT NULL,
    output_price_per_1k NUMBER(10,6) NOT NULL,
    cached_price_per_1k NUMBER(10,6),
    max_context_tokens  INTEGER NOT NULL,
    capabilities        JSON,
    is_active           CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y' CHECK (is_active IN ('Y','N')),
    effective_from      TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    effective_to        TIMESTAMP,
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 2. COST TRANSACTIONS (Time-Series Partitioned)
CREATE TABLE finops_cost_transaction (
    transaction_id      NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id          VARCHAR2(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp     TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    
    -- Agent & User Context
    agent_id            VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    user_id             VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    user_email          VARCHAR2(255),
    
    -- IDE & Environment
    ide_type            VARCHAR2(50),
    ide_version         VARCHAR2(50),
    plugin_version      VARCHAR2(50),
    environment         VARCHAR2(50) DEFAULT 'DEV',
    
    -- Model & Tokens
    provider            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    model_version       VARCHAR2(50),
    input_tokens        INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens       INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens       INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens        GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_tokens + output_tokens) VIRTUAL,
    
    -- Cost
    input_cost          NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost         NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    cache_discount      NUMBER(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost          GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost - cache_discount) VIRTUAL,
    
    -- Organizational Hierarchy
    project_id          VARCHAR2(100),
    application_name    VARCHAR2(200),
    product_name        VARCHAR2(200),
    lob_code            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    org_unit            VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    cost_center         VARCHAR2(50),
    
    -- Metadata & Optimization
    request_type        VARCHAR2(50),
    prompt_hash         VARCHAR2(64),
    prompt_embedding    VECTOR(1536),
    response_time_ms    INTEGER,
    was_cached          CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N',
    cache_hit_type      VARCHAR2(20),
    optimization_flags  JSON,
    
    -- ARIA Context
    trust_score         NUMBER(3,2),
    decision_id         NUMBER,
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(
    PARTITION p_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2025-01-01 00:00:00')
);

-- 3. DAILY AGGREGATES (Materialized View for Performance)
CREATE TABLE finops_daily_aggregate (
    agg_id              NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    agg_date            DATE NOT NULL,
    user_id             VARCHAR2(255),
    agent_id            VARCHAR2(100),
    lob_code            VARCHAR2(50),
    org_unit            VARCHAR2(100),
    provider            VARCHAR2(50),
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100),
    ide_type            VARCHAR2(50),
    
    total_requests      INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_input_tokens  NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
    total_output_tokens NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
    total_cached_tokens NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost          NUMBER(14,6) DEFAULT 0,
    cache_hit_rate      NUMBER(5,2),
    tokens_saved        INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    cost_saved          NUMBER(14,6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT uq_daily_agg UNIQUE (agg_date, user_id, agent_id, lob_code, org_unit, provider, model_name)
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (agg_date)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(
    PARTITION p_agg_initial VALUES LESS THAN (DATE '2025-01-01')
);

-- 4. BUDGETS & ALERTS
CREATE TABLE finops_budget (
    budget_id           NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    scope_type          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, -- USER, TEAM, LOB, ORG
    scope_id            VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    lob_code            VARCHAR2(50),
    monthly_budget      NUMBER(14,2) NOT NULL,
    warning_threshold   NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.80,
    critical_threshold  NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.95,
    effective_month     DATE NOT NULL,
    approved_by         VARCHAR2(255),
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT uq_budget UNIQUE (scope_type, scope_id, effective_month)
);

CREATE TABLE finops_budget_alert (
    alert_id            NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    budget_id           NUMBER REFERENCES finops_budget(budget_id),
    alert_type          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, -- WARNING, CRITICAL, EXCEEDED
    threshold_pct       NUMBER(5,2) NOT NULL,
    current_spend       NUMBER(14,2) NOT NULL,
    budget_amount       NUMBER(14,2) NOT NULL,
    notification_sent   CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N',
    channels            JSON,
    triggered_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    acknowledged_at     TIMESTAMP,
    acknowledged_by     VARCHAR2(255)
);

-- 5. OPTIMIZATION RECOMMENDATIONS
CREATE TABLE finops_opt_recommendation (
    rec_id              NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    scope_type          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    scope_id            VARCHAR2(255),
    rec_type            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, -- MODEL_DOWNGRADE, CACHING, COMPRESSION
    current_state       JSON NOT NULL,
    recommended_state   JSON NOT NULL,
    est_monthly_savings NUMBER(14,2),
    est_token_reduction INTEGER,
    confidence_score    NUMBER(3,2),
    status              VARCHAR2(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    applied_at          TIMESTAMP,
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 6. SEMANTIC PROMPT CACHE
CREATE TABLE finops_prompt_cache (
    cache_id            NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    prompt_hash         VARCHAR2(64) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    prompt_embedding    VECTOR(1536),
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    cached_response     JSON NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens       INTEGER NOT NULL,
    hit_count           INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_hit_at         TIMESTAMP,
    expires_at          TIMESTAMP,
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- INDEXES FOR ANALYTICS
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_user_ts ON finops_cost_transaction(user_id, event_timestamp DESC) LOCAL;
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_lob_ts ON finops_cost_transaction(lob_code, event_timestamp DESC) LOCAL;
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_model_ts ON finops_cost_transaction(provider, model_name, event_timestamp DESC) LOCAL;
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_org_ts ON finops_cost_transaction(org_unit, lob_code, event_timestamp DESC) LOCAL;
CREATE VECTOR INDEX idx_cache_embedding ON finops_prompt_cache(prompt_embedding) 
    ORGANIZATION NEIGHBOR PARTITIONS 
    DISTANCE COSINE;
```

### 1.2 Oracle VPD (Virtual Private Database) Policies
```sql
-- Enforce LOB-level isolation automatically
BEGIN
    DBMS_RLS.ADD_POLICY(
        object_schema    => 'FINOPS',
        object_name      => 'finops_cost_transaction',
        policy_name      => 'finops_lob_rls',
        function_schema  => 'FINOPS_SEC',
        policy_function  => 'fn_get_lob_predicate',
        statement_types  => 'SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE',
        update_check     => TRUE,
        enable           => TRUE,
        static_policy    => FALSE
    );
END;
/

-- VPD Function (Application Context sets LOB_CODE)
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION finops_sec.fn_get_lob_predicate(
    p_schema IN VARCHAR2,
    p_object IN VARCHAR2
) RETURN VARCHAR2 IS
    v_lob VARCHAR2(50);
BEGIN
    v_lob := SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV', 'CLIENT_IDENTIFIER');
    IF v_lob IS NULL THEN
        RETURN '1=0'; -- Deny if no context
    END IF;
    RETURN 'lob_code = ''' || v_lob || '''';
END;
/
```

---

## ⚙️ PHASE 2: CORE FINOPS ENGINE (JAVA/SPRING BOOT 3.3)

### 2.1 Cost Calculation & Routing Service
```java
// ============================================
// CostCalculationService.java (Spring Boot 3.3 + Java 21)
// ============================================
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
@Slf4j
public class CostCalculationService {
    private final OracleJdbcTemplate oracle;
    private final RedisTemplate<String, Object> redis;
    private final ModelRouter modelRouter;
    private final TokenOptimizer tokenOptimizer;

    @Transactional
    public CostTransactionRecord processRequest(CostIngestionEvent event) {
        // 1. Route to optimal model based on trust & complexity
        RoutingDecision routing = modelRouter.route(event);
        
        // 2. Optimize prompt tokens
        OptimizationResult optimization = tokenOptimizer.compress(event.getPrompt());
        
        // 3. Calculate cost
        ModelPricing pricing = fetchPricing(routing.getModel(), event.getProvider());
        BigDecimal inputCost = calculateCost(optimization.getOptimizedTokens(), 
            pricing.getInputPricePer1k(), optimization.getCachedTokens(), pricing.getCachedPricePer1k());
        BigDecimal outputCost = calculateCost(event.getEstimatedOutputTokens(), pricing.getOutputPricePer1k());
        BigDecimal totalCost = inputCost.add(outputCost);
        
        // 4. Persist transaction (Async batch for performance)
        CostTransactionRecord record = CostTransactionRecord.builder()
            .requestId(event.getRequestId())
            .agentId(event.getAgentId())
            .userId(event.getUserId())
            .ideType(event.getIdeType())
            .provider(routing.getProvider())
            .modelName(routing.getModel())
            .inputTokens(optimization.getOptimizedTokens())
            .outputTokens(event.getEstimatedOutputTokens())
            .cachedTokens(optimization.getCachedTokens())
            .inputCost(inputCost)
            .outputCost(outputCost)
            .totalCost(totalCost)
            .lobCode(event.getLobCode())
            .orgUnit(event.getOrgUnit())
            .trustScore(event.getTrustScore())
            .optimizationFlags(optimization.getFlags())
            .build();
            
        finopsTransactionRepository.save(record);
        
        // 5. Update cache if applicable
        if (optimization.isCached()) {
            updateSemanticCache(event, optimization);
        }
        
        return record;
    }
}
```

### 2.2 Intelligent Model Router
```java
// ============================================
// ModelRouter.java
// ============================================
@Component
public class ModelRouter {
    private final Map<TaskComplexity, List<ModelCandidate>> routingMatrix = Map.of(
        TaskComplexity.SIMPLE, List.of(
            new ModelCandidate("gpt-4o-mini", "openai", 0.00015, 0.0006),
            new ModelCandidate("claude-3-haiku", "anthropic", 0.00025, 0.00125)
        ),
        TaskComplexity.MODERATE, List.of(
            new ModelCandidate("gpt-4o", "openai", 0.005, 0.015),
            new ModelCandidate("claude-3-sonnet", "anthropic", 0.003, 0.015)
        ),
        TaskComplexity.COMPLEX, List.of(
            new ModelCandidate("claude-3-opus", "anthropic", 0.015, 0.075),
            new ModelCandidate("o1-preview", "openai", 0.015, 0.06)
        ),
        TaskComplexity.CRITICAL, List.of(
            new ModelCandidate("claude-3-opus", "anthropic", 0.015, 0.075)
        )
    );

    public RoutingDecision route(CostIngestionEvent event) {
        TaskComplexity complexity = classifyComplexity(event.getPrompt(), event.getContext());
        List<ModelCandidate> candidates = routingMatrix.get(complexity);
        
        // Filter by trust score & budget constraints
        List<ModelCandidate> eligible = candidates.stream()
            .filter(m -> isWithinBudget(m, event.getLobCode()))
            .filter(m -> meetsTrustThreshold(m, event.getTrustScore()))
            .toList();
            
        ModelCandidate selected = eligible.isEmpty() ? candidates.get(0) : 
            eligible.stream().min(Comparator.comparing(ModelCandidate::getCostPer1kInput)).get();
            
        return new RoutingDecision(selected, complexity, generateReasoning(selected, complexity));
    }
}
```

##  PHASE 3: PLUGIN ARCHITECTURE & IDE INTERCEPTION

### 3.1 Plugin Contract (Java Interface)
```java
public interface FinOpsPlugin {
    String pluginId();
    PluginType type(); // IDE_INTERCEPTOR, MCP_GATEWAY, CI_CD_HOOK, SCANNER_ADAPTER
    
    CostIngestionEvent intercept(Object rawPayload);
    void postProcess(CostTransactionRecord record);
    default boolean isEnabled() { return true; }
}
```

### 3.2 VS Code / IntelliJ Interceptor (TypeScript/Java)
```typescript
// aria-finops-vscode/src/interceptor.ts
import { CostTracker } from './cost-tracker';

export class IDECostInterceptor {
  private tracker: CostTracker;
  
  constructor(config: PluginConfig) {
    this.tracker = new CostTracker(config);
  }

  async onLLMRequest(request: any, metadata: any): Promise<void> {
    const event: CostIngestionEvent = {
      requestId: crypto.randomUUID(),
      agentId: metadata.agentId || 'github-copilot',
      userId: metadata.userId,
      ideType: 'vscode',
      ideVersion: vscode.version,
      prompt: request.messages[0].content,
      provider: request.model.split('/')[0],
      model: request.model,
      lobCode: config.lobCode,
      orgUnit: config.orgUnit,
      trustScore: metadata.ariaTrustScore || 0.5,
      context: metadata.filePath ? { file: metadata.filePath, language: metadata.language } : {}
    };

    // Non-blocking async send to ARIA FinOps API
    this.tracker.sendAsync('/api/v1/finops/ingest', event);
  }
}
```
