## 📊 PHASE 4: EXECUTIVE ANALYTICS & DASHBOARDS

### 4.1 Multi-Dimensional Aggregation Query (Oracle 23c)
```sql
-- Executive Cost Breakdown by LOB, Product, Model
SELECT 
    lob_code,
    product_name,
    model_name,
    SUM(total_requests) AS total_requests,
    SUM(total_cost) AS total_cost,
    SUM(total_input_tokens) + SUM(total_output_tokens) AS total_tokens,
    ROUND(SUM(total_cached_tokens) * 100.0 / NULLIF(SUM(total_input_tokens),0), 2) AS cache_hit_pct,
    ROUND(SUM(cost_saved), 2) AS optimization_savings
FROM finops_daily_aggregate
WHERE agg_date BETWEEN :start_date AND :end_date
  AND lob_code IN (SELECT lob_code FROM finops_access_context WHERE user_id = SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV','CLIENT_IDENTIFIER'))
GROUP BY lob_code, product_name, model_name
ORDER BY total_cost DESC;
```

### 4.2 Forecasting Engine (Oracle Machine Learning)
```sql
-- OML Time-Series Forecasting (30/60/90 day)
BEGIN
    DBMS_DATA_MINING.CREATE_MODEL(
        model_name          => 'FINOPS_COST_FORECAST',
        mining_function     => DBMS_DATA_MINING.TIME_SERIES,
        data_table_name     => 'finops_daily_aggregate',
        case_id_column_name => 'agg_date',
        target_column_name  => 'total_cost',
        settings_table_name => 'forecast_settings'
    );
END;
/

-- Query forecast
SELECT PREDICTION(FINOPS_COST_FORECAST USING agg_date AS date, total_cost AS value) AS forecasted_cost
FROM DUAL CONNECT BY LEVEL <= 90;
```

## 🔗 PHASE 5: ARIA TRUST MODEL INTEGRATION

### 5.1 Trust-Cost Feedback Loop
| Metric | Impact on Trust Score | Impact on Cost Autonomy |
|--------|----------------------|------------------------|
| **Cost Efficiency Ratio** (Value delivered / $ spent) | +0.05 if > 1.2x baseline | Unlocks premium models (Opus/GPT-4o) |
| **Token Waste Rate** (Redundant/context bloat) | -0.03 if > 40% | Triggers auto-compression plugin |
| **Budget Overrun** | -0.08 per 10% over limit | Drops to REQUIRES_APPROVAL for prod |
| **Cache Hit Rate** | +0.02 if > 35% | Reduces risk weight in scoring |
| **Model Misuse** (Opus for simple tasks) | -0.05 | Forces Haiku/Mini routing |

### 5.2 Decision Archaeology Extension
```json
{
  "decisionId": "DEC-2025-8842",
  "timestamp": "2025-05-16T14:22:11Z",
  "agentId": "copilot-agent-7",
  "trustScoreAtDecision": 0.72,
  "costContext": {
    "estimatedCost": 0.0142,
    "selectedModel": "claude-3-sonnet",
    "routingReason": "Moderate complexity + trust >= 0.70 → Sonnet allowed",
    "optimizationApplied": ["prompt_compression", "exact_cache_miss"],
    "tokensSaved": 1240,
    "budgetUtilization": 0.68
  },
  "finalDecision": "ALLOW",
  "decisionArchaeology": "ARIA allowed deployment. Agent trust (0.72) qualifies for Sonnet. Cost ($0.0142) within LOB budget (68% utilized). Prompt compressed 18%. No security findings."
}
```

## 🛡️ PHASE 6: SECURITY, COMPLIANCE & OBSERVABILITY

### 6.1 Enterprise Controls
| Control | Implementation |
|---------|----------------|
| **Data Isolation** | Oracle VPD + `DBMS_RLS` + Application Context per LOB/Org |
| **Encryption** | Oracle TDE (Transparent Data Encryption) + TLS 1.3 in transit |
| **Audit Trail** | Oracle Unified Auditing → SIEM (Splunk/QRadar) |
| **7-Year Retention** | Oracle Archive/Partition drop → Object Store WORM (S3/GCS with Object Lock) |
| **SOX/DORA Mapping** | Immutable `finops_cost_transaction` + `decision_archaeology` JSON |
| **PII Safety** | Regex/NLP scrubbing before ingestion; never stored in raw form |

### 6.2 Observability Stack
```yaml
metrics:
  - aria_finops.cost_per_request (histogram)
  - aria_finops.tokens_per_request (histogram)
  - aria_finops.cache_hit_rate (gauge)
  - aria_finops.budget_utilization (gauge)
  - aria_finops.routing_accuracy (counter)
  
alerts:
  - p95_cost > $0.05 → PagerDuty
  - budget_utilization > 0.85 → Slack + JIRA
  - cache_hit_rate < 0.15 → Optimization recommendation trigger
  - trust_cost_mismatch > 0.2 → ARIA calibration alert
```

# 1. Plugin Hot-Reload (Zero Downtime)

# 2. Trust-Cost Calibration
java -cp aria-finops-cli.jar com.jpmc.aria.FinOpsCalibrator \
  --period=30d --lob=DIGITAL --threshold=0.75 --dry-run=true

# 3. Emergency Budget Circuit Breaker
curl -X POST https://aria-finops.internal/api/v1/admin/circuit-breaker/activate \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $ADMIN_TOKEN" \
  -d '{"scope":"LOB","scopeId":"DIGITAL","maxCostPerRequest":0.02}'

# 4. 7-Year Archive Execution (Scheduled)
BEGIN
  FOR p IN (SELECT partition_name FROM user_tab_partitions 
            WHERE table_name='FINOPS_COST_TRANSACTION' 
            AND partition_position <= 60) LOOP
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'ALTER TABLE finops_cost_transaction EXCHANGE PARTITION ' || p.partition_name || 
      ' WITH TABLE finops_cost_archive INCLUDING INDEXES WITHOUT VALIDATION';
    DBMS_CLOUD.OBJECT.PUT(uri => 'os://finops-archive/' || p.partition_name || '.parquet', 
                          credential_name => 'ARCH_CREDS');
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'ALTER TABLE finops_cost_transaction DROP PARTITION ' || p.partition_name;
  END LOOP;
END;
/
```

## 📐 PART 1: SPECIFICATION-DRIVEN DEVELOPMENT (SDD) FOUNDATION

SDD means **specs dictate implementation, validation gates deployment, and contracts guarantee interoperability**. We define three core specs that drive all code generation, testing, and plugin distribution.

### 1.1 Core SDD Specs
| Spec Type | Purpose | Format | Validation Tool |
|-----------|---------|--------|-----------------|
| `skill-manifest.spec.json` | Skill identity, permissions, routing, cost rules | JSON Schema Draft-07 | `ajv-cli` + custom validators |
| `ide-plugin.contract.yaml` | IDE ↔ FinOps API request/response shapes | OpenAPI 3.1 + WebSocket | `spectral` + `openapi-generator` |
| `cost-delta.schema.json` | Baseline vs Optimized calculation contract | JSON Schema + math constraints | `math-schema-validator` + unit tests |

### 1.2 Skill Manifest Specification (SDD Source of Truth)
```json
{
  "$schema": "https://aria.finops/specs/skill-manifest/v1.2.0.json",
  "skillId": "aria-cost-optimizer",
  "version": "1.2.0",
  "name": "Cost Optimizer & Delta Visualizer",
  "description": "Intercepts LLM calls, applies routing/compression/caching, calculates baseline vs optimized cost, and renders savings in IDE.",
  "specVersion": "1.0",
  "executionContract": {
    "input": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["requestId", "prompt", "model", "userId", "lobCode"],
      "properties": {
        "requestId": { "type": "string", "format": "uuid" },
        "prompt": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "model": { "type": "string" },
        "userId": { "type": "string" },
        "lobCode": { "type": "string" },
        "trustScore": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 1 }
      }
    },
    "output": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["baselineCost", "optimizedCost", "savingsDelta", "appliedOptimizations"],
      "properties": {
        "baselineCost": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 },
        "optimizedCost": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0 },
        "savingsDelta": { "type": "number" },
        "savingsPercent": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 100 },
        "appliedOptimizations": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } },
        "routedModel": { "type": "string" },
        "cacheHit": { "type": "boolean" }
      }
    }
  },
  "configSchema": {
    "type": "object",
    "properties": {
      "routingRules": { "type": "object" },
      "compressionThreshold": { "type": "number", "default": 0.3 },

        "type": "array",

          }

      }
    }
  },
  "permissions": ["read:llm_gateway", "write:cost_ledger", "read:trust_registry"],
  "costImpactRules": {
    "baselineMultiplier": 1.0,
    "optimizedMultiplier": 0.42,
    "reportingIntervalMs": 5000
  },
  "signingKey": "sha256:ARIA-SKILL-SIG-PROD-2026",
  "generatedArtifacts": ["ide-plugin.ts", "skill-runtime.jar", "openapi-client.java"]
}
```

## 🔌 PART 2: AGENTIC SKILLS RUNTIME & IDE EXECUTION

Skills are **sandboxed, config-driven units** that run locally in the IDE or remotely via ARIA Gateway. Each skill implements a strict contract, reads workspace config, and routes to configurable services.

### 2.1 Skill Runtime Architecture
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    IDE (VS Code / IntelliJ)                 │
│                                                             │
│  ┌─────────────────┐    ┌─────────────────────────────────┐ │
│  │ ARIA Skill Loader│───▶│ Skill Runtime (Sandboxed)       │ │
│  │ - Discovers      │    │ - Validates manifest            │ │
│  │ - Loads config   │    │ - Enforces permissions          │ │
│  │ - Injects LSP    │    │ - Routes to target services     │ │
│  ─────────────────┘    └───────────────┬─────────────────┘ │
│                                         │                   │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────                   │
│  │ Configurable Service Router (per LOB/Team)               │
│  │ - billing-api.internal                                    │
│  │ - llm-gateway.prod                                        │
│  │ - analytics-olap.aria                                     │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 2.2 IDE Plugin: Cost Calculator + Optimizer + Delta Visualizer
**Framework:** VS Code Extension API / JetBrains Plugin SDK (Kotlin)
**Language:** TypeScript (VS Code) / Kotlin (IntelliJ)
**Architecture:** LSP-based interceptor + WebSocket stream + Inline Diff Provider

#### 2.2.1 Core Interception & Delta Engine (TypeScript)
```typescript
// aria-finops-plugin/src/cost-delta-engine.ts
import { LLMRequest, LLMResponse, SkillConfig } from './types';
import { ARIAGatewayClient } from './gateway-client';

export class CostDeltaEngine {
  private gateway: ARIAGatewayClient;
  private config: SkillConfig;
  private savingsHistory: SavingsEvent[] = [];

  constructor(config: SkillConfig) {
    this.config = config;
    this.gateway = new ARIAGatewayClient(config.targetServices.ariaEndpoint);
  }

  async interceptAndOptimize(request: LLMRequest): Promise<CostDeltaResult> {
    // 1. Calculate BASELINE (Without ARIA)
    const baseline = this.calculateBaselineCost(request);

    // 2. Send to ARIA for optimization
    const optimized = await this.gateway.optimizeRequest(request);

    // 3. Calculate OPTIMIZED (With ARIA)
    const optimizedCost = this.calculateOptimizedCost(optimized);

    // 4. Compute DELTA
    const delta = baseline.cost - optimizedCost.cost;
    const savingsPct = (delta / baseline.cost) * 100;

    // 5. Persist & Stream to IDE UI
    const result: CostDeltaResult = {
      requestId: request.requestId,
      baseline,
      optimized: optimizedCost,
      delta,
      savingsPct: Math.round(savingsPct * 10) / 10,
      appliedOptimizations: optimized.optimizations,
      routedModel: optimized.routedModel,
      cacheHit: optimized.cacheHit
    };

    this.savingsHistory.push({
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      delta,
      savingsPct,
      userId: request.userId
    });

    // Stream to IDE status bar & inline diff
    this.ui.renderStatusBar(result);
    this.ui.renderInlineDiff(request.range, result);

    return result;
  }

  private calculateBaselineCost(req: LLMRequest): CostBreakdown {
    const listPrice = this.config.pricingCatalog[req.model];
    const inputCost = (req.inputTokens / 1000) * listPrice.input;
    const outputCost = (req.estimatedOutputTokens / 1000) * listPrice.output;
    return {
      cost: inputCost + outputCost,
      inputTokens: req.inputTokens,
      outputTokens: req.estimatedOutputTokens,
      model: req.model,
      priceSource: 'list_price'
    };
  }

  private calculateOptimizedCost(opt: OptimizedPayload): CostBreakdown {
    return {
      cost: opt.totalCost,
      inputTokens: opt.optimizedInputTokens,
      outputTokens: opt.estimatedOutputTokens,
      model: opt.routedModel,
      priceSource: 'aria_routed'
    };
  }
}
```

#### 2.2.2 IDE UI Integration (Status Bar + Inline Diff)
```typescript
// aria-finops-plugin/src/ui/status-bar.ts
import * as vscode from 'vscode';

export class StatusBarRenderer {
  private item: vscode.StatusBarItem;

  constructor() {
    this.item = vscode.window.createStatusBarItem(vscode.StatusBarAlignment.Right, 100);
    this.item.command = 'aria.showSavingsReport';
    this.item.show();
  }

  render(result: CostDeltaResult) {
    const icon = result.delta > 0 ? '💰' : '⚡';
    const savings = result.delta > 0 
      ? `Saved $${result.delta.toFixed(4)} (${result.savingsPct}%)`
      : 'Optimized';
    
    this.item.text = `${icon} ARIA: ${savings} | ${result.routedModel} | Cache: ${result.cacheHit ? '✅' : '❌'}`;
    this.item.tooltip = `Baseline: $${result.baseline.cost.toFixed(4)}\nOptimized: $${result.optimized.cost.toFixed(4)}\nTokens: ${result.baseline.inputTokens}→${result.optimized.inputTokens}`;
  }
}
```

## 🗄️ PART 3: ORACLE 23C SCHEMA EXTENSIONS (SDD + SKILLS + SAVINGS)

### 3.1 Skill Registry & Config Storage
```sql
-- ARIA Skills Registry (JSON Relational Duality View enabled)
CREATE TABLE finops_skills (
    skill_id          VARCHAR2(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    version           VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
    manifest          JSON NOT NULL,
    config_schema     JSON NOT NULL,
    execution_contract JSON NOT NULL,
    signing_key       VARCHAR2(128),
    is_active         CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y',
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Per-LOB/Team Skill Configuration
CREATE TABLE finops_skill_configs (
    config_id         NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    skill_id          VARCHAR2(100) REFERENCES finops_skills(skill_id),
    lob_code          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    org_unit          VARCHAR2(100),
    config_payload    JSON NOT NULL,
    applied_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    applied_by        VARCHAR2(255),
    CONSTRAINT uq_skill_lob UNIQUE (skill_id, lob_code)
);

-- Real-Time Savings Ledger (Time-Series Partitioned)
CREATE TABLE finops_savings_ledger (
    event_id          NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id        VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp   TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    user_id           VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    lob_code          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    baseline_cost     NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    optimized_cost    NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    savings_delta     NUMBER(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (baseline_cost - optimized_cost) VIRTUAL,
    savings_percent   NUMBER(5,2),
    applied_optimizations JSON,
    routed_model      VARCHAR2(100),
    cache_hit         CHAR(1),
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(
    PARTITION p_savings_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2025-01-01 00:00:00')
);

-- JSON Relational Duality View for Easy Querying
CREATE JSON RELATIONAL DUALITY VIEW finops_savings_dv AS
SELECT JSON {
    'eventId' : s.event_id,
    'requestId' : s.request_id,
    'timestamp' : s.event_timestamp,
    'userId' : s.user_id,
    'lobCode' : s.lob_code,
    'costComparison' : {
        'baseline' : s.baseline_cost,
        'optimized' : s.optimized_cost,
        'delta' : s.savings_delta,
        'savingsPercent' : s.savings_percent
    },
    'optimizations' : s.applied_optimizations,
    'routedModel' : s.routed_model,
    'cacheHit' : s.cache_hit
}
FROM finops_savings_ledger s
WITH INSERT UPDATE DELETE;
```

## 🔄 PART 4: SDD CI/CD & VALIDATION PIPELINE

SDD enforces **spec-first development, contract testing, and automated artifact generation**.

### 4.1 SDD Pipeline Stages
```yaml
# .github/workflows/sdd-finops.yml
name: SDD-FinOps-Skills-Validation
on: [push, pull_request]

jobs:
  validate-specs:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Validate Skill Manifests
        run: npx ajv-cli validate -s specs/skill-manifest.spec.json -d skills/**/*.json
      - name: Validate IDE Contract
        run: spectral lint ide-plugin.contract.yaml

  generate-scaffolding:
    needs: validate-specs
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Generate IDE Plugin (TS)
        run: openapi-generator-cli generate -i ide-plugin.contract.yaml -g typescript-axios -o plugins/ide/vscode
      - name: Generate Backend Client (Java)
        run: openapi-generator-cli generate -i ide-plugin.contract.yaml -g spring -o backend/clients/java

  contract-tests:
    needs: generate-scaffolding
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Run Contract Tests
        run: ./gradlew contractTest --tests "aria.finops.contract.*"
      - name: Validate Cost Delta Math
        run: ./gradlew test --tests "aria.finops.engine.CostDeltaEngineTest"

  sign-and-publish:
    needs: contract-tests
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Sign Skill Artifacts
        run: ./scripts/sign-skills.sh --key-id ${{ secrets.SIGNING_KEY }}
      - name: Publish to Oracle Registry
        run: ./scripts/publish-to-oracle.sh --registry ${ARIA_ORACLE_ENDPOINT}
```

### 4.2 SDD Enforcement Rules
| Rule | Enforcement | Gate |
|------|-------------|------|
| Manifest schema compliance | `ajv-cli` + custom validators | PR merge blocked if invalid |
| IDE contract compatibility | `spectral` + backward-compat check | Fails if breaking change |
| Cost delta math accuracy | Unit tests with ε ≤ 0.000001 | CI fails if drift > 0.01% |
| Permission boundaries | VPD + runtime capability checks | Blocked if over-privileged |
| Signature verification | SHA-256 + HSM-backed signing | Plugin rejected if unsigned |

## 📐 PART 1: SDD CONTRACT REGISTRY & PLUGIN SPECIFICATION
*Specification-Driven Development mandates that every component is defined by strict, versioned contracts before code generation. Aligns with ARIA's "Plugin Registry" and "execution/agent plugins" from the architecture doc.*

### 1.1 Core SDD Contracts
| Contract | Purpose | Format | Validation Gate |
|----------|---------|--------|-----------------|
| `aria-finops-skill.spec.json` | Skill identity, permissions, routing, cost rules | JSON Schema Draft-07 | `ajv-cli` + signature verification |
| `ide-interceptor.contract.yaml` | IDE ↔ ARIA FinOps API request/response | OpenAPI 3.1 + WebSocket | `spectral` + backward-compat check |
| `trust-cost-feedback.schema.json` | Mapping FinOps metrics → Trust Score deltas | JSON Schema + math constraints | Unit test ε ≤ 0.0001 drift |

### 1.2 Skill Manifest (SDD Source of Truth)
```json
{
  "$schema": "https://aria.jpmc/specs/finops-skill/v1.0.json",
  "skillId": "aria-cost-optimizer",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "name": "Cost Optimizer & Delta Visualizer",
  "specVersion": "1.0",
  "executionContract": {
    "input": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["requestId", "prompt", "model", "agentId", "lobCode"],
      "properties": {
        "requestId": { "type": "string", "format": "uuid" },
        "prompt": { "type": "string" },
        "model": { "type": "string" },
        "agentId": { "type": "string" },
        "lobCode": { "type": "string" },
        "trustScore": { "type": "number", "minimum": 0.0, "maximum": 1.0 }
      }
    },
    "output": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["baselineCost", "optimizedCost", "savingsDelta", "appliedOptimizations", "trustImpact"],
      "properties": {
        "baselineCost": { "type": "number" },
        "optimizedCost": { "type": "number" },
        "savingsDelta": { "type": "number" },
        "savingsPercent": { "type": "number" },
        "appliedOptimizations": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } },
        "trustImpact": { "type": "object", "properties": { "delta": { "type": "number" }, "reason": { "type": "string" } } }
      }
    }
  },
  "configSchema": {
    "type": "object",
    "properties": {
      "routingRules": { "type": "object" },
      "compressionThreshold": { "type": "number", "default": 0.3 },
      "cacheTTLSeconds": { "type": "number", "default": 3600 },
      "targetServices": { "type": "array" }
    }
  },
  "permissions": ["read:llm_gateway", "write:cost_ledger", "read:trust_registry", "update:agent_dna"],
  "signingKey": "sha256:ARIA-SKILL-SIG-PROD-2026",

## 🗄️ PART 2: ORACLE 23C SCHEMA (TRUST + FINOPS + SKILLS)
*Replaces PostgreSQL entirely. Uses VPD, JSON Relational Duality, Interval Partitioning, Vector Search, and Autonomous scaling. Aligns with ARIA's Agent DNA Registry, Cost Intelligence, and Plugin Store.*

### 2.1 Core Tables & Duality Views
```sql
-- 1. AGENT DNA REGISTRY (Trust Model Schema)
CREATE TABLE aria_agent_dna (
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    agent_type        VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,          -- Copilot, Claude, MCP
    trust_score       NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.30 CHECK (trust_score BETWEEN 0.0 AND 1.0),
    total_prs         INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    blocked_prs       INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    prod_incidents    INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    trend             VARCHAR2(20) DEFAULT 'NEW' CHECK (trend IN ('IMPROVING','STABLE','DECLINING','NEW')),
    recent_activity   JSON,                            -- Rolling window of trust scores
    specializations   JSON,                            -- ["Java","K8s","Auth"]
    last_incident     VARCHAR2(500),
    cost_efficiency   NUMBER(5,2) DEFAULT 1.00,        -- Value delivered / $ spent
    token_waste_rate  NUMBER(5,2) DEFAULT 0.0,         -- Redundant/context bloat %
    budget_compliance NUMBER(5,2) DEFAULT 1.00,        -- 1.0 = within budget
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 2. COST TRANSACTION (Time-Series Partitioned)
CREATE TABLE aria_cost_transaction (
    transaction_id    NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id        VARCHAR2(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp   TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL REFERENCES aria_agent_dna(agent_id),
    user_id           VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    ide_type          VARCHAR2(50),
    provider          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name        VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens      INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens     INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens     INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    input_cost        NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost       NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    total_cost        GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost) VIRTUAL,
    lob_code          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    org_unit          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    optimization_flags JSON,
    decision_id       VARCHAR2(100),
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(PARTITION p_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2025-01-01 00:00:00'));

-- 3. SAVINGS LEDGER (Baseline vs Optimized)
CREATE TABLE aria_savings_ledger (
    event_id          NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id        VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp   TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    baseline_cost     NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    optimized_cost    NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    savings_delta     NUMBER(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (baseline_cost - optimized_cost) VIRTUAL,
    savings_percent   NUMBER(5,2),
    applied_optimizations JSON,
    routed_model      VARCHAR2(100),
    cache_hit         CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N',
    trust_delta_applied NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.0,
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(PARTITION p_savings_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2025-01-01 00:00:00'));

-- 4. SKILL REGISTRY (Plugin Store)
CREATE TABLE aria_skill_registry (
    skill_id          VARCHAR2(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    version           VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
    manifest          JSON NOT NULL,
    execution_contract JSON NOT NULL,
    signing_key       VARCHAR2(128),
    is_active         CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y',
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- JSON RELATIONAL DUALITY VIEWS (Zero-ETL Analytics)
CREATE JSON RELATIONAL DUALITY VIEW aria_agent_dna_dv AS
SELECT JSON {
    'agentId' : d.agent_id,
    'trustScore' : d.trust_score,
    'trend' : d.trend,
    'costEfficiency' : d.cost_efficiency,
    'tokenWasteRate' : d.token_waste_rate,
    'specializations' : d.specializations
} FROM aria_agent_dna d;

CREATE JSON RELATIONAL DUALITY VIEW aria_savings_dv AS
SELECT JSON {
    'eventId' : s.event_id,
    'agentId' : s.agent_id,
    'costComparison' : {
        'baseline' : s.baseline_cost,
        'optimized' : s.optimized_cost,
        'delta' : s.savings_delta,
        'percent' : s.savings_percent
    },
    'trustImpact' : s.trust_delta_applied,
    'optimizations' : s.applied_optimizations
} FROM aria_savings_ledger s;
```

### 2.2 Oracle VPD (Row-Level Security)
```sql
-- Enforce LOB/Org isolation automatically
BEGIN
    DBMS_RLS.ADD_POLICY(
        object_schema    => 'ARIA',
        object_name      => 'aria_cost_transaction',
        policy_name      => 'aria_lob_rls',
        function_schema  => 'ARIA_SEC',
        policy_function  => 'fn_get_lob_predicate',
        statement_types  => 'SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE',
        update_check     => TRUE,
        enable           => TRUE
    );
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION aria_sec.fn_get_lob_predicate(
    p_schema IN VARCHAR2, p_object IN VARCHAR2
) RETURN VARCHAR2 IS
    v_lob VARCHAR2(50) := SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV', 'CLIENT_IDENTIFIER');
BEGIN
    IF v_lob IS NULL THEN RETURN '1=0'; END IF;
    RETURN 'lob_code = ''' || v_lob || '''';
END;
/
```

└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

### 3.2 Cost Delta Engine (TypeScript)
```typescript
// aria-finops-plugin/src/cost-delta-engine.ts
import { LLMRequest, SkillConfig } from './types';
import { ARIAGatewayClient } from './gateway-client';

export class CostDeltaEngine {
  private gateway: ARIAGatewayClient;
  private config: SkillConfig;

  constructor(config: SkillConfig) {
    this.config = config;
    this.gateway = new ARIAGatewayClient(config.targetServices.ariaEndpoint);
  }

  async interceptAndOptimize(request: LLMRequest): Promise<CostDeltaResult> {
    // 1. BASELINE (Without ARIA)
    const baseline = this.calculateBaselineCost(request);

    // 2. OPTIMIZE (With ARIA)
    const optimized = await this.gateway.optimizeRequest(request);

    // 3. DELTA
    const delta = baseline.cost - optimized.cost;
    const savingsPct = (delta / baseline.cost) * 100;

    // 4. TRUST IMPACT
    const trustImpact = await this.calculateTrustImpact(request.agentId, savingsPct, optimized.optimizations);

    return {
      requestId: request.requestId,
      baseline,
      optimized,
      delta,
      savingsPct: Math.round(savingsPct * 10) / 10,
      trustImpact,
      ui: { icon: delta > 0 ? '💰' : '⚡', text: `Saved $${delta.toFixed(4)} (${savingsPct}%)` }
    };
  }

  private calculateBaselineCost(req: LLMRequest): CostBreakdown {
    const price = this.config.pricingCatalog[req.model];
    return {
      cost: (req.inputTokens / 1000) * price.input + (req.estimatedOutputTokens / 1000) * price.output,
      model: req.model, priceSource: 'list_price'
    };
  }

  private async calculateTrustImpact(agentId: string, savingsPct: number, optimizations: string[]): Promise<TrustImpact> {
    const response = await this.gateway.post('/api/v1/trust/calculate-delta', { agentId, savingsPct, optimizations });
    return response.data;
  }
}
```

## 🔄 PART 4: TRUST-COST FEEDBACK ENGINE
*Maps FinOps metrics directly to ARIA's Trust Model Schema. Aligns with "Production Feedback Loop" and "Adaptive Risk Model".*

### 4.1 Mathematical Mapping
| FinOps Metric | Trust Schema Field | Impact Formula | Trust Band Effect |
|---------------|-------------------|----------------|-------------------|
| `savings_percent ≥ 30%` | `trust_score` | `+0.02` (clean efficiency) | Moves toward HIGH/ELITE |
| `token_waste_rate > 40%` | `trend` | `DECLINING` if sustained 3 cycles | Drops to LOW/CRITICAL |
| `budget_compliance < 0.85` | `trust_score` | `-0.05` per 10% overage | Triggers REQUIRES_APPROVAL |
| `cache_hit_rate ≥ 35%` | `cost_efficiency` | `+0.01` efficiency bonus | Reduces risk weight |
| `model_misuse_rate > 20%` | `trust_score` | `-0.03` (Opus for simple tasks) | Forces Haiku/Mini routing |

### 4.2 Trust Delta Calculation Service (Java/Spring Boot 3.3)
```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class TrustCostFeedbackEngine {
    private final OracleJdbcTemplate oracle;
    private final AdaptiveRiskModel riskModel;

    @Transactional
    public TrustDelta applyFinOpsFeedback(String agentId, double savingsPct, List<String> optimizations) {
        // Fetch current DNA
        AgentDNA dna = oracle.queryForObject(
            "SELECT * FROM aria_agent_dna WHERE agent_id = ?", new BeanPropertyRowMapper<>(AgentDNA.class), agentId
        );

        double delta = 0.0;
        String reason = "";

        if (savingsPct >= 30.0) {
            delta += 0.02;
            reason = "High cost efficiency (+30% savings)";
        }
        if (optimizations.contains("prompt_compression")) delta += 0.01;
        if (optimizations.contains("model_downgrade")) delta += 0.005;

        double newScore = Math.min(1.0, Math.max(0.0, dna.getTrustScore() + delta));
        String newTrend = riskModel.calculateTrend(dna.getRecentActivity(), newScore);

        // Update DNA
        oracle.update(
            "UPDATE aria_agent_dna SET trust_score = ?, trend = ?, cost_efficiency = ?, updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP WHERE agent_id = ?",
            newScore, newTrend, dna.getCostEfficiency() + (delta * 10), agentId
        );

        // Persist to savings ledger
        oracle.update(
            "INSERT INTO aria_savings_ledger (request_id, agent_id, trust_delta_applied) VALUES (?, ?, ?)",
            UUID.randomUUID().toString(), agentId, delta
        );

        return new TrustDelta(agentId, delta, newScore, newTrend, reason);
    }
}
```

## 🚦 PART 5: ARIA → ACES DECISION & EXECUTION FLOW
*Aligns with the 6-stage ARIA decision pipeline and ACES core execution. FinOps data directly gates autonomy.*

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    ARIA GOVERNANCE LAYER                        │
│                                                                 │
│  STAGE 1: Request Intake → PR/MCP payload + agentId + context   │
│  STAGE 2: Agent DNA Load → trust_score, trend, cost_efficiency  │
│  STAGE 3: Policy Plugins → PCI, auth, domain, budget rules      │
│  STAGE 4: Signal Aggregation → Snyk/Sonar + COST SIGNALS        │
│           • token_waste_rate, budget_compliance, model_misuse   │
│  STAGE 5: Risk Scoring → criticality × tools × trust × cost     │
│  STAGE 6: Decision + Archaeology → Verdict + plain-English      │
│                                                                 │
│  DECISION OUTCOMES:                                             │
│  ✓ ALLOW          → trust ≥ 0.80, cost within budget            │
│  ⚠ ALLOW + WARN   → trust 0.60-0.79, minor cost overage         │
│  ◎ REQUIRES_APPROVAL → trust < 0.60 OR budget > 0.90           │
│  ✕ BLOCK          → critical risk OR severe cost violation      │
│                                                                 │
└───────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                │ ONLY ALLOW / ALLOW+WARN PROCEEDS
                ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    ACES EXECUTION LAYER                         │
│                                                                 │
│  • Agent Runtime injects ARIA trust context                     │
│  • MCP Dispatch respects rate limits & tool policies            │
│  • Workflow Engine re-evaluates ARIA on each step               │
│  • ARIA Reporter posts execution record back to Oracle          │
│  • OpenTelemetry trace ID propagates end-to-end                 │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## 🛡️ PART 7: OPERATIONAL RUNBOOK & COMPLIANCE MAPPING
*Aligns with ARIA's security, observability, and 7-year retention constraints.*

### 7.1 Enterprise Controls
| Control | Implementation | Compliance Mapping |
|---------|----------------|-------------------|
| **Data Isolation** | Oracle VPD + `DBMS_RLS` + Application Context per LOB/Org | SOX Change Management, DORA |
| **Encryption** | Oracle TDE + TLS 1.3 in transit + HSM-backed plugin signing | NIST AI RMF, JPMC Internal Audit |
| **Audit Trail** | Oracle Unified Auditing → SIEM (Splunk/QRadar) + `decision_archaeology` JSON | 7-year immutable retention |
| **PII Safety** | Regex/NLP scrubbing before ingestion; never stored in raw form | GDPR Right-to-Erasure, PCI-DSS |
| **Failsafe** | Circuit breaker → REQUIRES_APPROVAL on ARIA unavailability | Production Safety P0 |

### 7.2 OpenTelemetry Trace Propagation
```yaml
# otel-collector-config.yaml
processors:
  batch:
  attributes:
    actions:
      - key: aria.trace_id
        from_context: trace_id
      - key: aria.agent_id
        from_attribute: agent.id
      - key: aria.cost_delta
        from_attribute: finops.savings_delta
exporters:
  otlp/aria:
    endpoint: "aria-observability.internal:4317"

  pipelines:
    traces:
      processors: [batch, attributes]
      exporters: [otlp/aria, otlp/aces]
```

# 4. 7-Year Archive Execution (Scheduled)
BEGIN
  FOR p IN (SELECT partition_name FROM user_tab_partitions 
            WHERE table_name='ARIA_COST_TRANSACTION' AND partition_position <= 84) LOOP
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'ALTER TABLE aria_cost_transaction EXCHANGE PARTITION ' || p.partition_name || 
      ' WITH TABLE aria_cost_archive INCLUDING INDEXES WITHOUT VALIDATION';
    DBMS_CLOUD.OBJECT.PUT(uri => 'os://aria-archive/' || p.partition_name || '.parquet', 
                          credential_name => 'ARCH_CREDS');
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'ALTER TABLE aria_cost_transaction DROP PARTITION ' || p.partition_name;
  END LOOP;
END;

## 🔐 FIRST: Oracle VPD Access Clarification (Your Question)

### Can Developers Deploy VPD Policies?

**Short Answer:** **No — not directly in production Oracle environments.** VPD (Virtual Private Database / Row-Level Security) requires elevated DBA privileges that are typically restricted in enterprise settings like JPMorgan Chase.

### VPD Privilege Requirements
```sql
-- VPD policy creation requires:
GRANT EXECUTE ON DBMS_RLS TO <schema_owner>;  -- Usually DBA-only
GRANT CREATE PROCEDURE TO <schema_owner>;       -- For policy functions
GRANT ALTER ANY TABLE TO <schema_owner>;        -- To enable RLS on tables
```

### ✅ Practical Solutions for Pilot

| Option | Description | Pilot Viability | Production Path |
|--------|-------------|----------------|-----------------|
| **A. DBA Partnership Model** | DBA team deploys VPD policies from your DDL scripts via ServiceNow change request | ✅ **Recommended for Pilot** | Same process, automated via Terraform + Ansible |
| **B. Application-Layer Isolation** | Enforce `lob_code`/`org_unit` filters in Java/Spring repository layer + integration tests | ✅ Fallback if VPD delayed | Hybrid: App-layer + VPD once approved |
| **C. Oracle Database Vault** | Use Oracle DV realms for isolation (if licensed) | ⚠️ Requires security review | Enterprise standard post-pilot |
| **D. Schema-per-LOB** | Separate Oracle schemas per LOB with distinct credentials | ✅ Quick start, higher ops cost | Consolidate to VPD later |

### 🎯 Recommended Pilot Approach: **Option A + B Hybrid**
1. **Submit VPD deployment request** via JPMC Change Management (ServiceNow) with pre-approved DDL scripts
2. **Implement application-layer filters** as immediate fallback (code already written)
3. **Validate both paths** in pilot: if VPD is approved, enable it; if not, app-layer filters suffice for pilot scope
4. **Document compliance mapping** showing app-layer filters meet SOX/DORA for pilot phase

### Day 3-4: Schema Deployment (With/Without VPD)
```sql
-- finops_schema_ddl.sql (Pilot-Optimized)
-- Deploy tables with conditional VPD enablement

-- 1. Core tables (always deployed)
CREATE TABLE finops_cost_transaction_pilot (
    transaction_id    NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id        VARCHAR2(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp   TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    user_id           VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    lob_code          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,      -- Critical for isolation
    org_unit          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens      INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens     INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_cost        NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    optimization_flags JSON,
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(PARTITION p_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2025-01-01 00:00:00'));

-- 2. Conditional VPD enablement (DBA executes if approved)
-- [[VPD_ENABLED]] marker for automated script processing
BEGIN
  -- Only execute if VPD privileges granted
  IF USER = 'DBA_ADMIN' THEN
    DBMS_RLS.ADD_POLICY(
      object_schema    => 'FINOPS_PILOT',
      object_name      => 'finops_cost_transaction_pilot',
      policy_name      => 'finops_lob_isolation',
      function_schema  => 'FINOPS_PILOT',
      policy_function  => 'fn_lob_predicate',
      statement_types  => 'SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE',
      update_check     => TRUE,
      enable           => TRUE
    );
  END IF;
END;
/

-- 3. Application-layer fallback filter (always active)
-- Implemented in Spring Data repository (see Week 2)
```

### Day 6-7: Interceptor Validation & Success Criteria
```typescript
// pilot-validation/interceptor-test.ts
import { CostInterceptor } from '../src/interceptor';

async function validateInterceptor() {
  const interceptor = new CostInterceptor(pilotConfig);
  
  // Test 1: Request capture rate
  const captured = await interceptor.captureTestRequests(100);
  console.assert(captured >= 95, `Capture rate ${captured}% < 95% threshold`);
  
  // Test 2: Interceptor overhead
  const overhead = await interceptor.measureOverhead(50);
  console.assert(overhead.p95 <= 50, `Overhead ${overhead.p95}ms > 50ms SLO`);
  
  // Test 3: Async ingestion reliability
  const delivered = await interceptor.verifyAsyncDelivery(20);
  console.assert(delivered >= 19, `Delivery rate ${delivered}/20 < 95%`);
  
  return { captured, overhead, delivered };
}
```

## 📅 WEEK 3: Cost Calculator + Trust-Cost Feedback

### Day 1-3: Cost Engine Calibration
```java
// pilot-calibration/CostEngineCalibrator.java
@Service
public class PilotCostCalibrator {
    
    @PostConstruct
    public void calibratePilot() {
        // 1. Load pilot pricing catalog (discounted pilot rates)
        pricingRepo.loadPilotCatalog("PILOT_2026_Q2");
        
        // 2. Validate cost calculation accuracy
        List<CostValidationCase> testCases = loadPilotTestCases();
        double accuracy = testCases.stream()
            .mapToDouble(tc -> {
                BigDecimal calculated = costService.calculate(tc.getRequest());
                return 1.0 - Math.abs(calculated.subtract(tc.getExpected()).doubleValue()) / tc.getExpected().doubleValue();
            })
            .average().orElse(0.0);
        
        // 3. Assert pilot threshold
        if (accuracy < 0.999) { // 99.9% accuracy required
            throw new CalibrationException("Cost accuracy " + accuracy + " < 99.9% threshold");
        }
        
        // 4. Log calibration result for audit
        auditLog.log("PILOT_CALIBRATION", Map.of("accuracy", accuracy, "timestamp", Instant.now()));
    }
}
```

### Day 4-5: Trust-Cost Feedback Loop Integration

-- Pilot trust-cost mapping table (simplified for pilot)
CREATE TABLE pilot_trust_cost_mapping (
    mapping_id      NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    savings_percent NUMBER(5,2) NOT NULL,      -- e.g., 35.5 = 35.5% savings
    trust_delta     NUMBER(3,2) NOT NULL,      -- e.g., +0.02
    optimization_type VARCHAR2(50),            -- 'model_downgrade', 'compression', etc.
    effective_from  DATE DEFAULT TRUNC(SYSDATE),
    CONSTRAINT chk_pilot_delta CHECK (trust_delta BETWEEN -0.10 AND 0.05)
);

-- Pilot-specific mappings (conservative for safety)
INSERT INTO pilot_trust_cost_mapping (savings_percent, trust_delta, optimization_type) VALUES
(30.0, 0.02, 'model_downgrade'),
(25.0, 0.01, 'prompt_compression'),
(40.0, 0.03, 'semantic_caching'),
(-10.0, -0.03, 'budget_overrun'); -- Penalty for overspending
```

  --transaction-id=$LAST_TXN_ID \

  exit 0
else
  echo "❌ WEEK 3 FAILED: Delta accuracy=$DELTA_ACCURACY, Trust update=$TRUST_UPDATE"
  exit 1
fi

### Day 4-5: ACES Trace Integration
```java
// pilot-aces/AriaAcesTracer.java
@Component
public class PilotAcesTracer {
    
    private final OpenTelemetry otel;
    private final OracleJdbcTemplate oracle;
    
    @Async
    public void propagateTrace(CostTransactionRecord record, String acesExecutionId) {
        // 1. Extract ARIA trace context
        SpanContext ariaContext = otel.getPropagators().getTextMapPropagator()
            .extract(Context.current(), record, (r, key) -> r.getHeaders().get(key));
        
        // 2. Inject into ACES execution record
        oracle.update(
            "INSERT INTO aces_execution_trace_pilot (execution_id, aria_trace_id, cost_delta, trust_score_at_execution) " +
            "VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)",
            acesExecutionId,
            record.getTransactionId(),
            record.getSavingsDelta(),
            record.getTrustScore()
        );
        
        // 3. Emit combined metric for observability
        otel.getMeter("aria-finops")
            .counter("aces.aria.cost_delta")
            .add(record.getSavingsDelta().doubleValue(), 
                 Attributes.builder()
                     .put("agent.id", record.getAgentId())
                     .put("lob.code", record.getLobCode())
                     .put("trace.propagated", true)
                     .build());
    }
}
```

## 🔄 Fallback Architecture: If VPD Deployment Is Delayed

### Application-Layer Isolation Implementation
```java
// repository/FinopsTransactionRepository.java
@Repository
public interface FinopsTransactionRepository extends JpaRepository<CostTransaction, Long> {
    
    // CRITICAL: Every query MUST include lob_code filter
    @Query("SELECT t FROM CostTransaction t WHERE t.lobCode = :lobCode AND t.eventTimestamp BETWEEN :start AND :end")
    List<CostTransaction> findByLobAndDateRange(@Param("lobCode") String lobCode, 
                                               @Param("start") Timestamp start, 
                                               @Param("end") Timestamp end);
    
    // Aggregation queries also enforce isolation
    @Query("SELECT t.lobCode, SUM(t.totalCost) FROM CostTransaction t " +
           "WHERE t.lobCode = :lobCode GROUP BY t.lobCode")
    List<Object[]> aggregateCostByLob(@Param("lobCode") String lobCode);
}

// Service layer enforces context
@Service
public class FinopsService {
    public List<CostTransaction> getTransactions(String requestedLob) {
        // Get caller's authorized LOB from JWT
        String callerLob = SecurityContextHolder.getContext().getAuthorizedLob();
        
        // CRITICAL: Reject if caller requests data outside their LOB
        if (!callerLob.equals(requestedLob)) {
            auditLog.logSecurityEvent("LOB_ISOLATION_VIOLATION", callerLob, requestedLob);
            throw new AccessDeniedException("Cross-LOB access denied");
        }
        
        return repository.findByLobAndDateRange(callerLob, start, end);
    }
}
```

### Compliance Mapping for App-Layer Isolation (Pilot Phase)
| Control Requirement | VPD Implementation | App-Layer Fallback | Pilot Acceptability |
|--------------------|-------------------|------------------|-------------------|
| Data isolation | Oracle VPD policy at DB level | Spring Security + repository filters + integration tests | ✅ Acceptable for pilot with enhanced testing |
| Audit trail | Oracle Unified Auditing | Application audit log + database change log | ✅ Acceptable if logs shipped to SIEM |
| SOX Change Management | DBA change ticket for VPD | Code review + CI/CD gate for isolation logic | ✅ Acceptable with peer review evidence |
| Penetration testing | DB-level access tests | API-level isolation tests + red team exercise | ✅ Required before pilot go-live |

### Day 2-3: Simplified Schema DDL (No VPD, No DBA)
```sql
-- ============================================
-- ARIA FINOPS SCHEMA — DEVELOPER ACCESS ONLY
-- No DBA privileges required
-- ============================================

-- 1. AGENT DNA REGISTRY (Trust Model)
CREATE TABLE aria_agent_dna (
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    agent_type        VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    trust_score       NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.30 CHECK (trust_score BETWEEN 0.0 AND 1.0),
    total_prs         INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    blocked_prs       INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    prod_incidents    INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    trend             VARCHAR2(20) DEFAULT 'NEW',
    recent_activity   JSON,
    specializations   JSON,
    last_incident     VARCHAR2(500),
    cost_efficiency   NUMBER(5,2) DEFAULT 1.00,
    token_waste_rate  NUMBER(5,2) DEFAULT 0.0,
    budget_compliance NUMBER(5,2) DEFAULT 1.00,
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 2. COST TRANSACTIONS (No partitioning if not allowed)
CREATE TABLE aria_cost_transaction (
    transaction_id    NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id        VARCHAR2(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp   TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL REFERENCES aria_agent_dna(agent_id),
    user_id           VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    lob_code          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,      -- Critical for app-layer isolation
    org_unit          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    ide_type          VARCHAR2(50),
    provider          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name        VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens      INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens     INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens     INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    input_cost        NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost       NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    total_cost        GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost) VIRTUAL,
    optimization_flags JSON,
    decision_id       VARCHAR2(100),
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Try partitioning (will fail gracefully if not permitted)
BEGIN
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'ALTER TABLE aria_cost_transaction MODIFY PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp) ' ||
        'INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, ''MONTH'')) ' ||
        '(PARTITION p_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP ''2025-01-01 00:00:00''))';
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- Partitioning not allowed - continue without it
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('Partitioning not available. Using unpartitioned table.');
END;
/

-- 3. SAVINGS LEDGER (Baseline vs Optimized)
CREATE TABLE aria_savings_ledger (
    event_id          NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id        VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp   TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    baseline_cost     NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    optimized_cost    NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    savings_delta     NUMBER(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (baseline_cost - optimized_cost) VIRTUAL,
    savings_percent   NUMBER(5,2),
    applied_optimizations JSON,
    routed_model      VARCHAR2(100),
    cache_hit         CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N',
    trust_delta_applied NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.0,
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 4. SKILL REGISTRY
CREATE TABLE aria_skill_registry (
    skill_id          VARCHAR2(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    version           VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
    manifest          JSON NOT NULL,
    execution_contract JSON NOT NULL,
    signing_key       VARCHAR2(128),
    is_active         CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y',
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 5. INDEXES (All allowed with developer access)
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_user_ts ON aria_cost_transaction(user_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_lob_ts ON aria_cost_transaction(lob_code, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_agent_ts ON aria_cost_transaction(agent_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_tx_model_ts ON aria_cost_transaction(provider, model_name, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_savings_agent_ts ON aria_savings_ledger(agent_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_agent_dna_trend ON aria_agent_dna(trend, trust_score);

-- 6. VIEWS FOR ISOLATION (Application-layer enforcement helper)
CREATE VIEW aria_cost_transaction_vw AS
SELECT * FROM aria_cost_transaction
WHERE lob_code = SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV', 'CLIENT_IDENTIFIER')
   OR lob_code IN (
       SELECT DISTINCT lob_code FROM user_lob_access 
       WHERE user_id = SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV', 'SESSION_USER')
   );
-- Note: This view requires application to set CLIENT_IDENTIFIER context

-- 7. SEQUENCES (If GENERATED AS IDENTITY fails)
CREATE SEQUENCE seq_agent_dna START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1;
CREATE SEQUENCE seq_cost_txn START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1;
CREATE SEQUENCE seq_savings_ledger START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1;
```

### Day 4: Application-Layer Isolation Implementation
```java
// ============================================
// SPRING SECURITY + REPOSITORY LAYER
// Enforces LOB isolation WITHOUT VPD
// ============================================

// 1. Custom Annotation for LOB Isolation
@Target(ElementType.METHOD)
@Retention(RetentionPolicy.RUNTIME)
@PreAuthorize("@lobSecurity.hasAccess(#lobCode)")
public @interface RequireLobAccess {
}

// 2. LOB Security Service
@Service("lobSecurity")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class LobSecurityService {
    private final JwtDecoder jwtDecoder;
    
    public boolean hasAccess(String requestedLobCode) {
        // Get user's authorized LOBs from JWT
        String token = SecurityContextHolder.getContext().getAuthentication().getCredentials().toString();
        Jwt jwt = jwtDecoder.decode(token);
        List<String> userLobs = jwt.getClaimAsStringList("authorized_lobs");
        
        boolean hasAccess = userLobs.contains(requestedLobCode);
        
        if (!hasAccess) {
            auditLog.logSecurityEvent(
                "LOB_ACCESS_DENIED",
                jwt.getSubject(),
                requestedLobCode,
                userLobs
            );
        }
        
        return hasAccess;
    }
}

// 3. Repository with Mandatory LOB Filter
@Repository
public interface CostTransactionRepository extends JpaRepository<CostTransaction, Long> {
    
    // EVERY query MUST include lobCode parameter
    @Query("SELECT t FROM CostTransaction t " +
           "WHERE t.lobCode = :lobCode " +
           "AND t.eventTimestamp BETWEEN :start AND :end " +
           "ORDER BY t.eventTimestamp DESC")
    @RequireLobAccess
    List<CostTransaction> findByLobAndDateRange(
        @Param("lobCode") String lobCode,
        @Param("start") Timestamp start,
        @Param("end") Timestamp end
    );
    
    // Aggregation queries also enforce isolation
    @Query("SELECT t.modelName, SUM(t.totalCost), COUNT(t) " +
           "FROM CostTransaction t " +
           "WHERE t.lobCode = :lobCode " +
           "GROUP BY t.modelName")
    @RequireLobAccess
    List<Object[]> aggregateCostByModel(@Param("lobCode") String lobCode);
    
    // CRITICAL: No query without lobCode filter allowed
}

// 4. Service Layer Validation
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class FinOpsService {
    private final CostTransactionRepository repository;
    private final JwtDecoder jwtDecoder;
    
    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
    public List<CostTransaction> getTransactions(String requestedLob, DateRange range) {
        // Double-check: get caller's authorized LOB from JWT
        String callerLob = getCallerAuthorizedLob();
        
        // ENFORCE: Reject if caller requests data outside their LOB
        if (!callerLob.equals(requestedLob)) {
            throw new AccessDeniedException(
                String.format("Cross-LOB access denied: user authorized for %s, requested %s", 
                    callerLob, requestedLob)
            );
        }
        
        return repository.findByLobAndDateRange(callerLob, range.getStart(), range.getEnd());
    }
    
    private String getCallerAuthorizedLob() {
        Authentication auth = SecurityContextHolder.getContext().getAuthentication();
        Jwt jwt = jwtDecoder.decode(auth.getCredentials().toString());
        List<String> lobs = jwt.getClaimAsStringList("authorized_lobs");
        return lobs.isEmpty() ? null : lobs.get(0); // Primary LOB
    }
}
```

### Day 5: Validation & Testing (No VPD)
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# validate_week1_no_vpd.sh

echo "🔍 Validating Oracle Schema (Developer Access)..."

# 1. Check tables created
TABLES=$(sqlplus -s $CONN <<EOF
SELECT COUNT(*) FROM user_tables WHERE table_name IN 
('ARIA_AGENT_DNA', 'ARIA_COST_TRANSACTION', 'ARIA_SAVINGS_LEDGER', 'ARIA_SKILL_REGISTRY');
EXIT;
EOF
)

if [ "$TABLES" -ne 4 ]; then
    echo "❌ FAILED: Expected 4 tables, found $TABLES"
    exit 1
fi

# 2. Check indexes
INDEXES=$(sqlplus -s $CONN <<EOF
SELECT COUNT(*) FROM user_indexes WHERE table_name = 'ARIA_COST_TRANSACTION';
EXIT;
EOF
)

echo "✅ Found $INDEXES indexes on cost_transaction table"

# 3. Test application-layer isolation
echo "🔐 Testing application-layer LOB isolation..."
java -cp isolation-test.jar com.jpmc.aria.LobIsolationTest \
  --user-lob=LOB_A \
  --attempt-access-to=LOB_B \
  --expected-result=ACCESS_DENIED

# 4. Verify no cross-LOB leakage
LEAKAGE_TEST=$(java -cp isolation-test.jar com.jpmc.aria.CrossLobLeakageTest \
  --test-cases=100 \
  --expected-leaks=0)

if [ "$LEAKAGE_TEST" != "0" ]; then
    echo "❌ FAILED: Cross-LOB leakage detected: $LEAKAGE_TEST"
    exit 1
fi

# 5. Test JWT-based LOB enforcement
echo "🎫 Testing JWT LOB claims enforcement..."
java -cp isolation-test.jar com.jpmc.aria.JwtLobEnforcementTest \
  --jwt-lob=LOB_A \
  --request-lob=LOB_A \
  --expected-result=ALLOW

echo "🎉 WEEK 1 SUCCESS: Schema deployed, app-layer isolation validated"
exit 0
```

### Quarterly Data Archival (No DBMS_CLOUD)
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# archive_quarterly.sh - Works with developer access

QUARTER=$(date +%YQ%q)
EXPORT_FILE="aria_finops_${QUARTER}.dmp"

# Use Data Pump Export (requires EXPDP privilege)
expdp $CONN \
  tables=aria_cost_transaction,aria_savings_ledger \
  query="WHERE event_timestamp < ADD_MONTHS(SYSDATE, -6)" \
  directory=DATA_PUMP_DIR \
  dumpfile=$EXPORT_FILE \
  logfile=archive_${QUARTER}.log

# If EXPDP not available, use simple SQL*Plus export
sqlplus -s $CONN <<EOF
SET HEADING OFF
SET FEEDBACK OFF
SPOOL aria_cost_export_${QUARTER}.csv
SELECT * FROM aria_cost_transaction 
WHERE event_timestamp < ADD_MONTHS(SYSDATE, -6);
SPOOL OFF
EOF

# Compress and move to archive storage
gzip aria_cost_export_${QUARTER}.csv
mv aria_cost_export_${QUARTER}.csv.gz /archive/finops/
```

## 🎯 Cost Intelligence Layer: Runtime Data Collection

### What We Capture (Every Agent Execution)

| Metric | Source | Granularity | Purpose |
|--------|--------|-------------|---------|
| **Token Usage** | LLM API response headers | Per-call: `prompt_tokens`, `completion_tokens`, `cached_tokens` | Cost calculation, efficiency scoring |
| **Model Identifier** | Request payload + response metadata | `provider/model/version` (e.g., `anthropic/claude-3-sonnet/3.5`) | Model performance comparison, routing optimization |
| **Latency & Retries** | Client-side timing + retry headers | `first_token_ms`, `total_ms`, `retry_count`, `error_code` | SLO monitoring, reliability scoring |
| **Tool Invocation** | MCP/Tool execution logs | `tool_name`, `input_size`, `output_size`, `duration_ms` | Workflow efficiency, redundant call detection |
| **Cost Per Unit** | Pricing catalog lookup | `cost_per_request`, `cost_per_workflow`, `cost_per_agent` | Budget tracking, chargeback, ROI analysis |
| **Context Metadata** | Interceptor injection | `user_id`, `agent_id`, `lob_code`, `use_case`, `environment` | Multi-dimensional attribution |

### Collection Mechanism: Interceptor Architecture

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    INTERCEPTION POINTS                      │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                             │
│  1. SDK-Level Interceptor (Agent Runtime)                   │
│     • Wraps LLM client calls (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.)      │
│     • Captures request/response + timing                    │
│     • Non-blocking async send to ARIA gateway               │
│                                                             │
│  2. Gateway-Level Interceptor (MCP / API Gateway)           │
│     • Centralized collection for all agent traffic          │
│     • Enriches with org context (LOB, cost center)          │
│     • Applies sampling rules for high-volume agents         │
│                                                             │
│  3. IDE Plugin Interceptor (Developer Tooling)              │
│     • VS Code / IntelliJ plugin captures Copilot usage      │
│     • Attributes to developer + project + LOB               │
│     • Shows real-time cost delta in status bar              │
│                                                             │
│  4. CI/CD Webhook Interceptor (Pipeline Events)             │
│     • Captures AI-generated PRs, test runs, deployments     │
│     • Correlates pipeline cost to agent + commit            │
│                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                            │
                            ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    CENTRAL AGGREGATION                      │
│                                                             │
│  • Async ingestion via Kafka/Pulsar                         │
│  • Schema validation against CostEvent contract             │
│  • Deduplication by request_id + timestamp window           │
│  • Batch write to Oracle cost ledger (aria_cost_transaction)│
│                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

## 🧠 Cost Intelligence: Analysis & Attribution

### 1. Cost Attribution Engine

```sql
-- Multi-dimensional cost aggregation (Oracle 23c)
SELECT 
    lob_code,
    agent_id,
    use_case,
    DATE_TRUNC('day', event_timestamp) AS day,
    SUM(total_cost) AS total_spend,
    SUM(input_tokens + output_tokens) AS total_tokens,
    AVG(total_cost / NULLIF(input_tokens + output_tokens, 0)) AS avg_cost_per_token,
    COUNT(DISTINCT request_id) AS request_count
FROM aria_cost_transaction
WHERE event_timestamp BETWEEN :start AND :end
  AND lob_code = :lob_code  -- VPD or app-layer filter
GROUP BY lob_code, agent_id, use_case, DATE_TRUNC('day', event_timestamp)
ORDER BY total_spend DESC;
```

**Attribution Dimensions Supported:**
| Dimension | Example Use Case |
|-----------|-----------------|
| `per-agent` | "Copilot-agent-7 spent $234 this week" |
| `per-use-case` | "Code generation: $1.2K, Documentation: $340, Testing: $890" |
| `per-team/LOB` | "Digital Banking LOB: $12.4K monthly AI spend" |
| `per-product` | "Payment Service: $3.2K in AI-assisted development" |
| `per-environment` | "Prod deployments: $8.1K, Dev: $1.2K" |
| `per-developer` | "dev@jpmc.com: $156 in Copilot usage" |

---

### 2. Pattern Detection Engine

```python
# Pattern detection rules (configurable YAML)
pattern_rules:
  - id: redundant_tool_calls
    description: "Same tool called >3x with identical inputs in 5min window"
    condition: |
      tool_name == prev.tool_name AND 
      input_hash == prev.input_hash AND 
      count_in_window(5min) >= 3
    action: alert + suggest_caching
    severity: medium

  - id: high_token_payload
    description: "Prompt exceeds 80% of model context window"
    condition: input_tokens / model_max_context > 0.80
    action: suggest_compression + flag_for_review
    severity: high

  - id: agent_loop_detected
    description: "Agent re-requests same task >2x without progress"
    condition: |
      task_hash == prev.task_hash AND 
      output_similarity(prev.output, curr.output) < 0.3 AND 
      retry_count >= 2
    action: break_loop + escalate_to_human
    severity: critical

  - id: model_misuse
    description: "Expensive model used for simple classification task"
    condition: |
      model_cost_tier == 'premium' AND 
      task_complexity == 'simple' AND 
      output_length < 200
    action: suggest_downgrade + log_waste
    severity: low
```

**Detected Patterns → Automated Actions:**
| Pattern | Detection Signal | Automated Response |
|---------|-----------------|-------------------|
| 🔁 Redundant calls | Same tool + input hash repeated | Suggest semantic cache key |
| 📦 High token payload | `input_tokens / max_context > 0.80` | Trigger prompt compression plugin |
| 🔄 Agent loop | Task hash repeated + low output similarity | Break loop + human escalation |
| 💸 Model misuse | Premium model + simple task + short output | Suggest cheaper model routing |
| 📉 Cost spike | 3σ deviation from 7-day baseline | Alert + budget throttle |

---

### 3. Cost Anomaly Detection

```sql
-- Oracle 23c ML: Anomaly detection on cost time-series
BEGIN
    DBMS_DATA_MINING.CREATE_MODEL(
        model_name          => 'COST_ANOMALY_DETECTOR',
        mining_function     => DBMS_DATA_MINING.ANOMALY_DETECTION,
        data_table_name     => 'aria_daily_cost_agg',
        case_id_column_name => 'agg_date',
        target_column_name  => 'total_cost',
        settings_table_name => 'anomaly_settings'
    );
END;
/

-- Query for anomalies in last 24h
SELECT agg_date, total_cost, 
       PREDICTION_PROBABILITY(COST_ANOMALY_DETECTOR USING *) AS anomaly_score
FROM aria_daily_cost_agg
WHERE agg_date >= SYSDATE - 1
  AND PREDICTION_PROBABILITY(COST_ANOMALY_DETECTOR USING *) < 0.05  -- Top 5% anomalies
ORDER BY anomaly_score ASC;
```

**Anomaly Types Detected:**
| Type | Trigger | Response |
|------|---------|----------|
| 🚨 Sudden spike | Cost > 3σ above 7-day rolling mean | Alert + auto-throttle high-cost agents |
| 📉 Unusual drop | Cost < 0.5σ (possible data loss) | Validate ingestion pipeline |
| 🔄 Pattern shift | Weekday/weekend ratio deviates > 40% | Investigate usage change |
| 🎯 Agent outlier | Single agent > 20% of LOB budget | Review agent configuration |

---

### 4. Predictive Cost Estimation

```java
// Cost forecasting service (Spring Boot + Oracle OML)
@Service
public class PredictiveCostService {
    
    public CostForecast forecastWorkflowCost(
        WorkflowDefinition workflow,
        HistoricalContext context
    ) {
        // 1. Extract workflow features
        WorkflowFeatures features = extractFeatures(workflow);
        
        // 2. Query historical similar workflows
        List<HistoricalExecution> similar = repository.findSimilar(
            features, 
            context.getLookbackDays()
        );
        
        // 3. Apply Oracle ML forecasting model
        ForecastResult forecast = oracleML.predict(
            "WORKFLOW_COST_FORECAST",
            features.toFeatureVector(),
            similar.stream().map(HistoricalExecution::toTrainingRow).toList()
        );
        
        // 4. Return confidence-bounded estimate
        return CostForecast.builder()
            .predictedCost(forecast.getMean())
            .confidenceInterval(
                forecast.getLowerBound(0.95),
                forecast.getUpperBound(0.95)
            )
            .primaryDrivers(forecast.getFeatureImportance().topN(3))
            .recommendations(generateRecommendations(forecast))
            .build();
    }
    
    private List<Recommendation> generateRecommendations(ForecastResult forecast) {
        List<Recommendation> recs = new ArrayList<>();
        
        if (forecast.getFeatureImportance().get("model_selection") > 0.4) {
            recs.add(Recommendation.suggestModelRouting(
                "Consider downgrading 30% of calls to Haiku for 40% savings"
            ));
        }
        if (forecast.getFeatureImportance().get("token_efficiency") > 0.3) {
            recs.add(Recommendation.suggestPromptCompression(
                "Enable compression to reduce avg tokens by 25%"
            ));
        }
        
        return recs;
    }
}
```

**Forecasting Outputs:**
| Output | Format | Use Case |
|--------|--------|----------|
| `predicted_cost` | `$XX.XX ± $Y.YY (95% CI)` | Budget planning, approval gates |
| `primary_drivers` | `["model_selection", "token_volume", "retry_rate"]` | Optimization prioritization |
| `recommendations` | Actionable suggestions with estimated savings | Automated optimization triggers |
| `risk_score` | `0.0–1.0` probability of budget overrun | Pre-execution gating |

## 🔗 Integration with ARIA Trust Model

The Cost Intelligence Layer **feeds directly into the Trust Model Schema**:

```
Cost Metrics → Trust Score Adjustments
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• cost_efficiency_ratio (value delivered / $ spent) 
    → +0.02 trust if > 1.2x baseline
    
• token_waste_rate (redundant/context bloat %) 
    → −0.03 trust if > 40% sustained
    
• budget_compliance (actual / allocated) 
    → −0.05 trust per 10% overage
    
• cache_hit_rate 
    → +0.01 trust if > 35%
    
• model_appropriateness (right model for task) 
    → +0.01 trust for optimal routing
```

This creates a **closed-loop system**: cost efficiency earns trust → higher trust grants autonomy → autonomy enables more executions → cost intelligence continues optimizing.

2.1 New Data Captured (Beyond Token Count)
Metric	Description	How it impacts Trust
Cost Efficiency Score	(Expected tokens / Actual tokens) * (Cheapest model capable / Model used).	High efficiency = trust_score boost.
Cache Hit Ratio	% of tool results/LLM responses served from Redis instead of recomputed.	Low cache hit ratio = penalty (wasteful).
Loop Depth Cost	Cost of each ReAct loop iteration (Planner -> Retriever -> Synthesizer).	Loop > 2 iterations with no improvement = BLOCK for that turn.
Anomaly Score	Statistical deviation from historical cost for that agent/task.	High anomaly = trigger REQUIRES_APPROVAL.
2.2 Integrated Decision Logic (The Real-Time Loop)
Modify Stage 5 (Risk Scoring) in the ARIA Pipeline to this:

python
# Pseudo-code inside ARIA's Risk Scoring Engine

final_risk_score = (
    (security_risk * 0.40) +      # Existing: Snyk, Sonar, PII
    (safety_risk * 0.35) +        # Existing: Harmful intent, escalation
    (COST_RISK * 0.25)            # <-- NEW: Make it 25% of the decision
)

# How COST_RISK is calculated:
cost_risk = 0.0
if predicted_cost > budget_allocated_for_this_task:
    cost_risk += 0.5
if cost_efficiency_score < 0.6:  # Agent is being wasteful
    cost_risk += 0.3
if cost_anomaly_score > 3_sigma:
    cost_risk += 0.8  # This is suspicious, likely a bug or loop

# Final ARIA Verdict based on new composite score:
if cost_risk > 0.7:
    return "BLOCK"  # "Agent exceeding cost budget or anomalous"
elif cost_risk > 0.4:
    return "REQUIRES_APPROVAL"  # "This will cost $1.50, confirm?"
2.3 The "Cost-Aware Agent" Pattern (Model Selection)
This is the most powerful upgrade. Modify the ACES Orchestrator to use a "Cost-Aware Router":

Aria (User Assistant): Default to Haiku (cheap). Only route to Sonnet if Haiku's confidence score is < 0.7.

ACES (Background Agent): For non-interactive tasks (e.g., "Scan all repos for security issues"), use Haiku for filtering, only invoke Opus for the final synthesis.

ALTER TABLE aria_agent_dna ADD (
    cost_efficiency_score NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.80 CHECK (cost_efficiency_score BETWEEN 0.0 AND 1.0),
    total_cost_usd        NUMBER(14,4) DEFAULT 0.0,
    expensive_calls_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_cost_anomaly_at  TIMESTAMP,
    monthly_budget_usd    NUMBER(12,2) DEFAULT 500.00,
    budget_utilization    NUMBER(5,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE WHEN monthly_budget_usd > 0 
             THEN (total_cost_usd / monthly_budget_usd) * 100 
             ELSE 0 END
    ) VIRTUAL
);

-- Index for fast cost-anomaly queries
CREATE INDEX idx_agent_cost_anomaly ON aria_agent_dna(last_cost_anomaly_at DESC, trust_score);

## ⚡ 2. ARIA Stage 5 Integration: Cost Risk Engine
*Replaces static cost tracking with real-time risk scoring. Executes in <8ms pre-LLM. Fully async post-LLM trust updates preserve p95 ≤ 500ms latency SLO.*

```java
// ============================================
// ARIA STAGE 5: COST RISK ADVISOR (Spring AI 1.0)
// Runs BEFORE LLM call. Non-blocking. <8ms overhead.
// ============================================
@Component
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class CostRiskAdvisor implements PreChatClientAdvisor {
    
    private final AgentDnaRepository dnaRepo;
    private final PricingCatalog pricing;
    private final RedisTemplate<String, Object> redis;
    private static final double COST_RISK_WEIGHT = 0.25;

    @Override
    public AdvisedRequest advise(AdvisedRequest request) {
        String agentId = request.getMetadata().get("agent_id");
        String model = request.getChatOptions().getModel();
        
        // 1. Fast pre-check: Budget & Anomaly (Cached in Redis)
        AgentCostContext ctx = redis.opsForValue().get("cost:ctx:" + agentId);
        if (ctx == null) ctx = dnaRepo.loadCostContext(agentId);
        
        double costRisk = 0.0;
        
        // Budget threshold check
        if (ctx.budgetUtilization > 95.0) costRisk += 0.50;
        
        // Model misuse check (e.g., Opus for simple FAQ)
        if (isModelMismatch(model, request.getPrompt())) costRisk += 0.30;
        
        // Anomaly detection (z-score pre-computed nightly)
        if (ctx.anomalyZScore > 3.0) costRisk += 0.80;
        
        // Inject cost risk into request metadata for Stage 5
        request.getMetadata().put("cost_risk", costRisk);
        request.getMetadata().put("cost_risk_verdict", calculateVerdict(costRisk));
        
        return request;
    }

    private String calculateVerdict(double costRisk) {
        if (costRisk > 0.70) return "BLOCK";
        if (costRisk > 0.40) return "REQUIRES_APPROVAL";
        if (costRisk > 0.20) return "ALLOW_WITH_WARN";
        return "ALLOW";
    }
    
    // Async post-LLM trust update (runs AFTER streaming completes)
    @Async
    public void postProcess(String agentId, CostMetrics metrics) {
        double efficiency = calculateEfficiency(metrics);
        dnaRepo.updateCostMetrics(agentId, metrics, efficiency);
        
        // Trust penalty logic
        if (efficiency < 0.50) dnaRepo.applyTrustPenalty(agentId, -0.02);
        if (metrics.expensiveCallsInWindow > 5) dnaRepo.applyTrustPenalty(agentId, -0.05);
    }
}
```

**Answer**: ML Platform (25.3% of costs, best cost-per-task)
- Cost per call: $0.032 (best in org)
- Cache hit rate: 42% (best practices in place)

### 6. "How many risky decisions did we block?"
**Answer**: 847 BLOCK decisions in April
- Cost avoided: ~$8.5K
- Estimated incident prevention: ~$50K+ per incident
- Risk reduction: High-impact governance working

### 7. "Can we reduce costs further?"
**Answer**: Yes, 25 optimization opportunities identified
- Use Sonnet instead of Opus for routine tasks
- Implement streaming for large outputs
- Batch similar requests for cache efficiency

### 8. "What's our annual AI spend?"
**Answer**: ~$888K (with current optimizations)

## How It Works (Non-Technical Summary)

### **Cost Tracking**
- Every AI call (Copilot, Claude, etc.) is logged
- Tokens counted automatically
- Cost calculated instantly: (prompt_tokens × price) + (completion_tokens × price)
- Aggregated by LOB, team, model, user

### **Auto-Optimization**
- ARIA identifies optimization opportunities
- Automatically applies cost-saving changes:
  - Switches to cheaper model when appropriate
  - Compresses prompts to reduce token count
  - Caches repeated system prompts
  - Prunes unnecessary context
- Savings tracked and reported

### **Governance**
- ARIA evaluates agent risk (trust score)
- Blocks high-risk, high-cost requests
- Routes medium-risk requests for human review
- Approves low-risk requests automatically
- Cost impact recorded for audit

### **Dashboard**
- Real-time visibility into spend
- Drill-down capability: Org → LOB → Team → User
- Budget tracking per team
- Anomaly alerts (unusual spending)
- Trend analysis (up/down/stable)

## Troubleshooting

### Q: Dashboard shows $0 cost
**A**: Real cost data syncing from Supabase. Give it 5 minutes for first sync.

### Q: Why is one team's cost suddenly high?
**A**: Check Executive Alerts section for anomalies. Likely causes:
- New project or workload
- Inefficient prompt or model choice
- Batch processing spike

### Q: How do I know if optimizations are working?
**A**: Look at "Savings Realized" card and trend over time
- If savings rate stable or increasing: ✅ Optimizations working
- If savings rate declining: ⚠️ Needs investigation

### Q: Can I see individual user costs?
**A**: Yes, drill-down through Cost by Team → click team → user list
- Shows cost per user, calls made, efficiency score

### Q: How often is data updated?
**A**: Real-time, every 5 minutes for KPI snapshots
- Individual calls logged immediately
- Charts update every 5 min
- Daily reports generated at midnight

## 2. How It Works (Technical Architecture)

### **Data Flow: Where Your FinOps Data Lives**

```
IDE (Copilot/Claude)
  ↓ [Cost Capture]
  └─ Prompt tokens: X
  └─ Completion tokens: Y
  └─ Model used: claude-opus
  └─ User: jane.doe@company.com
  └─ Team: ML Platform
  └─ LOB: Digital Banking

Cost Aggregator Edge Function (Deno)
  ↓ [Real-time Calculation]
  └─ Cost = (prompt_tokens / 1M * $0.003) + (completion_tokens / 1M * $0.015)
  └─ Aggregation: By LOB, team, model, user
  └─ Batching: Every 60 seconds

Supabase FinOps Tables
  ├─ cost_ledger
  │  └─ Individual call tracking (millions of records)
  ├─ finops_kpis
  │  └─ Daily snapshots (rollups by LOB, team, user)
  ├─ optimization_impact
  │  └─ $X saved via model downgrade, caching, etc.
  ├─ governance_cost_impact
  │  └─ $Y avoided via BLOCK/REVIEW decisions
  ├─ executive_alerts
  │  └─ Anomalies, budget overruns, optimization opportunities
  └─ team_cost_allocation
     └─ Monthly chargeback to cost centers

Executive FinOps Dashboard (React)
  ├─ Real-time charts (updated every 5 minutes)
  ├─ Drill-down: Org → LOB → Team → User → Individual call
  ├─ Savings tracking: Projected vs realized
  ├─ Budget status: Monthly utilization by team
  └─ Alerts: High-cost anomalies, policy violations
```

### **Oracle 23ai Role (Private Cloud)**

```
Oracle 23ai (Your Private Cloud)
├─ ARIA Governance Data
│  ├─ Agent Registry (Copilot, Claude, internal agents)
│  ├─ Trust Scores (updated per production event)
│  ├─ Decision History (BLOCK/REVIEW/ALLOW with reasoning)
│  └─ Governance Rules (risk thresholds, criticality tiers)
│
├─ Audit Trail (immutable log)
│  ├─ Who did what, when
│  ├─ Cost impact of each decision
│  ├─ Business justification recorded
│  └─ Compliance-ready timestamps
│
└─ ACES Spec History
   ├─ Specs that generated agents
   ├─ Code generated vs spec
   ├─ Deployment status
   └─ Performance vs projections

ADB Wallet (Encryption)
└─ TLS certificates + keys
   └─ Secure connection to Spring Boot services
   └─ Zero-trust encrypted tunnel
```

## 3. ACES: Spec-Driven Development (AI Builds Your Platform)

### **The Vision: Specs → Code → Agents (Fully Automated)**

#### **You Define (Product Spec)**
```yaml
feature: "Fraud Detection Agent"
description: "Real-time transaction analysis for fraud prevention"
inputs: [transaction_id, amount, user_profile, merchant_info]
outputs: [fraud_score 0-100, recommendation: ALLOW|REVIEW|BLOCK]
sla: 
  responseTime: 200ms
  availability: 99.9%
cost_constraint:
  maxPerCall: $0.05
  preferredModels: [claude-sonnet, gpt-4o-mini]
governance:
  trustScoreMin: 0.7
  auditLevel: critical
```

#### **Claude API Generates (Implementation Spec)**
```json
{
  "model": "claude-opus-4.6",
  "fallback": "claude-sonnet-4",
  "tools": ["transaction_api", "fraud_rules_db"],
  "cache_strategy": "prompt_caching",
  "spring_beans": [
    {
      "name": "fraudDetectionAgent",
      "class": "FraudDetectionAgent",
      "cost_tracking": true,
      "governance_check": true
    }
  ],
  "oracle_schema": [
    {
      "table": "fraud_rules",
      "columns": ["rule_id", "threshold_amount", "region_code"]
    }
  ],
  "cost_estimate": "$16K/month at projected volume"
}
```

#### **Spring Boot Generates (Deployment-Ready Code)**
```java
@Service
public class FraudDetectionAgent {
  
  public String detectFraud(String transaction) {
    long start = System.currentTimeMillis();
    costLedger.startSession("fraud-detection", teamId, userId);
    
    try {
      String result = claudeAPI.call(transaction);
      
      long elapsed = System.currentTimeMillis() - start;
      double cost = calculateCost(elapsed);
      
      costGovernor.checkBudget("fraud-detection", cost);
      costLedger.recordExecution(cost, elapsed);
      
      return result;
    } catch (CostExceededException e) {
      return retryWithFallback(transaction);
    }
  }
}
```

#### **Deployed to Kubernetes**
```bash
✅ Docker image built
✅ Prometheus metrics exported (cost_per_call, tokens_used, latency)
✅ Health checks passing
✅ Cost limits enforced
✅ Oracle wallet mounted (secure connection)
✅ Real-time cost tracking active
✅ Dashboard updated every 5 minutes
```

**Result**: 🎯 **From spec to production in ~30 minutes** (fully automated, AI-generated)
