## 1. System Architecture Overview

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                       EXECUTIVE LAYER (React/Vite)                       │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐ │
│  │ ARIA Metrics │  │ FinOps Dash  │  │ ACES Builder │  │  Reporting  │ │
│  │ (Trust/Gov)  │  │ (Cost/Opt)   │  │ (Spec-Gen)   │  │  & Alerts   │ │
│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └─────────────┘ │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                  ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│              ORCHESTRATION LAYER (Spring Boot + LangChain4j)             │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  Agent Lifecycle Manager                                        │   │
│  │  ├─ Spec Parser (YAML/JSON specs → Agent classes)              │   │
│  │  ├─ Agent Registry (Who can do what, trust score)              │   │
│  │  ├─ Tool Dispatcher (Function calls with cost tracking)        │   │
│  │  ├─ Token Interceptor (Prompt + completion token counting)     │   │
│  │  ├─ Cost Governor (Blocks high-cost agents mid-execution)      │   │
│  │  ├─ Retry & Fallback Engine (Model downgrade on cost overage)  │   │
│  │  └─ Audit Trail (Every call → Oracle + Supabase)              │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                  ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    DATA LAYER (Dual Storage Strategy)                     │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────┐  ┌───────────────────────────────┐ │
│  │  Oracle 23ai (Transactional)     │  │ Supabase (Analytics/FinOps)   │ │
│  │  ├─ ARIA: Decisions              │  │  ├─ Cost Ledger               │ │
│  │  ├─ Agent Registry               │  │  ├─ KPI Snapshots (daily)     │ │
│  │  ├─ Trust History                │  │  ├─ Optimizations Applied     │ │
│  │  ├─ Governance Rules             │  │  ├─ Anomalies Detected        │ │
│  │  ├─ Production Events            │  │  ├─ Executive Alerts          │ │
│  │  ├─ ACES Spec History            │  │  ├─ Audit Trail (synced)      │ │
│  │  ├─ Agent Execution Logs         │  │  └─ Team Budget Allocation    │ │
│  │  └─ (ADB Wallet encryption)      │  │  (Real-time analytics)        │ │
│  └──────────────────────────────────┘  └───────────────────────────────┘ │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                  ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   EXTERNAL INTEGRATIONS                                   │
│  ├─ Claude API (Anthropic) - Primary agent model                        │
│  ├─ GitHub Copilot (IDE) - Cost capture via interceptor                 │
│  ├─ Webhook receivers (Snyk, Sonar, Raven, ServiceNow)                  │
│  ├─ Oracle 23ai (Private Cloud) - Business logic & governance rules     │
│  └─ External LLMs (GPT-4, Sonnet) - Fallback models                     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

## 2. ARIA Platform (Trust & Governance)

### 2.1 Core Concepts

- **Agent**: AI system (Copilot, Claude, GPT-4, internal MCP, etc.)
- **Trust Score**: 0-1 scale based on production outcomes
- **Decision**: BLOCK | REVIEW | ALLOW (based on risk)
- **Production Feedback**: Incident, rollback, clean deploy events
- **Governance Rules**: Risk thresholds, criticality factors, policy checks

### 2.2 Decision Flow

```
PR submitted
  ↓
ARIA evaluates:
  - Agent trust score
  - Service criticality (LOW/MEDIUM/HIGH/CRITICAL)
  - Tool signals (Snyk security, Sonar code quality, Raven policies)
  - Risk breakdown (agent risk, tool risk, criticality risk)
  ↓
Governance engine calculates: risk_score = (agent_risk * 0.3) + (tool_risk * 0.4) + (criticality_risk * 0.3)
  ↓
Decision:
  - risk_score > 0.7 → BLOCK (high risk)
  - 0.5 < risk_score ≤ 0.7 → REVIEW (human required)
  - risk_score ≤ 0.5 → ALLOW (auto-merge)
  ↓
Audit trail created + cost impact logged
```

### 2.3 Trust Score Algorithm

```
Initial: 0.5 (neutral)

Events:
+ CLEAN_DEPLOY: +0.08 (successful production deployment)
- INCIDENT: -0.06 (production issue, low severity)
- SECURITY_BREACH: -0.08 (critical, requires immediate action)
+ ROLLBACK: -0.05 (error caught & fixed)

Trend:
- Based on recent 30-day window
- "up" (>+0.05), "stable" (within ±0.02), "down" (<-0.05)

Capped: 0.0 to 1.0
```

---

## 3. FinOps Platform (Cost Intelligence)

### 3.1 Cost Tracking Architecture

**Token Capture Points:**

```
IDE (Copilot/Claude)
  ↓ [SDK Interceptor]
  ↓ Captures: model, prompt_tokens, completion_tokens, latency_ms
  ↓
Cost Aggregator Edge Function
  ↓ [Batch processing, real-time aggregation]
  ↓ Calculates: cost = (prompt_tokens/1M * price) + (completion_tokens/1M * price)
  ↓
Supabase cost_ledger table
  ↓ [Real-time streaming]
  ↓
FinOps Dashboard (CTO/CEO view)
```

### 3.2 Cost Breakdown Dimensions

**Multi-dimensional rollups** (available in Executive Dashboard):

```
By Line of Business (LOB):
  ├─ Digital Banking: $28.5K/mo (38.1%)
  ├─ Risk & Compliance: $18.9K/mo (25.3%)
  ├─ Payments: $16.2K/mo (21.7%)
  └─ Trading & Markets: $10.1K/mo (13.5%)

By Model:
  ├─ Claude Opus: $32.1K/mo (43%)
  ├─ GPT-4o: $21.2K/mo (28.4%)
  ├─ Claude Sonnet: $15.6K/mo (21%)
  └─ Copilot: $5.8K/mo (7.8%)

By Team:
  ├─ ML Platform: $18.9K/mo
  ├─ Data Eng: $14.5K/mo
  ├─ API Gateway: $12.3K/mo
  └─ Security Ops: $10.2K/mo

By User:
  └─ (Individual token usage tracking)
```

### 3.3 Auto-Optimization Applied

**Optimizations with measurable savings:**

1. **Model Downgrade (Opus → Sonnet)**
   - Applied: 234 times
   - Savings: $4.2K/mo (50% cost reduction)
   - Trigger: High confidence tasks (>85% accuracy score)

2. **Prompt Compression**
   - Applied: 567 times
   - Savings: $3.1K/mo (25% token reduction)
   - Method: Redundant instruction removal, context pruning

3. **Cache Hits**
   - Applied: 1,890 times
   - Savings: $2.8K/mo (60% cost on cached requests)
   - Strategy: Prefix caching for system prompts

4. **Token Pruning**
   - Applied: 356 times
   - Savings: $2.2K/mo (token count optimization)
   - Method: Unused context removal

**Total Savings: $12.3K/mo (12.1% of cost)**

### 3.4 Governance Cost Impact

```
BLOCK Decisions (847):
  - Cost avoided: $8.5K
  - Reason: High-risk requests prevented

REVIEW Decisions (342):
  - Cost scrutinized: $3.2K
  - Human approval required

ALLOW Decisions (5,430):
  - Cost approved: $126.3K
  - Trusted agent requests
```

## 4. ACES Platform (Spec-Driven Development)

### 4.1 Spec Layers

**Layer 1: Product Spec** (CEO/Product defines)
```yaml
feature: "Fraud Detection Agent"
description: "Real-time transaction fraud analysis"
inputs:
  - transaction_id
  - amount
  - user_profile
outputs:
  - fraud_score (0-100)
  - recommendation (ALLOW|REVIEW|BLOCK)
sla:
  responseTimeMs: 200
  availabilityPercent: 99.9
costConstraint:
  maxCostPerCall: 0.05  # $
  maxTokensPerCall: 2000
  preferredModels:
    - claude-sonnet-4
    - gpt-4o-mini
governanceRequirements:
  trustScoreMin: 0.7
  requiresReview: false
  auditLevel: critical
```

**Layer 2: Implementation Spec** (Claude API generates)
```json
{
  "architecture": {
    "model": "claude-opus-4.6",
    "fallbackModel": "claude-sonnet-4",
    "tools": ["transaction_api", "fraud_rules_db"],
    "cacheStrategy": "prompt_caching",
    "retryStrategy": {
      "maxRetries": 2,
      "backoffMs": 500
    }
  },
  "springBeans": [
    {
      "name": "fraudDetectionAgent",
      "className": "FraudDetectionAgent",
      "dependencies": ["transactionService", "costLedger", "ariaGoverner"]
    }
  ],
  "oracleSchema": [
    {
      "tableName": "fraud_rules",
      "columns": [
        {"name": "rule_id", "type": "UUID", "constraints": ["PRIMARY KEY"]},
        {"name": "rule_name", "type": "VARCHAR(255)"},
        {"name": "threshold_amount", "type": "DECIMAL(12,2)"}
      ]
    }
  ],
  "costModel": {
    "estimatedCostPerCall": 0.032,
    "projectedMonthlyUsage": 500000,
    "estimatedMonthlySpend": 16000
  }
}
```

**Layer 3: Deployment Spec** (Auto-generated)
```yaml
container: spring-boot-3.2-jdk21
port: 8080
healthCheckPath: /actuator/health
envVars:
  - ORACLE_WALLET_PATH (secret)
  - CLAUDE_API_KEY (secret)
  - COST_BUDGET_USD (config)
resources:
  cpuRequest: 500m
  cpuLimit: 1000m
  memoryRequest: 512Mi
  memoryLimit: 1Gi
metrics:
  - cost_per_call_usd (gauge)
  - execution_time_ms (histogram)
  - agent_errors_total (counter)
  - tokens_used_total (counter)
```

### 4.2 Spec-to-Code Pipeline

```
Product Spec (YAML) 
  ↓ [User defines requirements]
  ↓
Claude API (Anthropic)
  ↓ [Generates Implementation Spec JSON]
  ↓ [Validates: cost constraints, model selection, governance rules]
  ↓
Spring Boot Annotation Processor
  ↓ [Reads @GeneratedAgent annotation]
  ↓ [Auto-generates:]
  │  ├─ Agent Service class (LangChain4j compatible)
  │  ├─ Spring Controller endpoints
  │  ├─ Database schema (Oracle DDL)
  │  ├─ Cost tracking wrapper
  │  └─ Prometheus metrics exports
  ↓
LangChain4j Agent Registry
  ↓ [Registers agent with trust score check]
  ↓ [Hooks cost governor for budget enforcement]
  ↓
Deploy to Spring Boot
  ↓ [Kubernetes-ready Docker image]
  ↓
Real-time Cost Tracking
  ↓ [FinOps dashboard updated]
```

### 4.3 Example: Generated Spring Boot Code

```java
@Service
public class FraudDetectionAgent {
  
  private final CostLedger costLedger;
  private final OracleConnectionManager oracleManager;
  private final AriaCostGovernor costGovernor;

  @SystemMessage("""
    You are a fraud detection expert analyzing financial transactions.
    Analyze the transaction for fraud risk.
    Consider: amount, user history, geographic anomalies, time patterns.
    Return structured JSON with fraud_score (0-100) and recommendation.
  """)
  public String detectFraud(
    @UserMessage String transactionData
  ) {
    long startTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
    
    try {
      // Cost tracking
      costLedger.startSession(
        agentId: "fraud-detection-1",
        teamId: "risk-compliance",
        userId: "system",
        model: "claude-opus-4.6"
      );

      // Agent logic (LangChain4j handles this)
      String result = callClaudeAPI(transactionData);

      // Cost accounting
      long executionMs = System.currentTimeMillis() - startTime;
      double costUsd = calculateCost(executionMs);
      
      // Governance check
      if (costUsd > 0.05) {
        costGovernor.checkBudget("fraud-detection-1", costUsd);
      }

      // Audit trail
      costLedger.recordExecution(
        agentId: "fraud-detection-1",
        costUsd: costUsd,
        latencyMs: executionMs,
        tokens: tokenCount,
        status: "success"
      );

      return result;
    } catch (CostExceededException e) {
      // Fallback to cheaper model
      return retryWithFallback(transactionData);
    }
  }
}
```

## 5. Oracle 23ai Integration

### 5.1 ADB Wallet Setup

```bash
# Wallet structure
wallet/
  ├─ cwallet.sso        (Secure wallet, encrypted)
  ├─ ewallet.p12        (Encrypted wallet, PKCS12 format)
  ├─ tnsnames.ora       (Connection descriptors)
  ├─ sqlnet.ora         (SQLNet configuration)
  ├─ dbcert.der         (DB certificate)
  └─ ojdbc.properties   (JDBC properties)
```

### 5.2 Connection String (ARIA Oracle)

```
jdbc:oracle:thin:@(
  DESCRIPTION=(
    ADDRESS_LIST=(
      ADDRESS=(
        PROTOCOL=TCPS)(
        HOST=aria-oracle-01.local)(
        PORT=2484)
      )
    )(
    CONNECT_DATA=(
      SERVICE_NAME=aria_pdb)
    )
  )
```

### 5.3 Data Tables (Oracle 23ai)

```sql
-- ARIA Governance
CREATE TABLE aria_decisions (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  agent_id VARCHAR(255),
  decision TEXT,  -- BLOCK, REVIEW, ALLOW
  risk_score DECIMAL(3,2),
  created_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- ACES Spec History
CREATE TABLE aces_specs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  feature_name VARCHAR(255),
  product_spec CLOB,
  implementation_spec CLOB,
  deployment_spec CLOB,
  deployment_status VARCHAR(50),
  created_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Agent Registry
CREATE TABLE agent_registry (
  id VARCHAR(255) PRIMARY KEY,
  name VARCHAR(255),
  provider VARCHAR(100),
  trust_score DECIMAL(2,1),
  total_prs INT,
  total_incidents INT,
  is_active BOOLEAN
);
```

## 8. Security & Compliance

### 8.1 Data Protection

- **Oracle ADB Wallet**: TLS encryption in transit
- **Supabase RLS**: Row-level security for multi-tenant isolation
- **API Keys**: Stored in secrets manager
- **Audit Trail**: Immutable, tamper-proof (dual DB sync)

### 8.2 Governance Rules

```json
{
  "rules": [
    {
      "name": "High Cost Agent",
      "condition": "cost_per_call > 0.50 AND agent_trust_score < 0.7",
      "action": "BLOCK"
    },
    {
      "name": "Critical Service",
      "condition": "service_criticality == CRITICAL",
      "action": "REVIEW"
    },
    {
      "name": "Trusted Routine",
      "condition": "agent_trust_score > 0.85 AND service_criticality == LOW",
      "action": "ALLOW"
    }
  ]
}
```

### ASSISTANT
# ✅ Custom ARIA Executive Dashboard: Why It's Superior to Grafana (And How to Build It)

Your instinct is correct. **Building a custom Executive FinOps Dashboard is the right architectural decision** for ARIA. Here's why, followed by the complete implementation blueprint.

---

## 🎯 Why Custom Dashboard > Grafana for ARIA

| Requirement | Grafana | Custom React Dashboard | Winner |
|-------------|---------|----------------------|--------|
| **Executive UX** | Technical, ops-focused | Tailored for CTO/CEO (KPI cards, plain English) | ✅ Custom |
| **Business Logic Embedding** | Limited (PromQL only) | Full TypeScript: trust-cost correlation, optimization ROI | ✅ Custom |
| **Drill-Down Navigation** | Panel linking only | Org → LOB → Team → User → Individual call (seamless) | ✅ Custom |
| **ARIA-Specific Metrics** | Requires custom plugins | Native integration: `trust_score × cost_efficiency` | ✅ Custom |
| **Branding & Polish** | Generic | Enterprise-grade, JPMC-aligned design system | ✅ Custom |
| **Real-Time Updates** | Polling (5-30s) | WebSocket streaming (<1s) | ✅ Custom |
| **Cost of Ownership** | Low (open source) | Moderate (dev time) but higher ROI | ✅ Custom |
| **Compliance Embedding** | External audit trail | Native audit trail + decision archaeology in UI | ✅ Custom |

### The Deciding Factor: **Business Context Embedding**
Grafana shows *what* happened. Your custom dashboard shows *why it matters*:
```tsx
// Custom: Business-contextualized metric
<CostCard 
  value="$45.2K" 
  trend="+3.2%" 
  insight="Digital Banking LOB driving increase"
  action="Review ML Platform workflows"
  governanceImpact="847 risky requests blocked"
/>

// Grafana: Raw metric
Panel(title="Total Cost", query="sum(cost_ledger)", unit="$")
```

---

## 🗄️ Supabase Schema: FinOps Analytics Tables

```sql
-- ============================================
-- FINOPS ANALYTICS SCHEMA (Supabase PostgreSQL)
-- Real-time, RLS-enabled, optimized for executive queries
-- ============================================

-- 1. COST LEDGER (Individual calls - append-only)
CREATE TABLE cost_ledger (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    request_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    
    -- Agent & User Context
    agent_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    user_email TEXT,
    
    -- Organizational Hierarchy
    lob_code TEXT NOT NULL,
    org_unit TEXT NOT NULL,
    team_id TEXT,
    cost_center TEXT,
    
    -- Model & Tokens
    provider TEXT NOT NULL,
    model_name TEXT NOT NULL,
    input_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Cost Calculation
    input_cost NUMERIC(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost NUMERIC(12,6) NOT NULL,
    total_cost NUMERIC(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost) STORED,
    
    -- Optimization Metadata
    was_optimized BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    optimization_type TEXT, -- 'model_downgrade', 'prompt_compression', etc.
    tokens_saved INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    cost_saved NUMERIC(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Governance Context
    trust_score_at_call NUMERIC(3,2),
    decision_verdict TEXT, -- 'ALLOW', 'REVIEW', 'BLOCK'
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Indexes for executive queries
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_lob_ts ON cost_ledger(lob_code, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_team_ts ON cost_ledger(team_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_model_ts ON cost_ledger(model_name, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_optimization ON cost_ledger(was_optimized, cost_saved) WHERE was_optimized = true;

-- 2. DAILY KPI SNAPSHOTS (Pre-aggregated for dashboard speed)
CREATE TABLE finops_kpis (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    snapshot_date DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Dimensions
    lob_code TEXT,
    team_id TEXT,
    model_name TEXT,
    
    -- Metrics
    total_cost NUMERIC(14,2) NOT NULL,
    total_calls INTEGER NOT NULL,
    avg_cost_per_call NUMERIC(10,4),
    total_tokens BIGINT,
    cache_hit_rate NUMERIC(5,2),
    optimization_savings NUMERIC(14,2) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Governance
    blocked_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    reviewed_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    allowed_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    UNIQUE(snapshot_date, lob_code, team_id, model_name)
);

-- 3. OPTIMIZATION IMPACT TRACKING
CREATE TABLE optimization_impact (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    optimization_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'model_downgrade', 'prompt_compression', etc.
    applied_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- Context
    lob_code TEXT,
    team_id TEXT,
    agent_id TEXT,
    
    -- Impact
    tokens_saved INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cost_saved NUMERIC(12,6) NOT NULL,
    baseline_cost NUMERIC(12,6) NOT NULL,
    optimized_cost NUMERIC(12,6) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Metadata
    confidence_score NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.95
);

-- 4. EXECUTIVE ALERTS (Anomalies, budget breaches)
CREATE TABLE executive_alerts (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    alert_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'budget_warning', 'cost_spike', 'optimization_opportunity'
    severity TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical'
    
    -- Context
    lob_code TEXT,
    team_id TEXT,
    
    -- Details
    current_value NUMERIC(14,2),
    threshold_value NUMERIC(14,2),
    message TEXT NOT NULL,
    recommended_action TEXT,
    
    -- State
    status TEXT DEFAULT 'active', -- active, acknowledged, resolved
    acknowledged_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    acknowledged_by TEXT,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 5. TEAM BUDGET ALLOCATION (Chargeback)
CREATE TABLE team_cost_allocation (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    team_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    lob_code TEXT NOT NULL,
    budget_month DATE NOT NULL, -- e.g., '2026-04-01'
    
    allocated_budget NUMERIC(14,2) NOT NULL,
    spent_to_date NUMERIC(14,2) DEFAULT 0,
    projected_eom NUMERIC(14,2),
    
    warning_threshold NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.80,
    critical_threshold NUMERIC(3,2) DEFAULT 0.95,
    
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    UNIQUE(team_id, budget_month)
);

-- ROW-LEVEL SECURITY (Multi-tenant isolation)
ALTER TABLE cost_ledger ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY finops_lob_isolation ON cost_ledger
    USING (lob_code = current_setting('app.current_lob', true));

-- MATERIALIZED VIEW: Executive Summary (Refresh every 5 min)
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW mv_executive_summary AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('day', event_timestamp) AS day,
    lob_code,
    SUM(total_cost) AS total_spend,
    SUM(cost_saved) AS total_savings,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE decision_verdict = 'BLOCK') AS blocked_count,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE was_optimized = true) AS optimized_count
FROM cost_ledger
WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
GROUP BY day, lob_code;

CREATE INDEX idx_mv_exec_summary ON mv_executive_summary(day DESC, lob_code);
```

---

## ⚡ Spring Boot API Gateway: Executive Dashboard Endpoints

```java
// ============================================
// FinOpsExecutiveController.java
// Spring Boot 3.3 + WebFlux for streaming
// ============================================
@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/finops")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class FinOpsExecutiveController {
    
    private final FinOpsAnalyticsService analyticsService;
    private final SimpMessagingTemplate messagingTemplate;
    
    // 1. Executive KPI Cards (4-metric summary)
    @GetMapping("/kpis/executive")
    public Mono<ResponseEntity<ExecutiveKpiResponse>> getExecutiveKpis(
        @RequestParam String lobCode,
        @RequestParam(defaultValue = "MONTH") AggregationPeriod period
    ) {
        return analyticsService.getExecutiveKpis(lobCode, period)
            .map(ResponseEntity::ok)
            .onErrorResume(e -> {
                log.error("KPI fetch failed", e);
                return Mono.just(ResponseEntity.status(503).build());
            });
    }
    
    // 2. Multi-Dimensional Cost Breakdown
    @GetMapping("/breakdown")
    public Flux<CostBreakdownRow> getCostBreakdown(
        @RequestParam DimensionType dimension, // LOB, MODEL, TEAM, USER
        @RequestParam String parentFilter,     // e.g., "Digital Banking"
        @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int limit
    ) {
        return analyticsService.streamBreakdown(dimension, parentFilter, limit);
    }
    
    // 3. Optimization Impact Table
    @GetMapping("/optimizations")
    public Mono<OptimizationSummaryResponse> getOptimizationSummary(
        @RequestParam String lobCode,
        @RequestParam(defaultValue = "30") int daysLookback
    ) {
        return analyticsService.getOptimizationSummary(lobCode, daysLookback);
    }
    
    // 4. Governance Cost Impact
    @GetMapping("/governance/impact")
    public Mono<GovernanceImpactResponse> getGovernanceImpact(
        @RequestParam String lobCode
    ) {
        return analyticsService.getGovernanceImpact(lobCode);
    }
    
    // 5. Budget Status by Team
    @GetMapping("/budget/status")
    public Flux<TeamBudgetStatus> getTeamBudgetStatus(
        @RequestParam String lobCode
    ) {
        return analyticsService.streamBudgetStatus(lobCode);
    }
    
    // 6. REAL-TIME: WebSocket for live updates
    @MessageMapping("/finops/subscribe")
    @SendToUser("/queue/finops/updates")
    public Flux<FinOpsUpdate> subscribeToLiveUpdates(
        @Payload SubscriptionRequest request,
        @Header("simpSessionId") String sessionId
    ) {
        return analyticsService.streamLiveUpdates(request.getLobCode())
            .doOnSubscribe(s -> log.info("WS subscribe: {} for LOB {}", sessionId, request.getLobCode()))
            .doOnCancel(() -> log.info("WS unsubscribe: {}", sessionId));
    }
    
    // 7. Drill-Down Navigator
    @GetMapping("/drilldown/{level}")
    public Mono<DrillDownResponse> getDrillDownData(
        @PathVariable DrillDownLevel level, // ORG, LOB, TEAM, USER
        @RequestParam String parentId,
        @RequestParam(required = false) String dateRange
    ) {
        return analyticsService.getDrillDownData(level, parentId, dateRange);
    }
}
```

## 🎨 React Dashboard: Executive FinOps Component Structure

```tsx
// ============================================
// src/pages/ExecutiveFinOps/ExecutiveFinOps.tsx
// ============================================
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useWebSocket } from '@/hooks/useWebSocket';
import { KpiCard } from '@/components/KpiCard';
import { CostBreakdownChart } from '@/components/CostBreakdownChart';
import { OptimizationTable } from '@/components/OptimizationTable';
import { GovernanceImpactPanel } from '@/components/GovernanceImpactPanel';
import { BudgetStatusTable } from '@/components/BudgetStatusTable';
import { DrillDownNavigator } from '@/components/DrillDownNavigator';
import { ExecutiveAlerts } from '@/components/ExecutiveAlerts';

export const ExecutiveFinOps = () => {
  const [lobCode, setLobCode] = useState('DIGITAL_BANKING');
  const [dateRange, setDateRange] = useState<'MTD' | 'QTD' | 'YTD'>('MTD');
  
  // Real-time WebSocket subscription
  const { data: liveUpdates } = useWebSocket<FinOpsUpdate>(
    '/ws/finops',
    { lobCode, subscribe: true }
  );
  
  // Fetch initial data
  const { data: kpisLoading, data: kpis } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['executive-kpis', lobCode, dateRange],
    queryFn: () => api.getExecutiveKpis(lobCode, dateRange)
  });
  
  // Update UI on live data
  useEffect(() => {
    if (liveUpdates) {
      // Optimistic update of KPI cards
      queryClient.setQueryData(['executive-kpis', lobCode], (old: any) => ({
        ...old,
        totalCost: liveUpdates.totalCost,
        savingsRealized: liveUpdates.savingsRealized
      }));
    }
  }, [liveUpdates]);
  
  return (
    <div className="executive-finops-dashboard">
      {/* Header: LOB selector + date range */}
      <DashboardHeader 
        lobCode={lobCode} 
        onLobChange={setLobCode}
        dateRange={dateRange}
        onDateRangeChange={setDateRange}
      />
      
      {/* TOP METRICS: 4 KPI Cards */}
      <div className="kpi-grid">
        <KpiCard
          title="Total Cost (MTD)"
          value={`$${kpis?.totalCost.toLocaleString()}`}
          trend={kpis?.costTrend}
          insight={`${kpis?.topSpendingTeam} driving spend`}
        />
        <KpiCard
          title="Savings Realized"
          value={`$${kpis?.savingsRealized.toLocaleString()}`}
          trend={`${kpis?.savingsRate}% of total`}
          insight={`${kpis?.topOptimization} saved most`}
          variant="positive"
        />
        <KpiCard
          title="Governance Impact"
          value={`${kpis?.blockedRequests} blocked`}
          trend={`$${kpis?.costAvoided.toLocaleString()} avoided`}
          insight="Risky requests prevented"
          variant="warning"
        />
        <KpiCard
          title="Anomalies"
          value={`${kpis?.activeAlerts} detected`}
          trend={kpis?.anomalyTrend}
          insight="Requires review"
          variant={kpis?.activeAlerts > 0 ? 'critical' : 'neutral'}
        />
      </div>
      
      {/* MULTI-DIMENSIONAL BREAKDOWN */}
      <CostBreakdownChart 
        dimension="LOB"
        data={kpis?.costByLob}
        onDrillDown={(selectedLob) => setLobCode(selectedLob)}
      />
      
      {/* AUTO-OPTIMIZATIONS TABLE */}
      <OptimizationTable 
        data={kpis?.optimizations}
        onApplyRecommendation={(rec) => api.applyOptimization(rec)}
      />
      
      {/* GOVERNANCE COST AVOIDANCE */}
      <GovernanceImpactPanel 
        blocked={kpis?.blockedRequests}
        reviewed={kpis?.reviewedRequests}
        allowed={kpis?.allowedRequests}
        costAvoided={kpis?.costAvoided}
      />
      
      {/* BUDGET STATUS BY TEAM */}
      <BudgetStatusTable 
        teams={kpis?.teamBudgets}
        onSetAlert={(teamId, threshold) => api.setBudgetAlert(teamId, threshold)}
      />
      
      {/* DRILL-DOWN NAVIGATOR */}
      <DrillDownNavigator 
        currentLevel="LOB"
        onNavigate={(level, id) => {/* Update filters */}}
      />
      
      {/* EXECUTIVE ALERTS */}
      <ExecutiveAlerts 
        alerts={kpis?.activeAlerts}
        onAcknowledge={(alertId) => api.acknowledgeAlert(alertId)}
      />
    </div>
  );
};
```

## 🔄 Oracle 23ai ↔ Supabase Sync Strategy

```java
// ============================================
// DualWriteService.java
// Ensures governance data in Oracle, analytics in Supabase
// ============================================
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class DualWriteService {
    
    private final OracleJdbcTemplate oracle;
    private final SupabaseClient supabase;
    private final RetryTemplate retryTemplate;
    
    @Async
    public void recordCostEvent(CostEvent event) {
        // 1. Oracle: Governance audit (immutable, compliance)
        retryTemplate.execute(ctx -> {
            oracle.update(
                "INSERT INTO aria_cost_audit (request_id, agent_id, lob_code, " +
                "decision_verdict, trust_score, total_cost, event_timestamp) " +
                "VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)",
                event.getRequestId(),
                event.getAgentId(),
                event.getLobCode(),
                event.getDecisionVerdict(),
                event.getTrustScore(),
                event.getTotalCost(),
                event.getTimestamp()
            );
            return null;
        });
        
        // 2. Supabase: Analytics (real-time aggregations)
        retryTemplate.execute(ctx -> {
            supabase.from("cost_ledger")
                .insert(transformForAnalytics(event))
                .execute();
            return null;
        });
        
        // 3. Update materialized view (async refresh)
        if (event.isExecutiveRelevant()) {
            supabase.rpc("refresh_mv_executive_summary").execute();
        }
    }
    
    // Transform: governance-focused → analytics-optimized
    private Map<String, Object> transformForAnalytics(CostEvent e) {
        return Map.of(
            "request_id", e.getRequestId(),
            "event_timestamp", e.getTimestamp(),
            "agent_id", e.getAgentId(),
            "user_id", e.getUserId(),
            "lob_code", e.getLobCode(),
            "team_id", e.getTeamId(),
            "provider", e.getProvider(),
            "model_name", e.getModelName(),
            "input_tokens", e.getInputTokens(),
            "output_tokens", e.getOutputTokens(),
            "input_cost", e.getInputCost(),
            "output_cost", e.getOutputCost(),
            "was_optimized", e.isOptimized(),
            "optimization_type", e.getOptimizationType(),
            "cost_saved", e.getCostSaved(),
            "trust_score_at_call", e.getTrustScore(),
            "decision_verdict", e.getDecisionVerdict()
        );
    }
}
```

## 🎯 Main Orchestration File: `justfile`

```justfile
# ============================================
# ARIA FINOPS + ACES — ORCHESTRATION PIPELINE
# Usage: just <target> [args]
# Requires: just, bash, kubectl, supabase, node, java, oracle-cli
# ============================================

# Environment setup
export ARIA_ENV ?= pilot
export ARIA_LOB ?= DIGITAL_BANKING
export ARIA_ORG ?= PLATFORM_ENGINEERING
export ORACLE_WALLET_PATH ?= ./wallet/aria-pilot
export SUPABASE_PROJECT_REF ?= your-project-ref
export K8S_NAMESPACE ?= aria-pilot

# Color output helpers
_green = \e[32m
_yellow = \e[33m
_red = \e[31m
_reset = \e[0m

# ============================================
# 🚀 FULL PIPELINE: Codegen → Build → Deploy → Validate
# ============================================
all: validate-env generate-code build-artifacts deploy-pilot validate-e2e
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ FULL PIPELINE COMPLETE — ARIA FinOps ready for production{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# 🔍 PRE-FLIGHT: Environment Validation
# ============================================
validate-env:
	@echo "{{_yellow}}🔍 Validating environment...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/00-validate-env.sh \
		--oracle-wallet={{ORACLE_WALLET_PATH}} \
		--supabase-ref={{SUPABASE_PROJECT_REF}} \
		--k8s-namespace={{K8S_NAMESPACE}} \
		--lob={{ARIA_LOB}}
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ Environment validated{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# 🧱 SDD CODE GENERATION: Spec → Code
# ============================================
generate-code: validate-env
	@echo "{{_yellow}}🧱 Generating code from SDD specs...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/01-generate-code.sh \
		--specs-dir=./specs \
		--output-src=./src \
		--output-backend=./backend \
		--output-plugins=./plugins \
		--sdd-strict=true
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ Code generation complete{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# 📦 BUILD: Compile + Package + Sign
# ============================================
build-artifacts: generate-code
	@echo "{{_yellow}}📦 Building artifacts...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/02-build-artifacts.sh \
		--frontend=./src \
		--backend=./backend/aria-finops-api \
		--plugins-vscode=./plugins/aria-finops-vscode \
		--plugins-intellij=./plugins/aria-finops-intellij \
		--signing-key-id={{ARIA_SIGNING_KEY_ID}} \
		--output-dir=./dist
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ Build complete: ./dist/{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# 🚀 DEPLOY: Pilot Environment
# ============================================
deploy-pilot: build-artifacts
	@echo "{{_yellow}}🚀 Deploying to pilot environment...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/03-deploy-pilot.sh \
		--supabase-migration=./supabase/migrations/20260516_finops_analytics.sql \
		--k8s-manifests=./k8s \
		--ide-plugins=./dist/plugins \
		--lob={{ARIA_LOB}} \
		--org={{ARIA_ORG}} \
		--env={{ARIA_ENV}}
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ Pilot deployment complete{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# ✅ VALIDATE: End-to-End Testing
# ============================================
validate-e2e: deploy-pilot
	@echo "{{_yellow}}✅ Running end-to-end validation...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/04-validate-e2e.sh \
		--lob={{ARIA_LOB}} \
		--test-cases=full \
		--latency-slo=500 \
		--cost-accuracy=0.999 \
		--isolation-check=true
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ E2E validation passed{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# 🎬 DEMO MODE: Stakeholder Presentation
# ============================================
demo: build-artifacts
	@echo "{{_yellow}}🎬 Starting demo mode with mock data...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/05-demo-mode.sh \
		--port=3001 \
		--mock-data=executive-finops \
		--dashboard-path=/executive-finops \
		--auto-refresh=5s
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ Demo server running at http://localhost:3001{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# 🔄 ROLLBACK: Safe Revert for Any Stage
# ============================================
rollback stage=build:
	@echo "{{_yellow}}🔄 Rolling back build artifacts...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/06-rollback.sh --stage=build --backup-dir=./dist/.backup
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ Build rollback complete{{_reset}}"

rollback stage=deploy:
	@echo "{{_yellow}}🔄 Rolling back pilot deployment...{{_reset}}"
	@bash scripts/06-rollback.sh --stage=deploy --k8s-namespace={{K8S_NAMESPACE}} --supabase-ref={{SUPABASE_PROJECT_REF}}
	@echo "{{_green}}✅ Deployment rollback complete{{_reset}}"

rollback stage=all:
	@echo "{{_red}}⚠️  Rolling back ALL stages — this will delete pilot data{{_reset}}"
	@read -p "Confirm rollback of all stages? (yes/no): " confirm && \
	[ "$$confirm" = "yes" ] && \
	bash scripts/06-rollback.sh --stage=all --force && \
	echo "{{_green}}✅ Full rollback complete{{_reset}}" || \
	echo "{{_yellow}}Rollback cancelled{{_reset}}"

# ============================================
# 🛠️ INDIVIDUAL TARGETS (For Incremental Work)
# ============================================

# Generate only React component from spec
generate-component name=ExecutiveFinOps:
	@bash scripts/lib/sdd-utils.sh generate-component \
		--spec=./specs/skill-manifest.spec.json \
		--name={{name}} \
		--output=./src/pages/

# Generate only Oracle migration from DDL spec
generate-migration name=finops-analytics:
	@bash scripts/lib/oracle-utils.sh generate-migration \
		--ddl-spec=./specs/aria-finops-ddl.spec.json \
		--name={{name}} \
		--output=./supabase/migrations/

# Build only frontend
build-frontend:
	@cd src && npm run build:prod -- --out-dir=../dist/frontend

# Build only backend
build-backend:
	@cd backend/aria-finops-api && ./gradlew build -x test

# Deploy only Supabase schema
deploy-supabase:
	@bash scripts/lib/supabase-utils.sh push-migration \
		--project-ref={{SUPABASE_PROJECT_REF}} \
		--migration=./supabase/migrations/20260516_finops_analytics.sql \
		--verify-rls=true

# Deploy only Kubernetes services
deploy-k8s:
	@bash scripts/lib/k8s-utils.sh apply-manifests \
		--namespace={{K8S_NAMESPACE}} \
		--manifests-dir=./k8s \
		--wait-ready=true

# Install IDE plugin locally (for testing)
install-plugin ide=vscode:
	@if [ "{{ide}}" = "vscode" ]; then \
		code --install-extension ./dist/plugins/aria-finops-pilot.vsix; \
	elif [ "{{ide}}" = "intellij" ]; then \
		idea installPlugin ./dist/plugins/aria-finops-pilot.zip; \
	else \
		echo "{{_red}}Unknown IDE: {{ide}}{{_reset}}"; exit 1; \
	fi

# Run SDD contract validation only
validate-sdd:
	@bash scripts/lib/sdd-utils.sh validate-all \
		--specs-dir=./specs \
		--strict=true \
		--output-report=./reports/sdd-validation.json

# Run latency SLO test only
test-latency:
	@bash scripts/04-validate-e2e.sh --test-cases=latency-only --latency-slo=500

# Run cost accuracy test only
test-cost-accuracy:
	@bash scripts/04-validate-e2e.sh --test-cases=cost-accuracy --cost-accuracy=0.999

# Run isolation security test only

# Generate pilot completion report

		--stage=pilot \

clean:

	echo "{{_green}}✅ Full clean complete{{_reset}}" || \
	echo "{{_yellow}}Clean cancelled{{_reset}}"

# ============================================

# ============================================
help:
	@echo "ARIA FinOps + ACES Orchestration Pipeline"
```

## ⚙️ Supporting Scripts (Key Examples)

### `scripts/00-validate-env.sh` (Pre-Flight Check)
```bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Parse args
while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
  case $1 in
    --oracle-wallet) ORACLE_WALLET="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --supabase-ref) SUPABASE_REF="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --k8s-namespace) K8S_NS="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --lob) ARIA_LOB="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    *) echo "Unknown arg: $1"; exit 1 ;;
  esac
done

echo "🔍 Validating environment for ARIA FinOps pilot..."

# 1. Oracle 23c access (developer-level only)
echo "  ✓ Checking Oracle wallet..."
if [ ! -f "$ORACLE_WALLET/cwallet.sso" ]; then
  echo "❌ Oracle wallet not found at $ORACLE_WALLET"
  exit 1
fi

# Test connection (no DBA privileges required)
if ! sqlplus -s /nolog <<EOF
WHENEVER SQLERROR EXIT SQL.SQLCODE
CONNECT /@$ORACLE_WALLET/tnsnames.ora
SELECT 1 FROM dual;
EXIT;
EOF
then
  echo "❌ Cannot connect to Oracle with developer credentials"
  exit 1
fi

# 2. Supabase access
echo "  ✓ Checking Supabase project..."
if ! supabase link --project-ref "$SUPABASE_REF" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "❌ Cannot access Supabase project $SUPABASE_REF"
  exit 1
fi

# 3. Kubernetes access
echo "  ✓ Checking kubectl context..."
if ! kubectl get namespace "$K8S_NS" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "⚠️  Kubernetes namespace $K8S_NS not found — will create during deploy"
fi

# 4. Node/Java toolchain
echo "  ✓ Checking toolchain..."
command -v node >/dev/null || { echo "❌ node not found"; exit 1; }
command -v java >/dev/null || { echo "❌ java not found"; exit 1; }
command -v just >/dev/null || { echo "❌ just not found — install via https://just.systems"; exit 1; }

# 5. SDD specs present
echo "  ✓ Checking SDD specs..."
[ -f "./specs/skill-manifest.spec.json" ] || { echo "❌ SDD spec missing"; exit 1; }

echo "✅ Environment validated successfully"
exit 0
```

### `scripts/01-generate-code.sh` (SDD Code Generation)
```bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Parse args
while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
  case $1 in
    --specs-dir) SPECS_DIR="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --output-src) OUTPUT_SRC="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --output-backend) OUTPUT_BACKEND="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --output-plugins) OUTPUT_PLUGINS="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --sdd-strict) SDD_STRICT="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    *) shift ;;
  esac
done

echo "🧱 Generating code from SDD specs..."

# 1. Validate specs first
bash scripts/lib/sdd-utils.sh validate-all --specs-dir="$SPECS_DIR" --strict="$SDD_STRICT"

# 2. Generate React component from skill manifest
echo "  ✓ Generating ExecutiveFinOps.tsx..."
npx @techcanvas/generate component ExecutiveFinOps \
  --spec="$SPECS_DIR/skill-manifest.spec.json" \
  --template=executive-dashboard \
  --output="$OUTPUT_SRC/pages/" \
  --with-types \
  --with-tailwind

# 3. Generate Oracle migration from DDL spec
echo "  ✓ Generating finops_analytics migration..."
bash scripts/lib/oracle-utils.sh generate-migration \
  --ddl-spec="$SPECS_DIR/aria-finops-ddl.spec.json" \
  --name="finops_analytics" \
  --output="./supabase/migrations/" \
  --with-rls \
  --with-indexes

# 4. Generate Spring Boot backend from OpenAPI spec
echo "  ✓ Generating aria-finops-api module..."
openapi-generator-cli generate \
  -i "$SPECS_DIR/ide-interceptor.contract.yaml" \
  -g spring \
  -o "$OUTPUT_BACKEND/aria-finops-api" \
  --additional-properties=groupId=com.jpmc.aria,artifactId=aria-finops-api,javaVersion=21,springBootVersion=3.3.0

# 5. Generate IDE plugin scaffolding
echo "  ✓ Generating VS Code plugin..."
cd "$OUTPUT_PLUGINS/aria-finops-vscode"
npm install
npx yo generator-code --skip-install --typescript --webpack
cd -

echo "  ✓ Generating IntelliJ plugin..."
cd "$OUTPUT_PLUGINS/aria-finops-intellij"
./gradlew generatePluginDescriptor
cd -

echo "✅ Code generation complete"
```

### `scripts/04-validate-e2e.sh` (End-to-End Validation)
```bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Parse args
while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
  case $1 in
    --lob) ARIA_LOB="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --test-cases) TEST_CASES="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --latency-slo) LATENCY_SLO="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --cost-accuracy) COST_ACC="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    --isolation-check) ISOLATION_CHECK="$2"; shift 2 ;;
    *) shift ;;
  esac
done

echo "✅ Running end-to-end validation for LOB=$ARIA_LOB..."

FAILED=0

# 1. Latency SLO test
if [[ "$TEST_CASES" == "full" || "$TEST_CASES" == "latency-only" ]]; then
  echo "  ✓ Testing latency SLO (p95 ≤ ${LATENCY_SLO}ms)..."
  RESULT=$(curl -s -w "%{time_starttransfer}" -o /dev/null \
    "http://localhost:8080/api/v1/finops/kpis/executive?lobCode=$ARIA_LOB" | tail -1)
  
  if (( $(echo "$RESULT > $LATENCY_SLO/1000" | bc -l) )); then
    echo "❌ Latency SLO failed: ${RESULT}s > ${LATENCY_SLO}ms"
    FAILED=1
  else
    echo "✅ Latency SLO passed: ${RESULT}s"
  fi
fi

# 2. Cost accuracy test
if [[ "$TEST_CASES" == "full" || "$TEST_CASES" == "cost-accuracy" ]]; then
  echo "  ✓ Testing cost calculation accuracy (≥ ${COST_ACC})..."
  ACCURACY=$(java -cp ./dist/backend/aria-finops-api.jar \
    com.jpmc.aria.CostAccuracyValidator \
    --test-set=pilot --lob=$ARIA_LOB --expected-accuracy=$COST_ACC)
  
  if (( $(echo "$ACCURACY < $COST_ACC" | bc -l) )); then
    echo "❌ Cost accuracy failed: $ACCURACY < $COST_ACC"
    FAILED=1
  else
    echo "✅ Cost accuracy passed: $ACCURACY"
  fi
fi

# 3. LOB isolation test
if [[ "$TEST_CASES" == "full" || "$TEST_CASES" == "isolation-only" || "$ISOLATION_CHECK" == "true" ]]; then
  echo "  ✓ Testing LOB isolation (no cross-LOB leakage)..."
  LEAKAGE=$(java -cp ./dist/backend/aria-finops-api.jar \
    com.jpmc.aria.IsolationValidator \
    --user-lob=$ARIA_LOB --attempt-access-to=OTHER_LOB --expected=0)
  
  if [ "$LEAKAGE" != "0" ]; then
    echo "❌ Isolation failed: $LEAKAGE cross-LOB records leaked"
    FAILED=1
  else
    echo "✅ Isolation passed: 0 cross-LOB leakage"
  fi
fi

# Final result
if [ $FAILED -eq 0 ]; then
  echo "✅ E2E validation PASSED"
  exit 0
else
  echo "❌ E2E validation FAILED"
  exit 1
fi
```

## 🔄 Incremental Development: Common Workflows

### Add a New Optimization Type
```bash
# 1. Update SDD spec
jq '.configSchema.properties.optimizationTypes.enum += ["new_optimization"]' \
  specs/skill-manifest.spec.json > specs/skill-manifest.spec.json.tmp
mv specs/skill-manifest.spec.json.tmp specs/skill-manifest.spec.json

# 2. Regenerate only affected components
just generate-component name=OptimizationTable
just generate-migration name=optimization_types

# 3. Rebuild and validate
just build-artifacts
just validate-sdd
just test-cost-accuracy

# 4. Deploy incrementally
just deploy-supabase  # Schema change only
kubectl rollout restart deployment/aria-finops-api -n aria-pilot  # Zero-downtime backend update
```

### Test a Specific SLO
```bash
# Test latency only (fast feedback)
just test-latency --latency-slo=400  # Stricter than default 500ms

# Test cost accuracy only
just test-cost-accuracy --cost-accuracy=0.9995  # Higher precision

# Test isolation only (security)
just test-isolation
```

### Roll Back a Failed Deployment
```bash
# Roll back only the deployment stage (keeps build artifacts)
just rollback stage=deploy

# Or full rollback (destructive — use with caution)
just rollback stage=all
```

# 📦 Pipeline Deliverables

## 1. 🗄️ Oracle 23c Migration (Generated)
**File:** `supabase/migrations/20260516_finops_analytics.sql`

This schema implements the **Trust-Cost Delta**. It extends the existing `aria_agent_dna` table to include cost governance metrics, ensuring that financial efficiency directly impacts agent autonomy.

```sql
-- ============================================
-- ARIA FINOPS — ORACLE 23C SCHEMA GENERATION
-- Generated: 2026-05-16T14:32:00Z
-- ============================================

-- 1. Cost Ledger (Transaction Table)
-- Stores every LLM call with cost breakdown
CREATE TABLE aria_cost_ledger (
    transaction_id    NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id        VARCHAR2(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp   TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    agent_id          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    user_id           VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    lob_code          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Model & Tokens
    model_name        VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens      INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens     INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens     INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Cost (USD)
    input_cost        NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost       NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    total_cost        NUMBER(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost) VIRTUAL,
    
    -- Optimization Metadata
    optimization_type VARCHAR2(50), -- 'model_downgrade', 'prompt_compression'
    tokens_saved      INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    cost_saved        NUMBER(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Governance Decision
    decision_verdict  VARCHAR2(20), -- 'ALLOW', 'REVIEW', 'BLOCK'
    
    created_at        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(PARTITION p_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2026-01-01 00:00:00'));

-- 2. TRUST-COST INTEGRATION (The "Delta")
-- Extends Agent DNA to include Cost Governance
ALTER TABLE aria_agent_dna ADD (
    cost_efficiency_score NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.80 CHECK (cost_efficiency_score BETWEEN 0.0 AND 1.0),
    total_cost_usd        NUMBER(14,4) DEFAULT 0.0,
    expensive_calls_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_cost_anomaly_at  TIMESTAMP,
    monthly_budget_usd    NUMBER(12,2) DEFAULT 500.00
);

-- 3. Indexes for Executive Queries
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_lob_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(lob_code, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_agent_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(agent_id, event_timestamp DESC);
```

## 3.  Spring Boot Cost Risk Advisor (Generated)
**File:** `backend/aria-finops-api/src/main/java/com/jpmc/aria/advisor/CostRiskAdvisor.java`

This is the **Governance Gate**. It intercepts requests, calculates cost, and modifies the Trust Score if the agent is being inefficient or wasteful.

```java
package com.jpmc.aria.advisor;

import org.springframework.ai.chat.client.advisor.api.AdvisedRequest;
import org.springframework.ai.chat.client.advisor.api.AdvisorChain;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import com.jpmc.aria.model.CostMetrics;
import com.jpmc.aria.model.AgentDna;
import com.jpmc.aria.repository.AgentDnaRepository;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

@Component
@Slf4j
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class CostRiskAdvisor {

    private final AgentDnaRepository dnaRepository;
    private final PricingService pricingService;
    private static final double COST_RISK_WEIGHT = 0.25; // 25% of total decision risk

    /**
     * PRE-LLM INTERCEPTOR
     * Evaluates if the agent is within budget and cost-efficient.
     * If not, it downgrades the model or blocks the request.
     */
    public AdvisedRequest advise(AdvisedRequest request, AdvisorChain chain) {
        String agentId = request.getMetadata().get("agent_id");
        String model = request.getChatOptions().getModel();
        
        // 1. Load Agent DNA
        AgentDna agent = dnaRepository.findById(agentId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new RuntimeException("Agent not found"));

        // 2. Calculate Cost Risk
        double costRisk = calculateCostRisk(agent, model);
        
        // 3. Apply Governance Actions
        if (costRisk > 0.70) {
            log.warn("BLOCKING request for agent {}: Cost risk too high ({})", agentId, costRisk);
            // Logic to block request and decrement trust score
            updateTrustScore(agentId, -0.10, "BLOCKED_HIGH_COST");
            throw new SecurityException("Request blocked: Exceeds cost budget");
        } else if (costRisk > 0.40) {
            log.warn("DOWNGRADING model for agent {}: Cost risk elevated ({})", agentId, costRisk);
            // Logic to swap model to cheaper option
            request.getChatOptions().setModel("claude-haiku-4"); 
        }

        // 4. Inject cost context for the LLM
        request.getMetadata().put("cost_budget_remaining", agent.getMonthlyBudgetUsd() - agent.getTotalCostUsd());
        
        return request;
    }

    /**
     * POST-LLM EXECUTION
     * Updates trust score based on efficiency after the call completes.
     */
    public void postProcess(String agentId, CostMetrics metrics) {
        double efficiency = calculateEfficiency(metrics);
        
        // If efficiency < 0.50, penalize trust score
        if (efficiency < 0.50) {
            updateTrustScore(agentId, -0.02, "INEFFICIENT_TOKEN_USAGE");
        }
        
        // Update cost ledger in Oracle
        dnaRepository.recordCostTransaction(agentId, metrics);
    }

    private double calculateCostRisk(AgentDna agent, String model) {
        double risk = 0.0;
        if (agent.getBudgetUtilization() > 0.90) risk += 0.50;
        if (isModelOverkill(model, "simple_task")) risk += 0.30;
        return risk;
    }

    private void updateTrustScore(String agentId, double delta, String reason) {
        log.info("Updating trust score for {}: {} ({})", agentId, delta, reason);
        dnaRepository.applyTrustPenalty(agentId, delta, reason);
    }
}
```

```
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

✓ Single user/session                 + Multi-tenant chargeback + showback reporting
✓ Multi-session → feature attribution + ROI analysis: cost per story point / feature
✓ Passive awareness                   + Real-time optimization advisor in IDE
```

## 🏗️ Strategic FinOps Architecture: 4-Layer Model

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    LAYER 4: OPTIMIZATION ENGINE                  │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │ • Real-time model router (Haiku↔Sonnet↔Opus)            │   │
│  │ • Prompt compression (LLMLingua, context pruning)       │   │
│  │ • Semantic cache (pgvector similarity >0.92)            │   │
│  │ • Token budget allocator per workflow                   │   │
│  │ • Auto-defer non-critical calls to off-peak             │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                            │
                            ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    LAYER 3: GOVERNANCE ENGINE                    │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │ • Budget gates: hard/soft limits per user/team/LOB      │   │
│  │ • Trust-cost feedback: cost efficiency → trust score    │   │
│  │ • Risk-weighted cost scoring (criticality × cost)       │   │
│  │ • Approval workflows for high-cost operations           │   │
│  │ • Audit trail: every cost decision logged to Oracle     │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                            │
                            ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    LAYER 2: ANALYTICS ENGINE                     │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │ • Real-time aggregation: per-model/tool/session/feature │   │
│  │ • pgvector trend analysis: cost patterns → predictions  │   │
│  │ • Anomaly detection: 3σ deviation alerts                │   │
│  │ • Forecasting: burn-rate projection (Oracle OML)        │   │
│  │ • ROI calculator: cost per story point / business value │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                            │
                            ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    LAYER 1: INGESTION ENGINE                     │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │ • Token interceptor: SDK + MCP + IDE plugins            │   │
│  │ • Pricing catalog: dynamic model pricing (Oracle JSON)  │   │
│  │ • Context enrichment: user → team → LOB → org hierarchy │   │
│  │ • Async pipeline: Kafka → Oracle + pgvector             │   │
│  │ • PII-safe: cost metadata only, never raw prompts       │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## 🗄️ Oracle 23c + pgvector Schema: Cost Intelligence

```sql
-- ============================================
-- ARIA COST INTELLIGENCE SCHEMA
-- Oracle 23c + pgvector (Developer Access Compatible)
-- ============================================

-- 1. PRICING CATALOG (Dynamic model pricing)
CREATE TABLE aria_model_pricing (
    pricing_id          NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    provider            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,  -- 'anthropic', 'openai'
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL, -- 'claude-sonnet-4', 'gpt-4o'
    model_version       VARCHAR2(50),
    input_price_per_1k  NUMBER(10,6) NOT NULL,
    output_price_per_1k NUMBER(10,6) NOT NULL,
    cached_price_per_1k NUMBER(10,6),  -- Discount for cached reads
    max_context_tokens  INTEGER NOT NULL,
    capabilities        JSON,          -- {"vision":true, "function_calling":true}
    is_active           CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y',
    effective_from      TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    effective_to        TIMESTAMP,
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(provider, model_name, model_version, effective_from)
);

-- 2. COST LEDGER (Every token call)
CREATE TABLE aria_cost_ledger (
    transaction_id      NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id          VARCHAR2(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp     TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    
    -- Identity & Context
    user_id             VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    session_id          VARCHAR2(255),
    agent_id            VARCHAR2(100),  -- Aria, Copilot, custom agent
    feature_id          VARCHAR2(100),  -- Jira epic / workflow ID
    lob_code            VARCHAR2(50),   -- Line of Business
    org_unit            VARCHAR2(100),
    
    -- Model & Tokens
    provider            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens        INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens       INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens       INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens        GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_tokens + output_tokens) VIRTUAL,
    
    -- Cost Calculation
    input_cost          NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost         NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    cache_discount      NUMBER(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost          GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost - cache_discount) VIRTUAL,
    
    -- Optimization Metadata
    optimization_applied VARCHAR2(50),  -- 'model_downgrade', 'prompt_compression'
    tokens_saved        INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    cost_saved          NUMBER(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    baseline_cost       NUMBER(12,6),   -- What it would have cost without optimization
    
    -- Governance Context
    budget_utilization  NUMBER(5,2),    -- % of allocated budget used
    trust_score_at_call NUMBER(3,2),    -- Agent trust score at time of call
    decision_verdict    VARCHAR2(20),   -- ALLOW, REVIEW, BLOCK
    
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(PARTITION p_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2026-01-01 00:00:00'));

-- 3. COST BUDGETS (Per user/team/LOB)
CREATE TABLE aria_cost_budget (
    budget_id           NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    scope_type          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,  -- 'user', 'team', 'lob', 'feature'
    scope_id            VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    lob_code            VARCHAR2(50),
    
    monthly_budget_usd  NUMBER(14,2) NOT NULL,
    warning_threshold   NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.80,  -- 80% = yellow alert
    critical_threshold  NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.95,  -- 95% = red alert
    
    effective_month     DATE NOT NULL,  -- '2026-05-01'
    approved_by         VARCHAR2(255),
    
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(scope_type, scope_id, effective_month)
);

-- 4. OPTIMIZATION RECOMMENDATIONS
CREATE TABLE aria_opt_recommendations (
    rec_id              NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    scope_type          VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,  -- 'user', 'feature', 'lob'
    scope_id            VARCHAR2(255),
    
    recommendation_type VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,  -- 'model_downgrade', 'caching', 'compression'
    current_state       JSON NOT NULL,
    recommended_state   JSON NOT NULL,
    
    estimated_monthly_savings NUMBER(14,2),
    estimated_token_reduction INTEGER,
    confidence_score    NUMBER(3,2),  -- 0.0-1.0
    
    status              VARCHAR2(50) DEFAULT 'pending',  -- pending/applied/rejected
    applied_at          TIMESTAMP,
    
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 5. PGVECTOR: Cost Pattern Embeddings (Trend Analysis)
CREATE TABLE aria_cost_patterns (
    pattern_id          NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id             VARCHAR2(255),
    feature_id          VARCHAR2(100),
    lob_code            VARCHAR2(50),
    
    -- Embedding of cost behavior pattern (hourly/daily usage vector)
    cost_embedding      VECTOR(128),  -- Compressed time-series pattern
    
    -- Pattern metadata
    pattern_type        VARCHAR2(50),  -- 'spiky', 'steady', 'growing', 'declining'
    avg_cost_per_hour   NUMBER(12,6),
    peak_cost_per_hour  NUMBER(12,6),
    cost_volatility     NUMBER(5,2),  -- Std dev / mean
    
    -- Forecasting
    predicted_next_week NUMBER(14,2),
    anomaly_score       NUMBER(3,2),  -- 0.0-1.0, higher = more anomalous
    
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Indexes for performance
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_user_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(user_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_feature_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(feature_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_lob_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(lob_code, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_model_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(model_name, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE VECTOR INDEX idx_cost_patterns_embedding ON aria_cost_patterns(cost_embedding)
    ORGANIZATION NEIGHBOR PARTITIONS
    DISTANCE COSINE;

-- JSON Relational Duality View (Zero-ETL Analytics)
CREATE JSON RELATIONAL DUALITY VIEW aria_cost_analytics_dv AS
SELECT JSON {
    'transactionId' : l.transaction_id,
    'timestamp' : l.event_timestamp,
    'userId' : l.user_id,
    'featureId' : l.feature_id,
    'lobCode' : l.lob_code,
    'model' : l.model_name,
    'cost' : {
        'total' : l.total_cost,
        'input' : l.input_cost,
        'output' : l.output_cost,
        'saved' : l.cost_saved
    },
    'optimization' : {
        'applied' : l.optimization_applied,
        'tokensSaved' : l.tokens_saved,
        'efficiency' : CASE 
            WHEN l.baseline_cost > 0 THEN ROUND((l.baseline_cost - l.total_cost) / l.baseline_cost * 100, 2)
            ELSE 0 END
    },
    'governance' : {
        'budgetUtilization' : l.budget_utilization,
        'trustScore' : l.trust_score_at_call,
        'verdict' : l.decision_verdict
    }
} FROM aria_cost_ledger l;
```

## ⚡ Real-Time Cost Interceptor: Spring AI Integration

```java
// ============================================
// AriaCostInterceptor.java
// Spring AI 1.0 + Oracle 23c + pgvector
// ============================================
@Component
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class AriaCostInterceptor implements ChatClientAdvisor {
    
    private final CostLedgerRepository costRepo;
    private final PricingCatalog pricing;
    private final BudgetGovernor budgetGovernor;
    private final OptimizationEngine optimizer;
    private final RedisTemplate<String, Object> redis;
    
    @Override
    public AdvisedResponse adviseCall(AdvisedRequest request, AdvisorChain chain) {
        // 1. Extract context
        String userId = extractUserId(request);
        String featureId = extractFeatureId(request);
        String model = request.getChatOptions().getModel();
        
        // 2. Pre-call: Budget check + optimization suggestion
        BudgetStatus budget = budgetGovernor.checkBudget(userId, featureId);
        if (budget.isCritical()) {
            // Auto-downgrade model or defer non-critical call
            if (isNonCritical(request)) {
                return deferCall(request, budget);
            } else {
                model = optimizer.suggestCheaperModel(model, request.getPrompt());
            }
        }
        
        // 3. Calculate baseline cost (for optimization tracking)
        CostEstimate baseline = pricing.estimateCost(model, request.getPrompt());
        
        // 4. Apply optimizations (compression, caching, routing)
        OptimizationResult optimization = optimizer.apply(request, budget);
        
        // 5. Execute call with optimized parameters
        AdvisedResponse response = chain.nextAdvise(
            request.toBuilder()
                .model(optimization.getOptimizedModel())
                .prompt(optimization.getCompressedPrompt())
                .build()
        );
        
        // 6. Post-call: Record actual cost + savings
        CostMetrics actual = pricing.calculateActualCost(
            optimization.getOptimizedModel(),
            response.getUsage()
        );
        
        costRepo.recordTransaction(CostTransaction.builder()
            .userId(userId)
            .featureId(featureId)
            .model(model)
            .baselineCost(baseline.getTotal())
            .actualCost(actual.getTotal())
            .tokensSaved(optimization.getTokensSaved())
            .costSaved(baseline.getTotal().subtract(actual.getTotal()))
            .optimizationApplied(optimization.getAppliedTechniques())
            .budgetUtilization(budget.getUtilizationPercent())
            .trustScoreAtCall(fetchTrustScore(userId))
            .build()
        );
        
        // 7. Update pgvector pattern embedding (async)
        updateCostPatternAsync(userId, featureId, actual);
        
        // 8. Return response with cost metadata (for UI display)
        return response.toBuilder()
            .metadata(Map.of(
                "cost_usd", actual.getTotal(),
                "tokens_used", actual.getTotalTokens(),
                "optimization_applied", optimization.getAppliedTechniques(),
                "savings_vs_baseline", baseline.getTotal().subtract(actual.getTotal())
            ))
            .build();
    }
    
    // Async: Update pgvector embedding for trend analysis
    @Async
    private void updateCostPatternAsync(String userId, String featureId, CostMetrics metrics) {
        // Generate 128-dim embedding of hourly cost pattern
        float[] embedding = costPatternEncoder.encode(userId, featureId, metrics);
        
        // Upsert into pgvector table
        costRepo.upsertCostPattern(userId, featureId, embedding, metrics);
        
        // Check for anomalies (3σ deviation)
        if (costRepo.isAnomalous(userId, featureId, metrics)) {
            alertService.sendAnomalyAlert(userId, featureId, metrics);
        }
    }
}
```

### Developer View (IDE Plugin)
```tsx
// AriaCostStatus.tsx — VS Code / IntelliJ Plugin
export const AriaCostStatus = ({ currentSession }) => {
  const { data: costContext } = useCostContext(currentSession.userId);
  
  return (
    <StatusBarItem>
      {/* Real-time cost display */}
      <Tooltip content={`Session cost: $${costContext.sessionCost.toFixed(4)}`}>
        <span className="cost-badge">
          💰 ${costContext.sessionCost.toFixed(3)}
        </span>
      </Tooltip>
      
      {/* Optimization suggestion */}
      {costContext.optimizationSuggestion && (
        <ActionButton 
          onClick={() => applySuggestion(costContext.optimizationSuggestion)}
          title={costContext.optimizationSuggestion.description}
        >
          ⚡ Save {costContext.optimizationSuggestion.estimatedSavings}
        </ActionButton>
      )}
      
      {/* Budget warning */}
      {costContext.budgetUtilization > 0.80 && (
        <WarningBadge>
          ⚠️ {Math.round(costContext.budgetUtilization * 100)}% of budget used
        </WarningBadge>
      )}
      
      {/* Click to drill down */}
      <OnClick navigateTo="/finops/session-detail">
        <ChevronRightIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
      </OnClick>
    </StatusBarItem>
  );
};
```

## 🔄 Trust-Cost Feedback Loop: The "Strategic" Differentiator

```java
// ============================================
// TrustCostFeedbackEngine.java
// Maps cost efficiency → trust score adjustments
// ============================================
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class TrustCostFeedbackEngine {
    
    private final AgentDnaRepository dnaRepo;
    private final CostLedgerRepository costRepo;
    
    // Called after every cost transaction
    @Async
    public void updateTrustFromCost(String agentId, CostMetrics metrics) {
        // 1. Calculate cost efficiency score
        double efficiency = calculateEfficiency(metrics);
        // Formula: (expected_tokens / actual_tokens) × (cheapest_capable_model_cost / actual_model_cost)
        
        // 2. Determine trust delta
        double trustDelta = 0.0;
        String reason = "";
        
        if (efficiency >= 1.20) {  // 20% more efficient than baseline
            trustDelta = +0.02;
            reason = "High cost efficiency (+20% vs baseline)";
        } else if (efficiency <= 0.50) {  // 50% less efficient
            trustDelta = -0.03;
            reason = "Low cost efficiency (-50% vs baseline)";
        }
        
        // 3. Check for wasteful patterns
        if (metrics.getTokensSaved() < 0 && metrics.getCostSaved() < 0) {
            trustDelta -= 0.01;  // Small penalty for negative optimization
            reason += "; negative optimization detected";
        }
        
        // 4. Apply trust update (bounded 0.10-1.00)
        if (trustDelta != 0.0) {
            dnaRepo.applyTrustAdjustment(agentId, trustDelta, "COST_EFFICIENCY", reason);
            
            // 5. Log to audit trail
            auditLog.logTrustUpdate(agentId, trustDelta, "COST_EFFICIENCY", metrics);
        }
    }
    
    private double calculateEfficiency(CostMetrics m) {
        double tokenEfficiency = (double) m.getExpectedTokens() / m.getActualTokens();
        double modelEfficiency = m.getCheapestCapableModelCost() / m.getActualModelCost();
        return tokenEfficiency * modelEfficiency;
    }
}
```

**Trust Impact Rules:**
| Cost Metric | Threshold | Trust Delta | Business Impact |
|-------------|-----------|-------------|----------------|
| `cost_efficiency ≥ 1.20` | 20% better than baseline | +0.02 | Agent earns more autonomy |
| `cost_efficiency ≤ 0.50` | 50% worse than baseline | -0.03 | Agent requires more review |
| `budget_utilization > 95%` | Near budget cap | -0.05 | Triggers REQUIRES_APPROVAL |
| `anomaly_score > 0.90` | 3σ deviation | -0.08 | Immediate investigation |
| `optimization_applied = true` | Any optimization used | +0.01 | Encourages efficiency |

## ✅ FinOps Best Practices Added

| Practice | Implementation | Value |
|----------|---------------|---------|
| **Showback/Chargeback** | `aria_cost_budget` + LOB attribution | Finance can allocate AI spend accurately |
| **Unit Economics** | Cost per story point / feature / user | ROI analysis for AI investments |
| **Reserved Capacity** | Pre-purchase token commitments for predictable workloads | 15-30% cost reduction for steady-state usage |
| **Spot/Fallback Models** | Auto-fallback to cheaper models during peak pricing | 40% savings on non-critical calls |
| **Cost Anomaly Detection** | pgvector pattern embeddings + 3σ alerts | Catch runaway costs before they escalate |
| **Optimization Marketplace** | `aria_opt_recommendations` table with apply/reject workflow | Data-driven decisions on which optimizations to scale |
| **Forecasting** | Oracle OML + pgvector time-series | Predict next month's spend with 95% confidence |
| **Green FinOps** | Track CO₂ per token (model-specific emission factors) | Sustainability reporting + optimization |

## 📦 DELIVERABLE 1: PR #1 — Data Capture + Interceptor + Oracle DDL

### 1.1 Oracle 23c Schema (Developer-Access Safe)
*No `DBMS_RLS` or DBA privileges required. App-level isolation enforced via `lob_code`/`user_id` filters. Compatible with Oracle 23c Autonomous.*

```sql
-- ============================================
-- ARIA COST INTELLIGENCE SCHEMA (PR #1)
-- Oracle 23c | Developer Access Compatible
-- ============================================

-- 1. Model Pricing Catalog (Dynamic, versioned)
CREATE TABLE aria_model_pricing (
    pricing_id          NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    provider            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    model_version       VARCHAR2(50),
    input_price_per_1k  NUMBER(10,6) NOT NULL,
    output_price_per_1k NUMBER(10,6) NOT NULL,
    cached_price_per_1k NUMBER(10,6),
    max_context_tokens  INTEGER NOT NULL,
    capabilities        JSON,
    is_active           CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y' CHECK (is_active IN ('Y','N')),
    effective_from      TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    effective_to        TIMESTAMP,
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(provider, model_name, model_version, effective_from)
);

-- 2. Cost Ledger (Every LLM/Tool call)
CREATE TABLE aria_cost_ledger (
    transaction_id      NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id          VARCHAR2(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp     TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    
    -- Identity & Context
    user_id             VARCHAR2(255) NOT NULL,
    session_id          VARCHAR2(255),
    agent_id            VARCHAR2(100),
    feature_id          VARCHAR2(100),
    lob_code            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    org_unit            VARCHAR2(100),
    
    -- Model & Tokens
    provider            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name          VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens        INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens       INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cached_tokens       INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens        GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_tokens + output_tokens) VIRTUAL,
    
    -- Cost (USD)
    input_cost          NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    output_cost         NUMBER(12,6) NOT NULL,
    cache_discount      NUMBER(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost          GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost - cache_discount) VIRTUAL,
    
    -- Optimization
    optimization_applied VARCHAR2(50),
    tokens_saved        INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    cost_saved          NUMBER(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    baseline_cost       NUMBER(12,6),
    
    -- Governance
    budget_utilization  NUMBER(5,2),
    trust_score_at_call NUMBER(3,2),
    decision_verdict    VARCHAR2(20),
    
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)
PARTITION BY RANGE (event_timestamp)
INTERVAL (NUMTOYMINTERVAL(1, 'MONTH'))
(PARTITION p_initial VALUES LESS THAN (TIMESTAMP '2026-01-01 00:00:00'));

-- 3. Agent DNA Extensions (Trust-Cost Integration)
ALTER TABLE aria_agent_dna ADD (
    cost_efficiency_score NUMBER(3,2) DEFAULT 0.80 CHECK (cost_efficiency_score BETWEEN 0.0 AND 1.0),
    total_cost_usd        NUMBER(14,4) DEFAULT 0.0,
    expensive_calls_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_cost_anomaly_at  TIMESTAMP,
    monthly_budget_usd    NUMBER(12,2) DEFAULT 500.00
);

-- 4. Performance Indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_user_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(user_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_lob_ts   ON aria_cost_ledger(lob_code, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_agent_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(agent_id, event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_cost_ledger_model_ts ON aria_cost_ledger(model_name, event_timestamp DESC);

-- 5. Seed Data (Initial Pricing)
INSERT INTO aria_model_pricing (provider, model_name, model_version, input_price_per_1k, output_price_per_1k, cached_price_per_1k, max_context_tokens, capabilities)
VALUES 
('anthropic', 'claude-haiku-4-5', '4.5', 0.00025, 0.00125, 0.0000625, 200000, '{"function_calling":true}'),
('anthropic', 'claude-sonnet-4-6', '4.6', 0.003, 0.015, 0.00075, 200000, '{"function_calling":true,"vision":true}'),
('anthropic', 'claude-opus-4', '4.0', 0.015, 0.075, 0.00375, 200000, '{"function_calling":true,"vision":true,"reasoning":true}'),
('openai', 'gpt-4o-mini', '2024-07', 0.00015, 0.0006, 0.0000375, 128000, '{"function_calling":true}'),
('openai', 'gpt-4o', '2024-08', 0.005, 0.015, 0.00125, 128000, '{"function_calling":true,"vision":true}');

COMMIT;
```

### 1.2 Spring AI Cost Interceptor (Java 21)
*Implements `ChatClientAdvisor`. Pre-call budget check + optimization. Post-call async trust update. Overhead ≤8ms.*

```java
package com.jpmc.aria.finops.advisor;

import org.springframework.ai.chat.client.advisor.api.*;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import com.jpmc.aria.finops.model.*;
import com.jpmc.aria.trust.AgentDnaRepository;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture;

@Component
@Slf4j
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class AriaCostInterceptor implements ChatClientAdvisor {
    
    private final CostLedgerRepository costRepo;
    private final PricingCatalog pricing;
    private final BudgetGovernor budgetGovernor;
    private final OptimizationEngine optimizer;
    private final AgentDnaRepository dnaRepo;
    
    @Override
    public AdvisedRequest advise(AdvisedRequest request) {
        long start = System.currentTimeMillis();
        
        String userId = request.getMetadata().getOrDefault("user_id", "anonymous");
        String agentId = request.getMetadata().getOrDefault("agent_id", "unknown");
        String lobCode = request.getMetadata().getOrDefault("lob_code", "DEFAULT");
        String featureId = request.getMetadata().getOrDefault("feature_id", "general");
        String model = request.getChatOptions().getModel();
        
        // 1. Pre-call: Budget & Optimization Check
        BudgetStatus budget = budgetGovernor.check(userId, lobCode, featureId);
        OptimizationResult opt = optimizer.apply(model, request.getPrompt(), budget);
        
        // 2. Calculate Baseline Cost (what it would cost without optimization)
        CostEstimate baseline = pricing.estimate(model, request.getPrompt());
        
        // 3. Inject cost context for downstream advisors & LLM
        request.getMetadata().put("cost_baseline_usd", baseline.total());
        request.getMetadata().put("cost_budget_utilization", budget.utilizationPercent());
        request.getMetadata().put("cost_verdict", budget.verdict());
        
        // 4. Apply optimizations to request
        request = request.toBuilder()
            .model(opt.optimizedModel())
            .prompt(opt.compressedPrompt())
            .build();
            
        log.debug("Cost interceptor pre-check completed in {}ms", System.currentTimeMillis() - start);
        return request;
    }

    @Override
    public AdvisedResponse adviseCall(AdvisedRequest request, ChatClientAdvisorChain chain) {
        // Execute LLM call
        AdvisedResponse response = chain.nextAdviseCall(request);
        
        // Async: Record cost & update trust (non-blocking, preserves ≤500ms first-token SLO)
        CompletableFuture.runAsync(() -> postProcess(request, response));
        
        return response;
    }
    
    private void postProcess(AdvisedRequest req, AdvisedResponse res) {
        try {
            Usage usage = res.getMetadata().getUsage();
            String model = req.getChatOptions().getModel();
            CostMetrics actual = pricing.calculateActual(model, usage);
            
            // Record to Oracle
            costRepo.recordTransaction(CostTransaction.builder()
                .requestId(req.getMetadata().get("request_id"))
                .userId(req.getMetadata().get("user_id"))
                .agentId(req.getMetadata().get("agent_id"))
                .lobCode(req.getMetadata().get("lob_code"))
                .featureId(req.getMetadata().get("feature_id"))
                .model(model)
                .inputTokens(usage.promptTokens())
                .outputTokens(usage.completionTokens())
                .baselineCost(req.getMetadata().get("cost_baseline_usd"))
                .actualCost(actual.total())
                .costSaved(actual.savings())
                .build()
            );
            
            // Update Trust-Cost Feedback
            dnaRepo.applyCostTrustUpdate(req.getMetadata().get("agent_id"), actual);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("Post-cost processing failed", e);
            // Fail-safe: never block LLM response on cost recording
        }
    }
}
```
